LUK 1:28 Kaha kangelo uezile kuli Maliya uamumenekele na kuhandekele nguendi, “Muene hali nove, kaha nakukuisula cikuma!”
LUK 1:29 Maliya uakele na citanga ha lizi lije liahandekele kangelo, uasinganiekele mu mutima uendi nguendi, “Majui aua analumbunuka vika?”
LUK 1:30 Kaha kangelo uahandekele kuli ikeye nguendi, “Keti uvue liova Maliya, omuo unauana kavumbi kuli Njambi.
LUK 1:31 Tala, ukakala na lizimo, kaha ukasema muana ua yala, ukamuluka lizina liendi Yesu.
LUK 1:32 Ou muana akapua uakama, kaha vakamutumbula Muna Njambi ua helu lia vioshe. Kaha Muene Njambi akamupuisa muene, ngue muapuile kukuyendi Ndaviti.
LUK 1:33 Kaha akapua muene ua miyati ya Yakomba kumiaka yoshe, na vumuene vuendi kuvukahu!”
LUK 1:34 Kaha Maliya uahandekele kuli kangelo nguendi, “Eci cikapua vati? Omuo yange njimuana mpuevo uje kanda alimone na yala.”
LUK 1:35 Kaha kangelo uamukumbuluile nguendi, “Cimbembesi ca Kulela cikeja hali yove, na nzili ya Njambi Uakuhiana ikakufuika. Nankuma, ha cuma eci uje muana Uakulela vakamutumbula Muna Njambi.
LUK 1:36 Tala! Munanoko Elizaveta na ikeye nemita muana ua yala muvukuluntu vuendi. Kaha ino inapu ngonde ya mucitanu na imo ya lizimo liendi cipue vene vamutumbuile nguavo ntsimpi.
LUK 1:37 Omuo cuma nacimo cahi cahona Njambi kulinga.”
LUK 1:38 Kaha Maliya uakumbuluile kangelo nguendi, “Yange njinapu njingamba ya Muene Njambi, cilingiue kuli yange ngue munahandekela.” Kaha munima yevi kangelo uamusezele.
LUK 1:39 Hanima ya matangua amandende, Maliya ualivuaheselele na kuya ku mbonge ya mu minkinda ya mu nganda ya Yundeya.
LUK 1:40 Omo uahete kaha uakovelele mu njivo ya Zakaliya, kaha uahinduisile Elizaveta.
LUK 1:41 Omo Elizaveta uovuile kuhinduisa ca Maliya, kaha kakeke uaniangumukile muzimo liendi. Kaha Elizaveta uashulile na Cimbembesi ca Kulela,
LUK 1:42 kaha uahandekele na lizi liakama nguendi, “Yove uakukuisula hhakati ka vampuevo voshe, nakuisuliua muana uje iukasema!”
LUK 1:43 Omuo vikahoni cuma cakama eci cilingiua kuli yange, ngeci vaina ya Muene yange veje kuli yange?
LUK 1:44 Tala! Omo vene njovuile lizi liakuhinduisa kuove, haje vene kakeke muzimo liange uaniangumukile na kujolela.
LUK 1:45 Yove uuakukuisula omuo uakutsiliela ngeci lizi lia Muene Njambi kuli yove likapua lia vusunga!
LUK 1:46 Maliya uahandekele nguendi, “Mutima uange ushangazala vukama vua Muene Njambi,
LUK 1:47 Muono uange unavuahelela omuo Njambi Muyoyesi uange,
LUK 1:48 Omuo nanuka yange ngamba yendi uamundende! Kuhuma hano nakuya kulutue, vantu voshe vakanjitumbula nguavo njimukakuvezika,
LUK 1:49 Omuo Njambi muka nzili yoshe nanjilingila viakama. Lizina liendi lia kulela.
LUK 1:50 Ikeye akamuesa cikeketima kuli voshe vamusingimika, kuhuma kucisemua cimo kutuala ku cisemua cikuavo.
LUK 1:51 Ikeye nolola livoko liendi lia nzili, nashandula vaka viyongola via kulihalesa.
LUK 1:52 Nahumisa vamiene vakama ha matanda avo, kaha nahaka vaje vavandende kuvukama.
LUK 1:53 Nalisa vaje vali na njala na viakulia viacili, kaha vaka kufuka navasheke mavoko voko.
LUK 1:54 Ikeye naniungu likulaheso lije lia lingile na vakuluntu vetu, kaha neja nakukuasa ngamba yendi Isaleli.
LUK 1:55 Nanuka kumuesa cikeketima kuli Avilahama naku vikota viendi vioshe ku miaka yoshe!”
LUK 1:56 Kaha Maliya uasikamene na Elizaveta vingote vitatu, kaha uahilukile kuimbo liavo.
LUK 1:57 Ntsimbu ya Elizaveta yakutota yahete kaha uapapele muana uayala.
LUK 1:58 Vandambo na vavushoko vendi vovuile muje Muene Njambi muanamumuesa ngozi yakama, kaha voshe vavuahelelele hamo nendi.
LUK 1:59 Kaha ha litangua lia mucitanu na atatu, vezile nakutuhula muana ku mukanda, vatondele kumuhindula ishe Zakaliya.
LUK 1:60 Vuno honi vaina vahandekele nguavo, “houe! Mulukeni Iuano.”
LUK 1:61 Vamukumbuluile nguavo, “Kukuesi kavushoko kove ivaluka lizina eli!”
LUK 1:62 Kaha vaniatele ishe na kulinga vitantekeyeso na mavoko avo ku muihula nguavo, “Lizina muka utonda kuluka munove?”
LUK 1:63 Kaha Zakaliya ualombele citale asonekeho, omo vacinehele uasonekeleho nguendi, “Lizina liendi Iuano.” Kaha voshe vali komokelele cikuma!
LUK 1:64 Ha ntsimbu ijevene Zakaliya uasele kuhandeka naua, kaha uaputukile kushangazala Njambi.
LUK 1:65 Vandambo voshe vakele na liova, kaha muzimbu ua uatsimanene ku mutambela uoshe ua minkinda mu nganda ya Yundeya.
LUK 1:66 Voshe vaje vovuile muzimbu ou vasinganiekeleho, kaha valihozuele nguavo, “Ou kanike akafua vati?” Omuo casholokele muacili ngeci nzili ya Muene Njambi yakele hali ikeye.
LUK 1:67 Ishe ya Iuano, Zakaliya, uashulile na Cimbembesi ca kulela, kaha uahandekele vimpande vije Njambi uamusholuelele nguendi,
LUK 1:68 “Kalemeso kuli Muene Njambi ya Isaleli! Neja nakukuasa vantu vendi na kuvapatula.
LUK 1:69 Natuhana muyoyesi ua nzili, mutekulu ua ngamba yendi Ndaviti.
LUK 1:70 Uakulahesele laja muli tunanguizi va Njambi vendi va kulela
LUK 1:71 linga vakatuamene ku nzili ya vitozi vetu voshe vaje vatuzinda.
LUK 1:72 Ualingile eci kumuesa cikeketima kuli vakukuluila vetu na kushulisilila litavasano liendi lia kulela.
LUK 1:73 Eci cikeco cisingo cije ca lisingile na cisemi cetu Avilahama.
LUK 1:74 Uakulahesele kutuohiela ku mavoko avitozi vetu, linga tukamupangele cakuhona liova,
LUK 1:75 linga tupue vakulela na vaka vusunga ku mesho endi ku matangua oshe a muono uetu.
LUK 1:76 “Kaha yove munange, vakakutumbula kananguizi ka Njambi uahelu lia vioshe. Kaha ukatuama kulutue lua Muene muku vuahesa ngila yendi,
LUK 1:77 nakuleka vantu vendi ngeci vakavovola haku vakonekela ku vupi vuavo.
LUK 1:78 Omuo Njambi yetu uakala na cikeketima cakama akatumenekela ngue litangua lituhuka kuhuminina kuilu.
LUK 1:79 Akatuila ceke kuli voshe vaje vanatumama mu milima na mucimbembe ca kutsa, nakutuamenena mikono yetu mu ngila ya ciyulo.”
LUK 1:80 Iuano uakolele mu muvila na mu Cimbembesi. Uakele mu mpambo noho litangua liendi lia kulisholola lia hete ku vantu va Isaleli.
LUK 2:1 Capuile ngacije ha ntsimbu ije, kuli Sezale Angushitu kua humine lizi lia kushika, linga vasonekese voshe vantu mu vumuene vua Maloma.
LUK 2:2 Eci kusoneka cije ca katete civa lingile omo Kiliniu uapuile nguvulu ua Silia.
LUK 2:3 Kaha voshe vaile ku membo avo, va kavasonekeleko.
LUK 2:4 Kaha Yosefa uahumine ku mbonge ya Nazaleta mu nganda ya Ngalileya, uaile ku mbonge ya Mbetehema mu Yundeya ku limbo lia semukilile Muene Ndaviti, muomu uapuile muka muyati ua Ndaviti.
LUK 2:5 Uaile nakumusoneka hamo na Maliya uje ya lamene ikeye, uje uakele na lizimo.
LUK 2:6 Capuile ngacije omo vakele kuje matangua endi a kutota a hete.
LUK 2:7 Kaha uapapele munendi ua ntuatua ua yala, kaha ua muzengelele ha ntanga, kaha uamu hakele mu cikasa ca kulila vangombe muomu kukuakele cihela cavo cakukala.
LUK 2:8 Ku mutambela uje vene kuakele tuniungi mucana, vakelenakuniuka vampanga vavo vutsiki.
LUK 2:9 Kangelo ua Muene uasholokele kuli vakevo, kaha vumpau vua Muene vuatuile ceke hhakati kavo. Vovuile liova liakama cikuma.
LUK 2:10 Kangelo uahandekele kuli vakevo nguendi, “Keti muvue liova! Omo njinaneha Muzimbu Uacili kuli yeni, uje ukaneha kujolela cakama kuli vantu voshe.
LUK 2:11 Vutsiki vunovene mu mbonge ya Ndaviti munasemuka Muyoyesi ueni, ikeye Kilistu Muene!
LUK 2:12 Kaha eci cikapua cizivukiso ceni, mukauana kakeke vanamuzengela ha vintanga vana mulangeka mu cikasa caku lila vangombe.”
LUK 2:13 Hajevene kuasholokele civunga cakama ca masualale ca tungelo va muilu vemanene hamo na kangelo uje uanehele muzimbu, vembile na kulemesa Njambi nguavo,
LUK 2:14 “Vumpau kuli Njambi ua muilu, ciyulo cikale hano ha mavu kuli vantu vaje valema!”
LUK 2:15 Omo tungelo vahilukile muilu kuhuma kuli tuniungi, kaha tuniungi valihandekesele umo na mukuavo nguavo, “Tuyeni honi ku Mbetehema linga tuka mone eci cuma cinalingiuako, cije cana tusholuela Muene.”
LUK 2:16 Nankuma, vaile hajevene vuasi vuasi vakauanene Maliya na Yosefa na kakeke vana mulangeka mucikasa caku lila vangombe.
LUK 2:17 Omo tuniungi vamumuene, vambuluile mezi aje avalekele kangelo hali kakeke.
LUK 2:18 Kaha voshe vaje vovuile valikomokelele ha viuma vije vivahandekele tuniungi.
LUK 2:19 Vuno honi Maliya uaniungile mezi oshe aje naku uayongola mu mutima uendi.
LUK 2:20 Kaha tuniungi vahilukile na kushangazala na kulemesa Njambi ha viuma vioshe voviule, na vije vamuene. Viuma vioshe vialingiuile ngue vene muje muavalekele kangelo.
LUK 2:21 Omo kunahiti matangua atanu na atatu, omo ntsimbu yahete yakutuhula kakeke ku mukanda, kaha vamulukile lizina liendi Yesu, lizina lije lia mulukile kangelo ntsimbu kanda amuimite.
LUK 2:22 Kaha omo matangua apuilemo akulilelesa, Yosefa na Maliya valingile ngue ku Lishiko lia Mosesa. Nankuma, vatualele kanike ku Yelusalema linga vaka mukundike kuli Muene Njambi,
LUK 2:23 ngue muvanasoneka mu Lishiko lia Muene Njambi, “Muana uoshe ua ntuatua ua yala vaka mukundike kuli Muene Njambi.”
LUK 2:24 Mu Lishiko lia Muene Njambi naua lihandeka ngualio visemi vanapande kukombelela nkombelo ya tute vavali cipue vana va mavembe vavali, eci cikeco civalingile Yosefa na Maliya.
LUK 2:25 Kaha honi kuakele yala umo mu Yelusalema lizina liendi Simoni. Uapuile muka vusunga kaha naua uazangele Njambi, uavandamanene kuovoka kua Isaleli. Cimbembesi cakulela cakele hali ikeye,
LUK 2:26 Kaha vavisholuele kuli ikeye kuli Cimbembesi uakulela kakatsi kuakuhona kumono Kilistu Muene.
LUK 2:27 Simoni ha kumutuamenena kuli Cimbembesi ca kulela, uakovelele mu Njivo ya Muene Njambi. Omo visemi vanehele kakeke Yesu mu Njivo ya Muene Njambi va mulinge ngue ku Lishiko vatumbikile lia Mosesa.
LUK 2:28 Simoni uatambuile kakeke mu mavoko endi, uatsatselele kuli Njambi na kuhandeka nguendi,
LUK 2:29 “Vuavuno Muene Njambi unaniungu likulaheso liove kuli yange, vuavuno tava yange ngamba yove njije nakukala nove mu ciyulo,
LUK 2:30 omuo mesho ange anamono Muyoyesi iunatumu.
LUK 2:31 Vantu voshe vakamono kuamena cije ciunavuahesa.
LUK 2:32 Cikapua ceke cakusholola kuli vaje keti Vayunda, nakuneha vumpau kuli vantu vove va Isaleli.”
LUK 2:33 Ishe na vaina vali komokelele hali vije via handekele Simoni hali Yesu.
LUK 2:34 Kaha Simoni uavakuisuile na kuhandeka kuli Maliya vanaye nguendi, “Tala! kakeke ou vamuhanguile kuli Njambi mukunongesa na kuamena vavengi mu Isaleli. Akapua cimueso ca kuhuma kuli Njambi, cije vantu vavengi vaka muluisa.
LUK 2:35 Cimueso cije vantu vavengi cikamuesa viyongola viavo via kushueka. Kaha yove Maliya vusiua vukatuva mutima uove ngue mukuale uakuhomona.”
LUK 2:36 Kuakele umo kananguizi uamukuluntu ua mpuevo ua ntuluue, lizina liendi Ana muna Fanuele uaku muyati ua Ashele. Uashombokele ha miaka itanu na ivali,
LUK 2:37 kaha honi uapuile ntuluue. Uakele na miaka makumi atanu na atatu na miaka iuana. Ikeye kahumine mu njivo ya Muene Njambi, mutania na vutsiki uakele nakulemesa Njambi ha kuliumina kulia na kulombela.
LUK 2:38 Ha ntsimbu ijevene uahete kuli Maliya na Yosefa uahanene cikandelela kuli Njambi. uahandekele hali uje muana kuli voshe vaje vavandamenene Njambi mukupatula Yelusalema.
LUK 2:39 Omo Yosefa na Maliya vamanesele vioshe ngue ku Lishiko lia muene Njambi, vahilukile kuimbo liavo ku Nazaleta mu Ngalileya.
LUK 2:40 Kaha muana uakolele uakele na nzili. Uakolele mu mana, kaha vikuisulo via Njambi viakele hali ikeye.
LUK 2:41 Ha muaka na muaka visemi va Yesu vakele nakuya ku Yelusalema ku Ciuano ca Paseka.
LUK 2:42 Omo Yesu uakele na miaka likumi na ivali, kaha vaile nendi ku Yelusalema ku cilika ca ciuano ngue ntsimbu yoshe.
LUK 2:43 Omo matangua aje a ciuano ahuile, kaha vaputukile kuya kuimbo, vuno honi Yesu uasalele munima mu Yelusalema. Visemi vendi kuvatantekeyele,
LUK 2:44 vayonguele nguavo hamo hali ha cendo, nankuma vendele vungezi vua litangua limo, kaha vaputukile kumutonda hhakati kava vushoko vuavo nava vusamba vavo,
LUK 2:45 vuno honi kuva muuanene. Nankuma, vahilukile naua ku Yelusalema na kumutonda.
LUK 2:46 Kaha ha litangua lia mu citatu vamuuanene mu Njivo ya Muene Njambi, natumama hhakati ka valongisi va mashiko a Njambi, na kuvovuilila naku vehozola vihula.
LUK 2:47 Kaha voshe vaje vovuile vali komokelele cikuma mangana endi nakukumbulula cendi.
LUK 2:48 Visemi vendi omo vamumuene valikomokelele, kaha vaina vahandekele kuli ikeye nguavo, “Munange, vika unatulingilamo? Tala! Isho nange tunaliniengele na kukutonda cikuma ngeci tukuuane.”
LUK 2:49 Kaha Yesu uavakumbuluile nguendi, “Vika munanjitondela? Nkuma kumuatantekeyele ngueni njinapande kukala mu njivo ya tate ndi?”
LUK 2:50 Vuno honi vakevo kuvatantekeyele kulumbunuka cakukumbulula cendi.
LUK 2:51 Kaha Yesu uaile navo ku Nazaleta, kaha kuje uatualeleleho kuvononoka. Vaina vaniungile vioshe evi mu mutima uavo.
LUK 2:52 Kaha Yesu uakolele mu muvila, na mu mana, uauanene kavumbi kakama kuli Njambi na vantu.
LUK 3:1 Evi vioshe vialingiuile omo Sezale Timbeliase te hanga aciyula ha miaka likumi na itanu mu vumuene vua Loma. Ha ntsimbu ije Pontiyu Pilato uapuile nguvulu uamu Yundeya, na Helonde uasuanene mu Ngalileya, munaina Filipu uasuanene mu nganda ya Ituleya na nganda ya Talakoniti, Lisaniya uasuanene mu nganda ya Ambilene,
LUK 3:2 na Anase na Kayafase vapuile Tusasendote Vakama. Ha ntsimbu ijevene Njambi uahandekele kuli Iuano muna Zakaliya omo uakele mu mpambo.
LUK 3:3 Kaha Iuano uaile ku cihela na cihela ca Ndonga ya Yundau na kuambulula nguendi, “Tengulukeni ku vupi vueni vamimbuitike, kaha Njambi akamisambesa ku vupi vueni.”
LUK 3:4 Ngue muvana soneka mu livulu lia Isaya kananguizi ua Njambi nguavo, “lizi lia umo atambeka mu mpambo nguendi, ‘Vuaheseni tapalo ya Muene Njambi, sungameseni ngila yendi linga akuhitilemo!
LUK 3:5 Vimbongo vioshe vanapande ku viofuela, minkinda yoshe yakama neyi yaindende vaka viniekumuna, na vingila via kuhenga vanapande kuviolola visungame, na vingila via kuzika vanapande kuvilambesa.
LUK 3:6 Vantu voshe vakamona kuamena ca Njambi.’ ”
LUK 3:7 Kaha Iuano ualekele vije vivunga via vantu vezile kuli ikeye nakuvambuitika nguendi, “Eni manoka! Iya honi naminangula linga muteue vukalu vua Njambi vuje vuli nakuija?
LUK 3:8 Nga mutonda kuteua kuvukalu vua Njambi lingeni viuma vije vimuesa ngeci munatenguluka ku vupi vueni. Keti mu lihandekese mu mitima yeni ngueni ‘Tuli na cisemi cetu Avilahama.’ Mua vusunga njimileka nguange Njambi asa kutengulula mavue aua naku uapuisa vatekulu va Avilahama!
LUK 3:9 Ngimbu vanaihaka laja kumizi ya muti, muti uoshe kuuimi vushuka vua cili vaka uteta nakuumbila mu tuhia.”
LUK 3:10 Vantu vamuihuile nguavo, “Kaha honi tulinga vati?”
LUK 3:11 Uavakumbuluile nguendi, “Ou hali na vikovelo vivali ahaneko cimo uje kesi naco, kaha nou alina via kulia ahaneko vakuavo.”
LUK 3:12 Vaka kutambula lisimo vezile linga avambuitike, kaha vamuihuile nguavo, “Mulongisi, yetu tunapande kulinga vika?”
LUK 3:13 Kaha uavalekele nguendi, “Keti mukatambule kupulakana omo muvemika.”
LUK 3:14 Masualale vamo naua vamuihuile nguavo, “Netu naua tunapande kulinga vika?” Kaha uavalekele nguendi, “Keti muka pukule viuma via vakueni, cipue kuvangela, simpeni na fueto yeni.”
LUK 3:15 Vantu vakele nalikulahelo lia kuvandamena nguavo Kilistu eja honi, voshe vakele na kulihozola mu mutima yavo hali Iuano nguavo hamo ikeye Kilistu.
LUK 3:16 Kaha Iuano uahandekele kuli voshe nguendi, “Njimimbuitika mu mema, vuno honi ouo akeja napu uakama kupulakana yange. Ku njapandele cipue kuzitula mikole ya ha vinkaku viendi. Ikeye akamimbuitika na Cimbembesi ca kulela na mu tuhia.
LUK 3:17 Lisehua lili mu livoko liendi, ikeye akapekula na kulelesa muacili vinona vioshe kulijunguilo liendi, kaha tiliku akaitulika mu cishete cendi, vuno honi mujungu uoshe akautsimika na tuhia tuakuhona kuzima!”
LUK 3:18 Ha kuvasindiya cikuma Iuano uambuluile Muzimbu ua Cili ku vantu.
LUK 3:19 Naua Iuano uatenukilile muene Helonde, omo Helonde uambate Helondiya mpuevo ya munaina Filipu, kaha naua uamutenukilile omuo ualingile viuma vieka via vipi.
LUK 3:20 Cuma cacipi cikuma ca lingile naua Helonde ca kuhaka Iuano mu kamenga.
LUK 3:21 Kaha omo Iuano uakele nakumbuitika vantu voshe na Yesu naua vamumbuitikile. Ha ntsimbu ijevene Yesu omo uakele na kulombela, lilu liashokolokele.
LUK 3:22 Kaha Cimbembesi ca kulela ca shulukile hali ikeye mucifua ca livembe. Kaha muilu mua humine lizi ngualio, “Yove munange injazema, njili na kuvuahelela hali yove.”
LUK 3:23 Yesu uaputukile kuambulula na kulongesa kucivunga te hali na miaka makumi atatu. Kaha vantu vamu tantekeyele nguavo ikeye muna Yosefa. Yosefa uapuile muna Heli,
LUK 3:24 Heli uapuile muna Matati, Matati uapuile muna Levi, Levi uapuile muna Meleki, Maleki uapuile muna Njanayi, Njanayi uapuile muna Yosefa,
LUK 3:25 Yosefa uapuile muna Matiyasi, Matayasi uapuile muna Amose, Amose uapuile muna Nashumi, Nashumi uapuile muna Eseli, Eseli uapuile muna Nangai,
LUK 3:26 Nangai uapuile muna Maate, Maate uapuile muna Matatiya, Matatiya uapuile muna Semehine, Semehine uapuile muna Yoseke, Yoseke uapuile muna Yonda,
LUK 3:27 Yonda uapuile muna Youanane, Youanane uapuile muna Lehesa, Lehesa uapuile muna Zelumbambele, Zelumbambele uapuile muna Sheyaletiyele, Sheyaletiyele uapuile muna Neli.
LUK 3:28 Neli uapuile muna Meleki, Meleki uapuile muna Andi, Andi uapuile muna Kosame, Kosame uapuile muna Elemandame, Elemandame uapuile muna Ele,
LUK 3:29 Ele uapuile muna Yoshiua, Yoshiua uapuile muna Ezazale, Ezazale uapuile muna Yolime, Yolime uapuile muna Matata, Matata uapuile muna Levi,
LUK 3:30 Levi uapuile muna Simioni, Simioni uapuile muna Yunda, Yunda uapuile muna Yosefa, Yosefa uapuile muna Njoname, Njoname uapuile muna Eliakime,
LUK 3:31 Eliakime uapuile muna Meleya, Meleya uapuile muna Mena, Mena uapuile muna Matata, Matata uapuile muna Natane, Natane uapuile muna Ndaviti,
LUK 3:32 Ndaviti uapuile muna Njesi, Njesi uapuile muna Ovende, Ovende uapuile muna Mbouasi, Mbouasi uapuile muna Salemone, Salemone uapuile muna Naheshoni,
LUK 3:33 Nashone uapuile muna Aminandave, Aminandave uapuile muna Andemine, Andamine uapuile muna Aleni, Aleni uapuile muna Izeloni, Izeloni uapuile muna Peleze, Peleze uapuile muna Yunda,
LUK 3:34 Yunda uapuile muna Yakomba, Yakomba uapuile muna Isake, Iseke uapuile muna Avilahama, Avilahama uapuile muna Tela, Tela uapuile muna Nahole,
LUK 3:35 Nahole ua puile muna Selunge, Selunge uapuile muna Leu, Leu uapuile muna Pelenge, Pelenge uapuile muna Hevele, Hevele uapuile muna shela,
LUK 3:36 Shela uapuile muna Kainane, Kainane uapuile muna Alepakeshande, Alepakeshande uapuile muna Shemi, Shemi uapuile muna Noua, Noua uapuile muna Lameki
LUK 3:37 Lameki uapuile muna Matusela, Matusela uapuile muna Enoki, uapuile muna Njalende, Njalende uapuile muna Maalalele, Maalalele uapuile muna Kenane
LUK 3:38 Kenane uapuile muna Enoshe, Enoshe uapuile muna Sete, Sete uapuile muna Andama, Andama uapuile muna Njambi.
LUK 4:1 Yesu hakushula na Cimbembesi ca kulela, uahumine ku Ndonga ya Yundau, kaha Cimbembesi camutuamenenene mu mpambo,
LUK 4:2 kuje Satana uakamuesekele matangua makumi auana. Ha ntsimbu ije yoshe Yesu kalile nacimo cahi, omo matangua aje ahuile, kaha uovuile njala.
LUK 4:3 Kaha Satana uahandekele kuli ikeye nguendi, “Nga u Muna Njambi shika livue eli linga lilihimpule mbolo.”
LUK 4:4 Vuno honi Yesu uamukumbuluile nguendi, “Vanavisoneka mu Visoneka nguavo, ‘Muntu kasa kuyoya na mbolo lika kuahi.’ ”
LUK 4:5 Kaha Satana ualondesele Yesu helu lia munkinda ualaha, kaha uamumuesele muka ntsimbu kakandende vumuene vuoshe vuahano ha mavu.
LUK 4:6 Kaha Satana uahandekele kuli ikeye nguendi, “Njikakuhana vumuene ovu na vufuko vuoshe vilimo, omuo vanjihanavio, kaha njikavihana kuli uoshe uje injitonda.
LUK 4:7 Nga unjilemesa, kaha vioshe evi vikapua viove.”
LUK 4:8 Yesu uahandekele kuli ikeye nguendi, “Vanavisoneka mu Visoneke nguavo, ‘Ukalemesa Muene Njambi yove, ikeye lika iukapangela!’”
LUK 4:9 Kaha Satana uamutualele ku Yelusalema, uamuhakele ha kashongua ka njivo ya Muene Njambi, uahandekele kuli ikeye nguendi, “Nga u Muna Njambi, liumbile ha mavu kuhuma kuno kuilu,
LUK 4:10 omuo vanavisoneka mu Visoneka nguavo, ‘Njambi akashika tungelo vendi na kukuniunga.’
LUK 4:11 Kaha vanavisoneka mu Visoneka naua nguavo, ‘Vakakukuata, linga viliato viove keti vikatsutsuke ku livue.’ ”
LUK 4:12 Vuno honi Yesu uahandekele kuli ikeye nguendi, “Vanavisoneka mu Visoneka nguavo, ‘Keti ueseke Muene Njambi yove.’ ”
LUK 4:13 Omo Satana uamanesele kueseka Yesu mu vingila vioshe, kaha uamusezele noho hakauana ntsimbu ikuavo.
LUK 4:14 Kaha Yesu uahilukile ku Ngalileya, na nzili ya Cimbembesi ca kulela yakele muli ikeye. Kaha muzimbu uendi uatsimanene mu nganda yoshe ya Ngalileya.
LUK 4:15 Yesu uavalongesele mu vinjivo viavo via malombelo, kaha voshe vamushangazalele.
LUK 4:16 Yesu uaile ku Nazaleta, kuje kuakolelele, kaha uakovelele mu njivo ya malombelo ha litangua lia Sapalalo ngue ku cilika cendi. Kaha uemanene na kutanda Visoneka.
LUK 4:17 Vamuhanene livulu lia sonekele Isaya Kananguizi ua Njambi. Kaha uazengunuine lije livulu liakuzenga, uauanene ha mutambela uje uatondele kutanda. Kaha uatandele nguendi,
LUK 4:18 “Cimbembesi ca Muene Njambi cili muli yange, omuo nanjihangula kuambulula Muzimbu ua Cili kuli vihutu. Nanjitumu kuambulula linga vinzinda vaka vapatule, nakuambulula linga tupuputua vakamone, nakunjituma kupatula vaje vavali nakuyandesa,
LUK 4:19 nakunjituma kuambulula ngeci ntsimbu inahete ya kavumbi ka Muene Njambi ku vantu vendi.”
LUK 4:20 Yesu uazengele lije livulu, ualihanene naua kuli muka kuniunga, kaha uatumamene. Vantu voshe vakele muje mu njivo ya malombelo vamutalele ntooma,
LUK 4:21 kaha uahandekele kuli vakevo nguendi, “Visoneka evi lelo vinapuisamo ku mesho eni, ngue omo munovu vanakele nakulitanda.”
LUK 4:22 Kaha voshe vamushangazalele, valikomokelele ku mezi endi acili aje ahandekele, vahandekele nguavo, “Ou ikeye uje muna Yosefa ndi?”
LUK 4:23 Kaha uahandekele kuli vakevo nguendi, “Mua vusunga mukanjitela cisimo eci ngueni, ‘Ove cimbanda likanguise yove vavenia!’ Cimukalumbununa cikapua ngueni, ‘Yove linga viuma vioshe muno muimbo liove, vijevene vituovuile viualingile mu Capenama.’
LUK 4:24 Mua vusunga njimileka, naumo uahi kananguizi ua Njambi ivakatava muimbo liendi.
LUK 4:25 Vuno honi muavusunga njimileka mu lifuti lietu lia Isaleli muakele vantuluue vavengi ha matangua a Eliya kananguizi ua Njambi, omo kalunga kanokele miaka itatu na vingonde vitanu na imo naua honi kuakele njala mu lifuti lioshe.
LUK 4:26 Eliya kuvamutumine kuli voshe, vuno honi kuli ntuluue uje keti Kayunda uje uakele mu limbo lia Zelefani kuyehi na mbonge ya Sindone.
LUK 4:27 Kuakele vantu vavengi vakele nakuvavala mbumba mu Isaleli ha ntsimbu ya Elisha kananguizi ua Njambi, vuno honi naumo uahi yakanguisile kuvanga lika Namane keti Kayunda uaku Silia.”
LUK 4:28 Omo vantu vaje vakele mu njivo ya malombelo vazivile evi, vakele na litoto.
LUK 4:29 Vakatukile, kaha vakokelele Yesu hambaza ya nganda, vamutualele kuntsongo ya munkinda haje ha vatungile nganda yavo. Vatondele ngeci vakamumbile mu cimbongo.
LUK 4:30 Kaha uahitile mukati kavo nakuya.
LUK 4:31 Yesu uaile ku Kapenama, mbonge ya mu Ngalileya, kuje uakalongesele vantu lia Sapalalo.
LUK 4:32 Vantu voshe vakomokele cikuma kuambulula nguendi, omuo mezi endi akele na nzili.
LUK 4:33 Kaha mu njivo ya malombelo muakele yala umo uakele na Cimbembesi ca kujuala, catambekele cikuma.
LUK 4:34 “Haa! Yove Yesu uaku Nazaleta utonda kulinga vika kuno netu? Uneja nakutunongesa ndi? Nja kutantekeya yove uapua umo Uakulela ua Njambi!”
LUK 4:35 Kaha honi Yesu uashikile Cimbembesi ca kujuala nguendi, “Kuluu huma muli muntu ou!” Kaha cije Cimbembesi ca kujuala cauisilile uje yala ha mavu ku mesho avo voshe, kaha ca humine muli ikeye kuakuhona kumuvetuesa.
LUK 4:36 Vantu voshe valikomokelele cikuma vaputukile kulihandekesa umo na mukuavo nguavo, “Majui muka aua? Muntu ou hali na nzili ya kushika vimbembesi via kujuala kaha vimuivuila.”
LUK 4:37 Kaha vialingile vioshe viovuikile mu cihela ca lifuti lije.
LUK 4:38 Kaha Yesu uahumine mu njivo ya malombelo uaile ku njivo ya Simoni. Uauanene vainamueno ya Simoni vavavala lisika sika liakama cikuma. Valombele Yesu linga amukangule.
LUK 4:39 Kaha Yesu uaile kuli ikeye nakumukotamena, kaha uashikile lije lisika sika kuhua kaha uakangukile na kuimana nakuputuka kuvapangela via kulia.
LUK 4:40 Hakulahuka kua litangua, voshe vaje vakele na mishongo yakuli sezaseza vavanehele kuli Yesu, voshe uavahakele mavoko na kuvakanguisa.
LUK 4:41 Kaha vimbembesi via kujuala naua via huminemo mu vantu vavengi na kutambeka nguavio, “Yove u Muna Njambi!” Vuno honi ikeye uashikile vimbembesi via kujuala ngeci keti vihandeka nacimo cahi naua, omuo vikevio viamutantekeyele nguavio ikeye Kilistu.
LUK 4:42 Omo kuacele Yesu uatuhukile, nakuya kuali kaliendi lika. Vantu vaputukile kumutondezeka, omo vamuuanene vatondele kumuvindika ngeci keti ahume kuli vakevo.
LUK 4:43 Vuno honi uahandekele kuli vakevo nguendi, “Njapande kuambulula Muzimbu Viacili via vumuene vua Njambi mu vimbonge vieka naua, omuo evi vikevo via njitumine kulinga Njambi.”
LUK 4:44 Uakele na kuambulula mu vinjivo via malombelo via Njambi vioshe viamu Yundeya.
LUK 5:1 Litangua limo Yesu uemanene ha ntunda ya cisali ca Ngenesaleta te vantu vakele nakulisindika kuya kuli ikeye linga vovue lizi lia Njambi.
LUK 5:2 Kaha uamuene mato avali vanaatutika ku mukulo ua cisali. Vaka kuta vatsi vahumine mu mato na kukusha manda avo.
LUK 5:3 Yesu uakovelele mu vuato vumo, vuakele vua Simoni, kaha uamulombele ngeci avusindikile alahako kamandende na hantunda. Yesu uatumamene mu vuato, kaha ualongesele cije civunga.
LUK 5:4 Omo Yesu uamanesele kuhandeka, kaha uahandekele kuli Simoni nguendi, “Sindikila vuato haje ha mema a kulova, kaha yove na vakueni teni manda eni linga mujevele vantsi.”
LUK 5:5 Simoni uamukumbuluile nguendi, “Muene, tunapanga cikuma vutsiki vuoshe vuno honi nakamo tunakuata kahi. Vuno honi omuo ukahandeka ngoco, kaha tuta manda.”
LUK 5:6 Kaha omo vate manda vakuate vatsi vavengi cikuma, kaha manda aputukile kutavuka.
LUK 5:7 Nankuma, vaniatele vavusamba vavo vakele mu vuato vukuavo veje vaku vakuase. Vezile vashulisile mato oshe na vatsi mukemo vaputukile kuvombela.
LUK 5:8 Omo Simoni Petulu uamuene vije vialingiuile, uatsikamene ha mavuli ku mesho a Yesu na kuhandeka nguendi, “Muene, huma kuli yange, omuo yange njimuka vupi!”
LUK 5:9 Simoni na vakuavo vali komokelele cikuma ha kumona vatsi vavengi vava kuatele.
LUK 5:10 Simoni uakele navavusamba vendi vavali mazina avo apuile Yakomba na Iuano vana va Zembendeo, nava kevo naua vali komokele cikuma. Yesu uahandekele kuli Simoni nguendi, “Keti uzive liova, hume hano ukata vantu.”
LUK 5:11 Vatutikile mato avo ku ntunda, vasezele vioshe, kaha vakavele Yesu.
LUK 5:12 Litangua limo Yesu uakele mu mbonge imo muje muakele yala umo uakele nakuyanda na mushongo ua mbumba. Omo uamuene Yesu, uauile nacihanga cendi ha mavu amulambelelele nguendi, “Muene, nga utonda, uasa kunjikanguisa!”
LUK 5:13 Yesu uoluele livoko liendi uamukuate uahandekele nguendi, “Njitonda, kanguka!” Hajevene uakangukile.
LUK 5:14 Yesu uamushikile nguendi, “Keti ulekeko muntu umo cuma eci kuahi, vuno honi ya ukalisholole kuli kasasendote linga vantu voshe vatantekeye nguavo vakukangula, ambahoni ukakombelele nkombelo ije yashikile Mosesa.”
LUK 5:15 Vuno honi muzimbu uahali Yesu uakele nakushanduokela kuoshe, kaha vivunga via vantu vezile nakumuivuilila na kuvakanguisa ku mishongo yavo.
LUK 5:16 Vuno honi Yesu kakengi uakele nakuvaseza nakuya kuali kaliendi lika na kulombela.
LUK 5:17 Litangua limo omo Yesu uakele nakulongesa, Vafaliseo vamo na valongisi va mezi a Lishiko lia Mosesa vatumamene kuje, vahumine mu membo a ku Ngalileya na ku Yundeya na ku mbonge yakama ya Yelusalema. Nzili ya Muene Njambi yakele hali Yesu mukukanguisa vantu.
LUK 5:18 Kaha vamala vamo vanehele yala muka kalepa vamulangeka ha citalatala, vesekele kumukovelesa mu njivo linga vamulangeke ku lutue lua Yesu.
LUK 5:19 Omuo civunga ca vantu, kuvauanene ngila yaku mukovelesela mukati. Nankuma, vamutualele helu lia njivo, vatuvile mbengua mu mateya, kaha vamusoselele na citalatala cendi ha mavu mukati ka civunga kulutue lua Yesu.
LUK 5:20 Omo Yesu uavamuene lutsilielo luavo, uahandekele kuli uje yala nguendi, “Kavusamba kange, vipi viove vana visambesa.”
LUK 5:21 Valongisi va mezi a Lishiko lia Mosesa na Vafaliseo vaputukile kusinganieka nguavo, “Iya ou yala alinakushaula Njambi? Njambi lika ikeye muka kusambuesa vupi!”
LUK 5:22 Yesu uazivukile viyongola viavo, kaha uahandekele kuli vakevo nguendi, “Vikahoni mulina kuyonguela viuma via ngacije?
LUK 5:23 Cacasi cika, kuhandeka nguange, ‘Vipi viove vana visambesa,’ indi kuhandeka nguange, ‘Katuka uende’?
LUK 5:24 Njimimuesa linga mutantekeye ngueni Muna Muntu hali na nzili hano ha mavu ya kusambuesa vipi.” Kaha uahandekele kuli uje muka kakalepa nguendi, “Njikuleka nguange katuka, ambata citalatala cove, uye ku njivo yove!”
LUK 5:25 Kaha hajevene uakatukile hhakati kavo, uambate citalatala cendi uaile ku njivo nakushangazala Njambi.
LUK 5:26 Kaha voshe valikomokelele cikuma! Vovuile liova, vashangazalele Njambi vahandekele nguavo, “Lelo tunamono viuma via kukomokesa!”
LUK 5:27 Munima yevi, Yesu uatuhukile, kaha uamuene muka kutambula lisimu, lizina liendi Levi, natumama mu njivo yendi ya kutambuila lisimu. Kaha Yesu uahandekele kuli ikeye nguendi, “Njikave.”
LUK 5:28 Kaha Levi uakatukile, uasezele vioshe na kumukava.
LUK 5:29 Kaha Levi calingiuile Yesu ciuano cakama cakulia mu njivo yendi, kaha hhakati kavaje vavalaniene hakele vaka kutambula lisimu na vantu veka vavengi.
LUK 5:30 Vafaliseo vamo na valongisi va mezi a Lishiko lia Mosesa vaje vakundamene ku mpunga yavo valiniengelele kuli vandongisi va Yesu. Vehuile nguavo, “Vikahoni mulia na kunua hamo na vaka kutambula lisimu na vaka vupi?”
LUK 5:31 Yesu uavakumbuluile nguendi, “Vakangule kuvekutonda cimbanda kuahi, kuvanga vaka kuvavala lika.
LUK 5:32 Ngoco vene yange kunjezile mukusana vantu vaje vanalimono vakevo vavenia nguavo vaka vusunga linga vatenguluke, vuno honi vantu vaje vaka vupi.”
LUK 5:33 Vantu vamo vahandekele kuli Yesu nguavo, “Vandongisi va Iuano vakalikela kulia vintsimbu viavingi na kulombela, na vandongisi va Vafaliseo naua vakalingi cuma cimo, vuno honi vandongisi vove vakali na kunua ntsimbu yoshe.”
LUK 5:34 Kaha Yesu uavakumbuluile nguendi, “Nkuma yeni mutalelela vangenzi ku ciuano ca vulo linga vaye na njala ndi? Muavusunga vene kuahi! Omo vavenia vulo acili navo kuvapandele kulinga ngacije.
LUK 5:35 Vuno honi litangua likeja omo vakahumisa vavenia vulo hhakati kavo, ambahoni vakalikela kulia.”
LUK 5:36 Yesu uavatelele naua cisimo eci nguendi, “Kuuasa kutavula cikamba ku kazaku kakaha na kucitongela ha kazaku ka laja. Nga ulingamo, kaha utavula kazaku kakaha, cikamba caciha kucilitombola na ntanga yalaja.
LUK 5:37 Naua vene kuvekulongela viniu viavihia mu vinjeke via vilambu vialaja. Nga ulingamo vije vinjeke via vilambu vitavuka kaha viniu vihitikila muangoco.
LUK 5:38 Vuno honi viniu viavihia vaka vilongela mu vinjeke via vilambu viavihia.
LUK 5:39 Kuuasa kunua viniu viavihia omo unanu laja viniu vialaja. Uhandeka nguove, ‘Viniu vialaja viacili.’ ”
LUK 6:1 Ha litangua limo lia Sapalalo Yesu na vandongisi vendi vakele nakuhita mu mehia a tiliku. Vandongisi vendi vaputukile kushututozola mitue ya tiliku, vaitsenene mu mavoko avo, kaha valile vinona.
LUK 6:2 Kaha Vafaliseo vamo vakele kuje vavehuile nguavo, “Omo vika mulinakulingila evi kuvekulinga ha litangua lia Sapalalo kuya mu Lishiko lia Mosesa?”
LUK 6:3 Yesu uavakumbuluile nguendi, “Nkuma kanda mutande vije vialingile Ndaviti na vaje vakele hamo nendi omo vazivile njala ndi?
LUK 6:4 Uakovelele mu njivo ya Muene Njambi, kasasendote uamuhanene lisesa lia kunona ije mbolo ivakombelele kuli Njambi, ualile, na kuhanako naua vantu vendi. Mbolo ije kuyapandele ku ilia kuli muntu uoshe kuvanga tusasendote lika.”
LUK 6:5 Kaha Yesu uamanesele nguendi, “Muna Muntu ikeye Muene ua Litangua lia Sapalalo.”
LUK 6:6 Ha litangua lia Sapalalo likuavo Yesu uakovelele mu njivo ya malombelo, kaha ualongesele. Muakele yala umo uakusekua livoko lia cilio.
LUK 6:7 Kaha valongisi va mezi a Lishiko lia Mosesa na Vafaliseo vamo vatondele kashuilo hali Yesu linga vamu uaneneho mulonga, nankuma, vamutalele ntoma muyehi yehi linga vamone nga ikeye akanguisa uje muntu ha litangua lia Sapalalo.
LUK 6:8 Vuno honi Yesu uazivukile viyongola viavo, kaha uahandekele kuli uje yala uakusekua livoko nguendi, “Katuka uije hano hhakati.” Kaha uje yala uakatukile uemanene mukati.
LUK 6:9 Nankuma, Yesu uahandekele kuli vakevo nguendi, “Njimihula nguange, cuma muka vanatutavesa ha Lishiko lietu kucilinga ha litangua lia Sapalalo? Kupanga viacili indi kupanga viavipi? Kuamena muono ua muntu indi kuunongesa?”
LUK 6:10 Uatalele kuli vakevo voshe noku noku, kaha uahandekele kuli uje yala nguendi, “Olola livoko liove.” Uoluele livoko liendi, kaha liakangukile.
LUK 6:11 Ha cuma eci valongisi va mezi a Lishiko lia Mosesa na Vafaliseo vakele na matoto, kaha valihandekesele hhakati kavo vivapandele kulinga kuli Yesu.
LUK 6:12 Ha ntsimbu ije Yesu ualondele ku munkinda na kulombela, kaha uakele nakulombela vutsiki vuoshe kuli Njambi.
LUK 6:13 Omo litangua liatuhukile, kaha uasanene vandongisi vendi linga veje kuli ikeye, kaha uahanguileho likumi na vavali hhakati kavo, vaje vatumbuile tunganda.
LUK 6:14 Aua akeuo mazina avo: Simoni uje yalukile Petulu na munaina Anduleo, Yakomba na Iuano, Filipu na Mbatolomeo,
LUK 6:15 Mateu na Tomasi, Yakomba muna Alufeya, na Simoni (uje ivatumbuile “Zelote.”)
LUK 6:16 Yundasa muna Yakomba, na Yundasa Sakaliote uje uamuendele vungungu.
LUK 6:17 Yesu na vandongisi vendi vahumine ku munkinda kaha vemanene ku mutambela uaku jalamanena. Na civunga ceka cakama ca vandongisi vakele kuje nakumuvandamena. Naua civunga cakama ca vantu cahumine ku Yundeya kuoshe na ku Yelusalema, naku vimbonge via ku cikuma ca Tile na ku Sindone.
LUK 6:18 Vezile nakumuvuilila na kuvakanguisa ku mishongo yavo. Voshe vaje vakele nakuyanda na vimbembesi via kujuala vezile, kaha uavakanguisile.
LUK 6:19 Kaha civunga coshe ca vantu vesekele kumukambeka mavoko, omuo nzili yahumine kuli ikeye na kuvakanguisa voshe.
LUK 6:20 Yesu uatalele vandongisi vendi, kaha uahandekele nguendi, “Muavezika yeni vaka kuhutua, omuo Vumuene vua Njambi vunapu vueni!”
LUK 6:21 “Muavezika yeni muli na njala vuavuno, omuo mukakuta!” “Muavezika yeni mulinakulila vuavuno, omuo mukajolelela!”
LUK 6:22 “Muavezika omuo vantu vamizinda na kumiviana na kumishaula na kumitumbula nguavo muva vapi, vioshe evi omuo mukavangeya Muna Muntu!”
LUK 6:23 Joleleni omo eci cilingiua, kineni na kujolela, omuo Njambi namivuahesela cikandelela ceni cakama muilu. Omuo vakuluntu vavo valingile ngacije kuli tunanguizi va Njambi va Njambi.
LUK 6:24 “Vuno honi tuyando kuli yeni munafuku laja, omuo muatambula laja kuyoya kuacili!”
LUK 6:25 “Tuyando tueni yeni munakuta vuavuno, omuo mukaziva njala!” “Tuyando tueni yeni muli nakujolela, omuo muka pihilila na kulila!
LUK 6:26 “Tuyando tueni omuo vantu voshe vali nakumishangazala, omuo vakuluntu vavo valingile ngacije kuli tunanguizi va Njambi va makuli.
LUK 6:27 “Vuno honi njimileka yeni vaka kunjitolilila nguange, zangeni vitozi veni, lingeni muacili kuli vaje vamizinda,
LUK 6:28 vezikiseni vaje vamisinga, kaha lombeleleni vaje vali nakumiyandesa.
LUK 6:29 Nga muntu akupupa ku litama limo, kaha mutenguluile akupupe ku litama likuavo naua, nga muntu akunieka kazaku kove, muhane naua na cikovelo cove.
LUK 6:30 Muntu uje amilomba muhaneni cuma cije canamilombo, omo muntu ambata cuma cove, kaha keti ucihule naua.
LUK 6:31 Viuma vioshe vimutonda ngeci vakueni vamilingilevio, mukemuo vene, neni naua valingilenavio.
LUK 6:32 “Nga muzanga lika vaje vamizanga, vikahoni mutambuila vishangalo? Cipue vaka vipi vakazanga vaka kuvazanga!
LUK 6:33 Nga mulinga lika muacili kuli vaje vakamilingi muacili, vikahoni mutambuila vishangalo? Cipue vaka vupi mukemuo muvakalingi!
LUK 6:34 Nga mukumuisa lika vaje muavandamena ngueni vamihiluisila, vikahoni mutambuila vishangalo? Cipue vaka vupi naua vakalikumuisa, linga vatambule ngue muje muvanahana.
LUK 6:35 Vuno honi zangeni vitozi veni, kaha lingeni muacili kuli vakevo, vakumuiseni vuno honi keti muvandamene ngueni mukavitambula naua. Kaha cikandelela ceni cikapua cakama, mukapua vana va Njambi ua Helu lia Helu. Omuo ikeye akevuila ngozi vaje kuvekumukandelela na vaje vaka vupi.
LUK 6:36 Pueni vaka cikeketima ngue Ishueni uapua muka cikeketima.
LUK 6:37 “Keti muhise, kuteua neni vakamihisa, keti mupaye, kuteua neni vakamipaya, sambeseni, kaha neni vakamisambesa.
LUK 6:38 Haneni, kaha neni vakamihana. Cikapua nge muka kulandesa uje akuhana seteko ya vinona, akaizindangeya nakui niekumuna kaha akashulilisaho cikuma noho ishulisa muvimbango via cisetekelo na kumuanianga kaha honi akakuhanavio vioshe. Seteko ije museteka nayo vakueni, ikeyo naua vakamiseteka nayo.”
LUK 6:39 Kaha Yesu uavatelele cisimo eci nguendi, “Kapuputua umo kasa kutuamenena kapuputua mukuavo, nga alingamo voshe vavali vakauila mucina.
LUK 6:40 Kukuesi ndongisi atuvakana mulongisi uendi vuno honi ndongisi uoshe, omo namanesa kulilongesa cendi, ikeye naua akapua hamo na mulongisi uendi.
LUK 6:41 “Vikahoni umona kacishoni kali ha lisho lia mukueni, vuno honi ku uyongola mukambo uli mulisho liove?
LUK 6:42 Vatihoni uhandeka na mukueni nguove, ‘Mukuetu, teua njikuhumise kacishoni kali ha lisho liove,’ omo yove uli na mukambo mu lisho liove? Ove muka civembulu! Ha kulivanga humisa mukambo uli mu lisho liove, kaha umone muacili hakuhumisa kacishoni kali ha lisho lia mukueni.
LUK 6:43 “Muti uacili kuuasa kuima vushuka vuavupi, cipue muti uaupi kuuasa kuima vushuka vuacili.
LUK 6:44 Muti uoshe vauzivukila ku vushuka vuauo, omuo kuuasa kuhela vushuka vua mukuyu na mikolovozi ya viniu ku muti ua mambimbo.
LUK 6:45 Muntu uacili ikeye muka kusholola viuma via viacili via ku mutima uendi, muntu ua mupi akasholola viuma viavipi via ku mutima uendi omuo kanua kakahandeka vije viashula mu mutima.
LUK 6:46 “Vika munjitumbuila ngueni, ‘Muene, Muene’, vuno honi kumulingi vinjimileka?
LUK 6:47 Njimileka cifua cendi uoshe uje eja kuli yange na kuvuilila mezi ange na kuuononoka.
LUK 6:48 Napu ngue yala uakutungila njivo yendi, uahindile nakulovesa luvula ha livue. Livazi liezile liapupile kuje ku njivo, vuno honi kuyaningangele, omuo luvula luaije njivo luakele ha livue.
LUK 6:49 Vuno honi uoshe aziva mezi ange kuakuhona kuuononoka napu ngue yala uatungile njivo yendi kuakuhona kuhinda luvula. Omo livazi liapupile kuje ku njivo, kaha yasiukile hajevene, kuua kuayo kuapuile kuakupi cikuma!”
LUK 7:1 Omo Yesu uamanesele kuhandeka viuma vioshe evi ku vantu, kaha uaile ku Kapenama.
LUK 7:2 Mu mbonge ije muakele mukuluntu ua masualale va Loma uje uakele na ngamba yendi uaseho cikuma kuli ikeye. Uje muntu uavavalele uatondele kutsa.
LUK 7:3 Omo uje mukuluntu uovuile lutsimo lua Yesu, uatumine vamo vakuluntu va Vayunda kuli ikeye nakumulomba eje mukukanguisa ngamba yendi.
LUK 7:4 Vezile kuli Yesu vamulambelelele cikuma nguavo, “Ou yala napande kumukuasa.
LUK 7:5 Ikeye uazanga vantu vetu, naua uatutungilile njivo ya malombelo yetu.”
LUK 7:6 Yesu uaile navo, vuno honi omo uahete kuyehi na njivo, uje mukuluntu ua masualale uatumine vavusamba vendi kuli Yesu nakumuleka nguavo, “Muene, keti ukaluuise mutima uove omuo kucanjipandele yove ukakovele mu njivo yange.
LUK 7:7 Ngecivene nange naua kucanjipandele kuheta kuli yove. Handeka lika lizi, kaha ngamba yange akakanguka.
LUK 7:8 Njitantekeye eci omuo nange njili muitsi lia nzili yakama, na masualale vali muitsi liange, njishika umo nguange, ‘Ya!’ kaha aya, kaha naua njishika mukuavo nguange, ‘Ija!’ kaha eja. Njihandeka kuli ngamba yange nguange, ‘Linga evi!’ kaha acilinga.”
LUK 7:9 Yesu ualikomokelele omo uovuile evi, kaha uatengulukilile kuli cije civunga camukavele, uahandekele nguendi, “Njimileka nguange, nakumo kuahi kunjinauana lutsilieloliakama ngue eli, cipue mu Isaleli luahimo.”
LUK 7:10 Omo vaje vamala vavatumine vahilukile ku njivo ya uje mukuluntu vaka uanene uje ngamba nakanguka.
LUK 7:11 Munima yevi Yesu uaile ku mbonge ya Naine, vandongisi vendi na civunga cakama vamukavele.
LUK 7:12 Omo ikeye uahete kuyehi na cikolo ca mbonge, kaha vantu vatuhuile civimbi ha mbanza, uje yala uatsile uapuile muana umolika uaumo ntuluue, kaha civunga cakama cahumine muje mu limbo cakele hamo nauje ntuluue.
LUK 7:13 Omo Muene Yesu uamumuene, kaha uamuivuilile cikeketima, kaha uahandekele kuli ikeye nguendi, “Keti ulile.”
LUK 7:14 Ambahoni Yesu uaile uakakuate ku citala tala, kaha vaje tufunde vemanene. Yesu uahandekele nguendi, “Ove kankalava, njikuleka nguange, hinduka!”
LUK 7:15 Kaha uje yala uatsile uasangukile uatumamene na kuputuka kuhandeka, kaha Yesu uamuhanene kuli vaina.
LUK 7:16 Vantu voshe vovuile liova, kaha vashangazalele Njambi, vahandekele nguavo, “Kananguizi ua Njambi uakama neja kuli yetu na Njambi neja nakuovola vantu vendi!”
LUK 7:17 Kaha lutsimo olu lua Yesu luashandokelele mu Yundeya muoshe na ku vinganda vioshe via kulihata.
LUK 7:18 Omo vandongisi va Iuano vamulekele viuma vioshe evi, kaha uasaneneko vandongisi vendi vavali.
LUK 7:19 Uavatumine kuli Muene Yesu nakumuihula nguavo, “Yove vene uija? Indi tuvandameneko ueka naua.”
LUK 7:20 Omo vamala vezile kuli Yesu vahandekele nguavo, “Iuano muka kumbuitika natutumu kuli yove nakuihula nga yove uje eja indi tucivandameneko ueka naua.”
LUK 7:21 Ha ntsimbu ijevene Yesu uakanguisile vantu vavengi ku kuvavala kuavo, naku mishongo yavo nakuhumisa mahamba na kumuesa tupuputua vavengi.
LUK 7:22 Kaha uatavele vandongisi va Iuano nguendi, “Yemuye mukahandeke kuli Iuano vimunamono nevi vimunevu. Tupuputua vamona, vilema venda, vaka mbumba vanalele, tusinda matuitui vaziva, vatsi vasanguka, kaha muzimbu uacili vauambulula kuli tuhutu.
LUK 7:23 Vanavezika vaje kuvakecela lutsilielo luavo muli yange.”
LUK 7:24 Omo vandongisi va Iuano vahilukile, kaha Yesu ualekele cije civunga hali Iuano nguendi, “Omo muaile kuli Iuano mu mpambo muatondele kukamona muntu ua vati? Indi muaile mukumona yala uakufua ngue vishoni via laha viakutepuzoka na mpunzi?
LUK 7:25 Muaile nakumona vika honi? Muntu nazala vuzalo vuasenga ndi? Vantu vakakuzala muacili na kukala muasenga vakakala mu mihela ya muene.
LUK 7:26 Njilekeni muatondele kukamona vikahoni? Muatondele kukamona kananguizi ua Njambi ndi? Eyo, ikeye vene naua ikeye kananguizi ua Njambi uakama.
LUK 7:27 Ou ikeye Iuano uje visoneka vihandeka nguavio, ‘Njikatuma kanganda kange kulutue luove. Akavuahesa ngila yove.’
LUK 7:28 Njimileka nguange, ku vantu voshe vaje vanakeleko, naumo uahi napulaka Iuano. Vuno honi uje uamundende kumaneselela mu vumuene vua Njambi ikeye napulakana Iuano.”
LUK 7:29 Vantu voshe hamo na vaka kutambula lisimo vononokele vusunga vua Njambi, kaha vavambuitikile kuli Iuano.
LUK 7:30 Vuno honi Vafaliseo na valongisi va Mashiko a Mosesa vavianene vilinga via Njambi hali vakevo, mukemo kuva vambuitikile kuli Iuano.
LUK 7:31 Yesu uahandekele nguendi, “Kuliveya njasa kusetekesa vantu va matangua ano? Vanapu ngue vika?
LUK 7:32 Vakevo vanapu ngue vanike vanatumama kumuhela uakulandesela viuma, kaha valitambakana umo na mukuavo, ‘Tunamimbilile miaso ya vushombolua, vuno honi kumuakinine! Tuamimbilile miaso ya vusiua vuno honi kumua lilile!’
LUK 7:33 Omo Iuano muka kumbuitika uezile, kalile mbolo cipue kunua viniu, kaha muahandekele ngueni, ‘Ali na mahamba!’
LUK 7:34 Kaha omo Muna Muntu uezile, ikeye ualile nakunua, kaha muahandekele ngueni, ‘Taleni ou yala! Uapua mukamutupu na kupenda, kaha kavusamba ua vaka kutambula lisimu na vaka vupi!’
LUK 7:35 Ngoco vene mana vana amuesa kupua acili kuvuyoye vua vaje vauakava.”
LUK 7:36 Litangua limo umo ua Vafaliseo ualizanga lia Simon ualaniene Yesu kulia nendi, kaha uakovelele mu njivo Yakafaliseo nakutumama ku mesa.
LUK 7:37 Kuakele mpuevo ua mu mbonge ije, uapuile muka vupi. Omo uovuile nguendi Yesu hali na kulia mu njivo ya Kafaliseo, uanehele kantsazi kacili ka mazi aluengo luacili.
LUK 7:38 Kaha uemanene kunima ya viliato via Yesu, na kulila kaha uaputukile kujulisa viliato via Yesu na misozi yendi, kaha uavihundile navi nkambu viendi naku tsuemba ku viliato viendi, kaha uamuitilile mazi kumikono.
LUK 7:39 Omo Kafaliseo uje uamusanene uamuene eci, uahandekele kuli ikeye vavenia nguendi, “Nga ou yala uapuile kananguizi, nge natantekeya nacifua muka cou mpuevo na mukuata. Nge natantekeya nguendi uapua muka vupi.”
LUK 7:40 Yesu uamulekele nguendi, “njili na cuma cimo njitonda kukuleka.” Kaha uatavele nguendi, “Cikahoni Mulongisi?”
LUK 7:41 Yesu uamutililile nguendi, “Kuakele vamala vavali vakumuine vimbongo kuli muka kukumuisa. Umo uakumuine vimbongo via Siliva viakupua vihita vitanu, mukuavo naua uakumuine vimbongo via Siliva makumi atanu.
LUK 7:42 Omo vahonouele kuvihiluisa, uava konekelele voshe vavali. Hakati kavo iya uje akamuzanga cikuma?”
LUK 7:43 Simoni uamukumbuluile nguendi, “Njasinganieka nguange uje yakonekelele cikuma.” Kaha Yesu uahandekele kuli ikeye nguendi, “Una yulu muacili.”
LUK 7:44 Tala ou mpuevo, kaha lisikanieke yove vavenia. Kaha uatengulukilile kuli mpuevo na kuhandekele kuli Simoni nguendi, “Uamumono ou mpuevo? Njakovelele mu njivo yove, kuuanjihanene mema akutana ku viliato viange, vuno honi najulisa viliato viange na misozi yendi na kunjihunda na vinkambu viendi.
LUK 7:45 Unahonouele cipue kunjitsuemba, vuno honi kuhuma ntsimbu njakovelele muno mu njivo yove kecelele kutsuemba viliato viange.
LUK 7:46 Kuuanjitambuile mukunjitila mazi ku mutue uange, vuno honi ikeye nanjitila mazi aluengo kuviliato viange.
LUK 7:47 Njimileka, vanamukonekela vupi vuavuingi mukemo uakala nacizangango cikuma, vuno honi uje vanakonekela muvundende, uazanga via vindende.”
LUK 7:48 Kaha Yesu uahandekele kuli uje mpuevo nguendi, “Vipi vuove vana vanavikonekela.”
LUK 7:49 Kaha vaje vakele nendi ku mesa vaputukile kusinganieka nguavo, “Iya ou, asa kukonekela vipi?”
LUK 7:50 Kaha uahandekele kuli mpuevo nguendi, “Lutsilielo luove lua kusambuesa. Ya mu ciyulo.”
LUK 8:1 Hanima yevi, Yesu uakele nakuendangana mu vimbonge na mu membo, nakuambulula muzimbu uacili ua vumuene vua Njambi. Vavandongisi vendi likumi na vavali vaile hamo
LUK 8:2 Navampuevo vamo vaile hamo nendi. Yesu uahumisile mahamba muli vakevo na kuvakanguisa ku mishongo yavo. Umo uavo uapuile Maliya mangandalena muli ikeye uahumisile mahamba atanu na avali.
LUK 8:3 Mukuavo uapuile Njuana mpuevo ya Kuza, mukuluntu uakulama vitenga via mu njivo ya Helonde, Mukuavo uapuile Susana na vakuavo vavengi. Ava vampuevo vakele nakukuasa Yesu na vandongisi vendi navukuasi vua vimbongo viavo.
LUK 8:4 Litangua limo vantu vavengi vezile nakukunguluka amo. Vahumine kuvi mbonge via vingi via kuli sezaseza kua kuivuilila Yesu. Uavatelele cisimo eci:
LUK 8:5 Muka kulima uaile na kukuna vimbuto viendi. Omo uakele nakukuna vimbuto viendi, imo yauililile kumukulo ua ngila kaha vantu valiatangeleleho na tuzila vailile.
LUK 8:6 Imo yauililile ha mavue kaha omo yamenene, yomine omuo kuya uanene mema.
LUK 8:7 Imo ya vimbuto yauililile ha mingonga, ha kukola kuayo vaituvile ku mingonga.
LUK 8:8 Vikuavo vimbuto via uililile ha mavu a vuilo, mbuto imo lika ya tuihuile cihita cavimbuto. Kaha Yesu uamanesele kuhandeka nguendi, “Uje uoshe hali na matuitui, azive!”
LUK 8:9 Vandongisi va Yesu Kilistu vamuihuile nguavo, Yesu, eci cisimo cilumbununa vika?
LUK 8:10 Uavakumbuluile nguendi, “Njambi namihangula linga mutantekeye vushueka vua vumuene vuendi, vuno honi kuli vamo njihandeka mu visimo linga, ‘Cipue vamona, vuno honi kuvamonesesa, cipue vovua vuno honi kuvovuisisa.’ ”
LUK 8:11 “Eci cikeco cilumbununa ca cisimo: mbuto ikeyo lizi lia Njambi.
LUK 8:12 Vimbuto vije via uililile kumukulo ua ngila vili ngue vantu vevua lizi lia Njambi. Kaha satana eja na kuambata lizi mu mitima yavo, linga keti vakulahele na kuyoyesiua.
LUK 8:13 Vimbuto viauililile ha mavu a mavue vinapu ngue vantu vaje vatambula lizi nakuvuahelelela omo valivua, vuno honi kuvesi na mizi. Ha ntsimbu ya vieseko vahilukila munima.
LUK 8:14 Vimbuto viauililile ha mingonga vinapu ngue vantu vaje vevua lizi lia Njambi, vuno honi kulinienga, vufuko na senga via vuyoye via vatuvile. Kaha kuviakolele na kuima vushuka.
LUK 8:15 Vuno honi vimbuto vije via uililile ha mavu acili vinapu ngue vantu vacili vaje vali na mitima yacili, vovua lizi lia Njambi na kuliniunga na kukolesa ngo noho vema vushuka.
LUK 8:16 “Naumo uahi a shuameka ndeya na kuishueka muintsi lia liendeko cipue kuyaka muintsi lia muhela. Vuno honi vaihaka helu lia citumbiko linga uoshe akovela amone ceke.
LUK 8:17 Vioshe vije vanashueke hano vikajomboloka na vioshe vije via kushueka hano vakavitantekeya, na kuvineha ha ceke.
LUK 8:18 Mukemo muapande kuivuilila muacili kuvilongesa viange. Vaje vali navimo vakatambula viavingi vuno honi voshe kuvesi nacimo vakavanieka cipue vije viavindende vivasinganieka nguavo valinavio.”
LUK 8:19 Kaha vaina ya Yesu na vamuanaye vezile kuli ikeye na kumumona, vuno honi vahonouele kushuena kuli ikeye omuo ya vantu vuingi.
LUK 8:20 Umo ua vantu vaje vakele kuje uamulekele nguendi, “Vanoko na vamuanoko vanemana hambanza, vatonda ku kumona.”
LUK 8:21 Yesu uamukumbuluile nguendi, “Vanana na vamuanetu vaje vaziva mezi a Njambi na kuakavangeya.”
LUK 8:22 Litangua limo Yesu uakovelele mu vuato na vandongisi vendi kaha uahandekele nguendi, “Tuyeni musinia lia cisali.” Kaha vaputukile kuya.
LUK 8:23 Omo vakele nakujavuka Yesu uaile mutulo. Linkimba liaputukile mu cisali, ngeci na vuato vuaputukile kushula na mema, kaha vakele muvukalu.
LUK 8:24 Vandongisi vaile nakumuhindula, nguavo, “Muene, Muene, tuli nakunonga!” Uahindukile kaha uashikile mpunzi na mankimba, kaha vioshe vialikelele na kuholoka.
LUK 8:25 Uavehuile nguendi, “Lutsilielo lueni luli kuli?” Mu liova na mukukomoka valihuezele umo na mukuavo nguavo, “Iya ou? Ashika mpunzi na mema, kaha vimuononoka.”
LUK 8:26 Yesu na vandongisi viendi vajavukilile ku cihela kuje vantu va Ngalasene vakele nakuyoya, cije cakele musinia lia cisali kuhuma ku Ngalileya.
LUK 8:27 Omo Yesu uahete ha ntunda, uali uanene na yala uje uakele na lihamba uamuje mbonge. Ntsimbu yailaha ou yala kakele nakuzala vuzalo cipue kukala hembo, vuno honi uakele nakukala lika ku vihilo.
LUK 8:28 Omo uamuene Yesu ualilile cikuma na kuuila ku mikono yendi, kaha uatambakanene nguendi, “Utonda kulinga vika kuli yange, Yesu Muna Njambi Uakuhiana? Njikulomba keti unjiyandese!”
LUK 8:29 Uje yala uahandekele evi omuo Yesu uahandekele kuli lije lihamba linga lihume muli uje yala. Vintsimbu viavingi viakele nakumuyandesa. Vantu vakele na kumukuta na malienge ku mavoko na ku mikono naku muniunga, vuno honi uakele nakuvatula kaha lihamba liakele nakumutuala mu musenge.
LUK 8:30 Yesu uamuihuile nguendi, “Lizina liove yove iya?” Kaha uamukumbuluile nguendi, “Tuvavengi,” omuo mahamba vavengi vakovelele muli ikeye.
LUK 8:31 Kaha mahamba vamulombele kushuakumo nguavo keti avatuale mu cina ca kuhona cimbaluila.
LUK 8:32 Kuakele vangulu vavengi vakele na kulia kumukulo ua munkinda. Kaha mahamba valombele Yesu nguavio vika kovele muli vaje vangulu, kaha uavitavesele.
LUK 8:33 Omo mahamba ahumine muli uje yala, aile muli vaje vangulu, kaha vaje vangulu vahumine ha munkinda vashatukilile mu cisali na kunonga.
LUK 8:34 Omo vaje vaka kuniunga vangulu vamuene vije vialingiuile, vashatukile naku kambulula mu mbonge na mu membo akulihata.
LUK 8:35 Kaha vantu vaile na kumona ovio vialingiuile. Omo vahete kuli Yesu, vamuene uje yala yahumisile mahamba natumama ku viliato via Yesu, nazala na visinganieka viendi viakele muacili, kaha vateuele.
LUK 8:36 Vaje va vimuene valekele vantu muje uje yala uakele na mahamba muamu kanguisile.
LUK 8:37 Kaha vantu voshe vamu mbonge ya Ngalasa na vakumihela yakulihata valombele Yesu nguavo, ahume kuli vakevo omuo vateuele cikuma. Kaha Yesu uakovelele mu vuato na kulivuahesela linga aye.
LUK 8:38 Uje yala ya humisile mahamba ualombele Yesu nguendi, “Njikukave!” Vuno honi Yesu uavianene ua handekele nguendi,
LUK 8:39 “Hiluka kuimbo ukavaleke viakama viana kulingila Njambi.” Kaha uje yala uaile na kuleka vantu mu mbonge vije Yesu namu lingilavio.
LUK 8:40 Omo Yesu uahilukile ku Ngalileya, vantu vavengi vamutambuile, omuo voshe vakele naku muvandamena.
LUK 8:41 Kaha yala umo uezile kuli Yesu. Lizina liendi Njailusi mukuluntu ua njivo ya malombelo. Uauile ku viliato via Yesu na kumulomba nguendi, aye ku njivo yendi,
LUK 8:42 omuo munendi umo lika ua miaka likumi na ivali, uatondele kutsa. Yesu uaile hamo nendi. Omo vakele nakuya civunga ca vantu vakele nakusindakana Yesu.
LUK 8:43 Mu civunga cije vene muakele mpuevo uakele na mushongo uakuhita maninga ha miaka likumi na ivali vuno honi naumo uahi uamukanguisile.
LUK 8:44 Uezile munima ya Yesu kaha uakuate ku mukunduilo ua vuzalo vuendi, kaha hajevene kuhita maninga kuemanene.
LUK 8:45 Yesu uehuile nguendi, “Iya nanjikuata?” Omo voshe vavianene Petulu uahandekele nguendi, “Muene vantu va kuzengeleka kaha naua vakusindakana.”
LUK 8:46 Vuno honi Yesu uahandekele nguendi, “Umo nanjikuata, omuo njatantekeya nguange nzili yahumu muli Yange.”
LUK 8:47 Kaha uje mpuevo ha kumona nge vanamutantekeya. Uezile nakujaja na kuuila ku viliato via Yesu. Kaha ku mesho a civunga ca vantu uahandekele omuo vika uakuatele Yesu nomu muana kangukila mu vuasi.
LUK 8:48 Kaha Yesu uahandekele kuli ikeye nguendi, “Munange, lutsilielo luove lua Kukuangisa. Ya na ciyulo.”
LUK 8:49 Tele Yesu uakele nakuhandeka, umo uezile kuhuma ku njivo ya Njailusi, Uahandekele nguendi, “Munove ua mpuevo natsi keti uyandese mulongisi naua.”
LUK 8:50 Ha kuivua eci, Yesu uahandekele kuli Njailusi nguendi, “keti uzive liova, kulahela lika, akayoya naua.”
LUK 8:51 Omo Yesu uahete ku njivo ya Njailusi, katavesele muntu kukovela nendi kuvanga Petulu, na luano, na Yakomba, na vaishe na vaina vauje mumbanda.
LUK 8:52 Ha ntsimbu ije, vantu voshe vakele nakulinienga na kulila. Kaha Yesu uahandekele nguendi, “Eceleni kulila, katsile vuno honi nakosa tulo.”
LUK 8:53 Vamujolele, omuo vatantekeyele nguavo natsi.
LUK 8:54 Kaha Yesu uaile kuje kumuhela kuakele uje mumbanda kaha uamukuate ku livoko na kumusana nguendi, “Kanike, hinduka!”
LUK 8:55 Muono uendi uahilukile kaha ha ntsimbu ijevene uemanene. Kaha Yesu ualekele visemi linga vamuhane viakulia alie.
LUK 8:56 Visemi vendi vali komokelele, kaha Yesu uavashikile keti valeke cipue umo via lingiuile.
LUK 9:1 Yesu uasanene vandongisi likumi na vavali veje kuli ikeye, kaha uavahanene nzili yakama ya kuhumisa mahamba voshe na kukanguisa mishongo.
LUK 9:2 Kaha uavatumine kuya na kuambulula Vumuene vua Njambi na kukanguisa vaka kuvavala.
LUK 9:3 Uavalekele nguendi, “Keti muambate cuma cimo ha vungenzi vueni, cipue mbueti, cipue cola, cipue viakulia, cipue vimbongo, cipue vikovelo vivali.
LUK 9:4 Kuoshe kuje kuvaka mitambula muacili, tumameni ku njivo ijevene noho mukahuma mu mbonge ije.
LUK 9:5 Kuoshe kuje vaka viana kumitambula, kaha humeni mu mbonge ije, kaha totomoneni likungu ku viliato vieni. Eci cikapua cinangulo ku vantu vamuje mu mbonge nge Njambi akavasompesa.”
LUK 9:6 Kaha vandongisi vaile, vaihitanganene mu membo oshe na kuambulula Muzimbu Uacili na kukanguisa vantu uoshe.
LUK 9:7 Omo Helonde, muka kusuana mu Ngalileya, uovuile viuma vioshe vialingiuile, kaha uakele na citanga, omuo vantu vamo vakele nakuhandeka nguavo, “Iuano muka kumbuitika nasanguka ku vatsi.”
LUK 9:8 Kaha vamo nguavo, kananguizi ua Njambi Eliya nasholoka, vamo nguavo, “Umo ua tunanguizi va Njambi veka va Njambi valaja nasanguka naua.”
LUK 9:9 Kaha Helonde uahandekele nguendi, “Iuano njamutapele mutue, vuno honi iya honi ou yala injili nakuvua viendi?” Kaha uatondele cikuma kumumona Yesu.
LUK 9:10 Tunganda va Yesu vahilukile vamulekele vioshe vije vivalingile. Kaha uaile hamo navo uavatualele kualikaliavo lika ku mbonge ivatumbuile Mbetesainda.
LUK 9:11 Omo civunga ca vantu vovuile evi, kaha vamukavele. Uavatambuile na kuvalongesa via Vumuene vua Njambi na kukanguisa vaje vakele nakuvavala.
LUK 9:12 Omo kuapuile cinguezi, vandongisi vaje likumi na vavali vezile kuli ikeye vahandekele nguavo, “Shandola vivunga evi linga vaye ku membo na ku mehia aua amuyehi vaka liuaneneko viakulia vakevo vavenia noku kuakukosa, omuo muno munapu mu musenge uangoco.”
LUK 9:13 Vuno honi Yesu uahandekele kuli vakevo nguendi, “Yeni vene vahaneni viakulia linga valie.” Kaha vamukumbuluile nguavo, “Kutuesi na viakulia vieka kuvanga vimbolo vitanu na vatsi vavali. Nkuma yove utonda tuye na kulanda viakulia via civunga coshe eci ndi?”
LUK 9:14 Kuakele vamala vakupua makulukazi atanu kuakuhona vampuevo na vanike kuje. Yesu uahandekele kuli vandongisi vendi nguendi, “Lekeni vantu vatumame ha mavu mu vimunga, munga na munga mukale vantu makumi atanu.”
LUK 9:15 Vandongisi valingile ngacije na vantu voshe vatumamene ha mavu.
LUK 9:16 Kaha Yesu uatambuile vije vimbolo vitanu na vatsi vavali, uatalele muilu, kaha uatsatselele kuli Njambi, kaha uavipazuile, uavihanene kuli vandongisi vendi linga vavipangezele vivunga via vantu.
LUK 9:17 Voshe valile, vakutile, kaha vandongisi vakunguluile vimbazuvuila vije viasaleleho, vashulisile mitonga likumi na ivali.
LUK 9:18 Litangua limo omo Yesu uakele nakulombela kualikaliendi lika, vandongisi vendi vakele kuyehi nendi. Kaha uavehuile nguendi, “Vantu vali nakunjitumbula nguavo yange iya?”
LUK 9:19 Vamukumbuluile nguavo, “Vamo vali nakuhandeka nguavo yove Iuano Muka kumbuitika, veka naua nguavo yove Eliya, vakuavo naua nguavo yove umo ua tunanguizi va Njambi va Njambi valaja uje nasanguka.”
LUK 9:20 Kaha Yesu uavehuile nguendi, “Yeni honi munjitumbula ngueni yange iya?” Petulu uakumbuluileko nguendi, “Yove Kilistu ua Njambi.”
LUK 9:21 Ambahoni Yesu uavashikile nguendi keti valekeko muntu umo cuma eci.
LUK 9:22 Kaha uahandekele naua kuli vakevo nguendi, “Muna Muntu napande kuyanda cikuma, vakuluntu na vakuluntu va vasasendote, na valongisi va mezi a Lishiko lia Mosesa vaka muviana. Kaha vakamutuala ku kutsa, vuno honi munima ya matangua atatu, akasanguka.”
LUK 9:23 Kaha Yesu uahandekele naua kuli vantu voshe vaje vakele kuje nguendi, “Nga muntu atonda kunjikava, napande kuliviana ikeye vavenia, ambate cilindakano cendi ha litangua na litangua, kaha anjikavangeye.
LUK 9:24 Omuo muntu uje uoshe atonda kuniunga muono uendi auzimbalesa, vuno honi muntu uje voshe azimbalesa muono uendi omuo lizina liange akauuana.
LUK 9:25 Nga muntu afuka mavu oshe, vuno honi alinongesa ikeye vavenia na kuzimbalesa muono uendi vika akauanaho?
LUK 9:26 Nga muntu anjuvuila shuamua na vilongesa viange, kaha Muna Muntu naua nendi akamiuvuila shuamua omo akeja mu vumpau vuendi na mu vumpau vua Ishe na mu vumpau vua tungelo vakulela.
LUK 9:27 Mua vusunga njimileka nguange, kuli vamo kuno, vaje kuvakatsi kuvanga vanamono Vumuene vua Njambi.”
LUK 9:28 Munima ya matangua atanu na atatu omo uahandekele viuma evi, Yesu uaile hamo na Petulu, na Iuano, na Yakomba ku munkinda nakulombela.
LUK 9:29 Ntsimbu uakele nakulombela, cihanga cendi cahimbukile, kaha vuzalo vuendi vuatokele too ngue ceke.
LUK 9:30 Hajevene vamala vavali vasholokele vaputukile kuhandeka nendi, vapuile Mosesa na Eliya.
LUK 9:31 Vakele mu misha ya muilu. Vakele nakuhandeka na Yesu ha kuija kua kutsa cendi mu Yelusalema muje muakashulisililamo vutumbe vua Njambi.
LUK 9:32 Petulu na vaje vakele navo vakele mu tulo, vuno honi omo vahindukile vamuene misha ya Yesu na vamala vavali vaje vemanene navo.
LUK 9:33 Omo Mosesa na Eliya vatonde kuya, kaha Petulu uahandekele kuli Yesu nguendi, “Muene, cacili kuli yetu nga tukala kuno! Tutunga vintsingi vitatu, imo yove, imo ya Mosesa na imo ya Eliya.” Kazivukile vije viakele nakuhandeka.
LUK 9:34 Ntsimbu Petulu uakele nakuhandeka, lishelua liezile na kuvafuika, kaha vandongisi vazivile liova omo lishelua liavafuikile.
LUK 9:35 Kaha lizi liahumine mu lishelua liahandekele kuli vakevo ngualio, “Ou ikeye Munange injinahangula, muivuilileni!”
LUK 9:36 Omo lizi liaholokele, Yesu uakele halikaliendi lika. Kaha vandongisi vaholokele kuluu ha viuma vioshe evi, kaha ha ntsimbu ije kuvalekeleko muntu umo viuma vije vivamuene.
LUK 9:37 Omo kuacele Yesu na vandongisi vendi vatatu vashulukile ku munkinda, civunga cakama caliuanene na Yesu.
LUK 9:38 Yala umo ua haje ha civunga uatambakanene nguendi, “Mulongisi, njikulomba tala munange, omuo ikeye lika umolika.
LUK 9:39 Evi vikevio vikalingika lihamba nga limu uana, kaha atambeka na kushinia na kututumuna lifulu ku kanua, umuvetuesa cikuma kaha kuumuecela vuasi.
LUK 9:40 Njalambelelele vandongisi vove nguange vamuhumise vuno honi kuvasele.”
LUK 9:41 Kaha Yesu uakumbuluile nguendi, “Yeni vaka kujeneka kutsiliela na vantu vaka vupi! Lungahi honi njikakala neni? Lungahi honi mukeseka kusimpa kuange?” Kaha uahandekele kuli uje yala nguendi, “Neha kuno munove.”
LUK 9:42 Omo kanike uakele nakuija, kaha lihamba liamu uisilile ha mavu na kumushiniisa cikuma. Kaha Yesu uashikile lije lihamba, uje kanike ka yala uakangukile kaha uamuhanene kuli ishe.
LUK 9:43 Kaha vantu voshe vali komokelele ha nzili yakama ya Njambi. Tele vantu voshe vakele nakulikomokela ha vioshe vije Yesu uapangele, kaha uahandekele kuli vandongisi vendi nguendi,
LUK 9:44 “Ivuilileni keti musuve evi njimileka! Muna Muntu vuavuno amuhana ku nzili ya vantu.”
LUK 9:45 Vuno honi vandongisi kuvatantekeyele mucalumbunukile cuma eci. Vavashuekelele linga keti vacitantekeye, vovuile liova liakumuihula vije viahandekele.
LUK 9:46 Kuaputukile vimpata hhakati ka vandongisi linga iya honi uakama kupulakana hhakati kavo.
LUK 9:47 Yesu uatantekeyele viyongola via mu mitima yavo, nankuma, uasanene kanike uamundende, uamuimikile kunionga yendi,
LUK 9:48 kaha uahandekele kuli vakevo nguendi, “Uoshe atambula kanike ou mu lizina liange, kaha natambula yange vene, uoshe uje anjitambula, natambula naua uje uanjitumine. Omuo uoshe uje napu uamundende hhakati keni muvavoshe, ikeye napu uakama kupulakana.”
LUK 9:49 Iuano uahandekele nguendi, “Muene, tuamuene yala umo uakele nakuhumisa mahamba mu lizina liove, kaha tuamulekele linga alikele, omuo ikeye keti uamu munga yetu.”
LUK 9:50 Yesu uahandekele nguendi, “Keti mumuvindike, omuo uoshe uje kamiluisa ikeye hali hamo neni.”
LUK 9:51 Omo matangua ashuenene kuyehi linga Yesu vamutuale muilu, uatenguluile viyongola viendi, nakuya ku Yelusalema.
LUK 9:52 Uatumine vamo va vandongisi vendi kulutue, kaha vaile na kukovela mu limbo lia muka Samaliya linga vaka muvuahesele vualumo kuakuhetela.
LUK 9:53 Vuno honi vantu vakele kuje kuva mutambuile, omuo vungenzi vuendi vuakele vuakuya ku Yelusalema.
LUK 9:54 Omo vandongisi vendi Yakomba na Iuano vamuene evi, vahandekele nguavo, “Muene, utonda linga tusane tuhia tua muilu tuije na kuvanongesa?”
LUK 9:55 Vuno honi Yesu uatengulukile kuli vakevo na kuvavindika.
LUK 9:56 Kaha vaile ku limbo likuavo.
LUK 9:57 Omo Yesu na vandongisi vendi vakele nakuya mu ngila, yala umo uahandekele kuli Yesu nguendi, “Njikakukava kuoshe kuuya.”
LUK 9:58 Yesu uahandekele kuli ikeye nguendi, “Vambanje vali na vina, na tuzila vali na mashua, vuno honi Muna Muntu kesi naha ha kusatela mutue uendi.”
LUK 9:59 Kaha Yesu uahandekele kuli yala mukuavo nguendi, “Njikave.” Vuno honi uje yala uahandekele nguendi, “Muene, ha kulivanga njitave njihiluke njikatsinde tahi tate.”
LUK 9:60 Yesu uamukumbuluile nguendi, “Seza vaka kutsa valitsinde vakevo vavenia. Yove ya na kuambulula via Vumuene vua Njambi.”
LUK 9:61 Yala mukuavo uahandekele nguendi, “Njikakukava Muene, vuno honi ha kulivanga njitave njiye njikasalese tahi vavushoko vuange.”
LUK 9:62 Yesu uahandekele kuli ikeye nguendi, “Nga umo naputuka kulima na vangombe kaha atala kunima vipangi viendi kuvikapu viaseho. Mucifua cimo vene nga umo anjikava kaha atenguluka kunima kuvipangi viendi vialaja kakapu uaseho kupanga vipangi mu Vumuene vua Njambi.”
LUK 10:1 Hanima yevi Muene Yesu uahanguile vandongisi makumi atanu na avali vakuavo. Kaha uavatumine kulutue luendi vavali na vavali vaye mu vimbonge namu vihela kuje vavenia uatondele kuya.
LUK 10:2 Tele kanda vaye uahandekele kuli vakevo nguendi, “Kuteja kuakama, vuno honi vaka kuteja vavandende. Kaha ihuleni Muene ua kuteja atume vaka kuteja mu lihia liendi.
LUK 10:3 Yeni! Njimituma kupua ngue vampanga mukati ka tungunga.
LUK 10:4 Keti muambate vikuama cipue vingonga cipue vinkaku, kaha keti mumeneke muntu uoshe mu ngila.
LUK 10:5 Ntsimbu yoshe nga mukovela mu njivo, cakulivanga handekeni ngueni, ‘Ciyulo cikale mu njivo ino.’
LUK 10:6 Nga muli muntu uayulo mu njivo ije, ciyulo ceni cikakala hali vakevo, nga keti ngoco kaha cikamihilukila.
LUK 10:7 Tumameni mu njivo ije, nueni na kulia vioshe vamihana, omuo muka kupanga napande kutambula fueto yendi. Keti muendangane ku njivo na njivo.
LUK 10:8 Nga mukovela mu mbonge na vantu vamo vamitambula, lieni vivana mivuahesela.
LUK 10:9 Kanguiseni vaka kuvavala valimo, kaha handekeni kuli vakevo ngueni, ‘Vumuene vua Njambi vuneja muyehi neni.’
LUK 10:10 Vuno honi nga mukovela mu mbonge ku vamitambula, kaha yeni mu vingila muhandeke ngueni,
LUK 10:11 ‘Cipue likungu lia mu mbonge yeni lili kumikono yetu tulitotomona linga limilemuise. Vuno honi tantekeyeni eci: Vumuene vua Njambi vuneja.’
LUK 10:12 Njimileka, ha litangua lia Cisompelo vukalu vua vantu vamu Sondoma vukapua nahongano kupulakana vantu vamu mbonge ije!
LUK 10:13 “Tuyando kuli yeni vantu vamu Kolazini! Tuyando kuli yeni naua vantu vamu Mbetesainda! Nga evi vikomoueso vivalingile mu vimbonge vieni, nge njavipangele mu vinganda via vaje keti Vayunda va mu Tile na Sindone vakevo vaje vantu nge vatengulukile laja ha kuzala vijeke naku likuita muto.
LUK 10:14 Ha litangua lia Cisompelo, vukalu vua vantu vamu Tile na Sindone vukapuako nahongano kupulakana vueni.
LUK 10:15 Yeni Vantu va mu Kapenama mutonda vaka mijundule kuheta na kuilu ndi? Houe, vaka mineha ha mavu nakuya mu Ngehena!”
LUK 10:16 Yesu ualekele vandongisi vendi nguendi, “Ou evuilila yeni novuilila yange, omuo ou aviana yeni naviana naua yange, kaha nou aviana yange naviana naua nauje ua njitumine.”
LUK 10:17 Vaje makumi atanu na avali vahilukile nakuvuahelela, na kuhandeka nguavo, “Muene mu lizina liove na mahamba a tuvuililile omo tuakele nakuuahumisa!”
LUK 10:18 Kaha Yesu uahandekele kuli vakevo nguendi, “Eyo! Njamuene Satana aua kuilu ngue muhiato.
LUK 10:19 Taleni, njamihana nzili ya kuliata manoka na manieue, na nzili yoshe ya citozi, kaha na cimo cahi cika mivetuesa.
LUK 10:20 Cipue ngocovene, keti muvuahelele hali eci lika, ngueni na mahamba amivuililile, vuno honi vuaheleleni cikuma ngueni mazina eni vana asoneka muilu.”
LUK 10:21 Ha ntsimbu ijevene Yesu ua vuahelelele mu Cimbembesi ca Kulela kaha uahandekele nguendi, “Njikusatsela Tate, Muene ua muilu na mavu, omuo unashueka viuma evi ku vaka mana na vaka kuzangama kaha uavisholola ku vanike vavandende, cili Tate, eci cikeco ca kuvuaheselele naco.
LUK 10:22 “Tate nanjihana viuma vioshe. Naumo uahi atantekeya Muana kuvanga Ishe cipue naumo uahi atantekeya Ishe kuvanga Muana. Na Muana akasholola Ishe kuli vaje vatonda.”
LUK 10:23 Kaha uatengulukile kuli vandongisi vendi na kuhandeka kuli vakevo ku mukulo nguendi, “Avezika aje mesho amona vije vimu mona!
LUK 10:24 Njimileka nguange vavengi tunanguizi va Njambi va Njambi na vamiene vazangele kumona vimumona, vuno honi kuva vimuene, naua vatondele kuivua vimuli na kuivua, vuno honi kuva vivuile.”
LUK 10:25 Hajevene mulongisi ua mashiko uemanene kueseka Yesu nguendi, “Mulongisi,” “Njilinge vati njikakale na muono ua yaye?”
LUK 10:26 Yesu uamuihuile nguendi, “Vika vanasoneka mu Lishiko lia Mosesa? Vika ukatandamo?”
LUK 10:27 Uamukumbuluile nguendi, “Zanga Muene Njambi yove na mutima uove uoshe, na muono uove uoshe, na nzili yove yoshe, na visinganieka viove vioshe, kaha zanga mukueni ngue omo nalivanga yove vavenia.”
LUK 10:28 Kaha Yesu uahandekele kuli ikeye nguendi, “Uahandeka muacili, linga eci, kaha ukakala muono ua yaye.”
LUK 10:29 Vuno honi uje mulongisi uatondele kulimuesa ikeye vavenia, uehuile Yesu nguendi, “Mukuetu ikeye iya?”
LUK 10:30 Yesu uamukumbuluile mu cisimo nguendi, “Litangua limo kuakele yala umo uahumine ku Yelusalema nakuya ku Yeliko, kaha ua liuanene na vezi. Vamuivilile vuzalo vuendi, na kumuveta na kuteua, na kumuseza na lezumuka.
LUK 10:31 Kaha capuile nge cakukasumuka, kasasendote uaile mu ngila ijevene, kaha omo uamuene ou yala, uamuongolokele kumukulo.
LUK 10:32 Na Kalevi naua omo uahete kucihela cije uamumuene nendi naua kaha uamuongolokele.
LUK 10:33 Kaha ka Samaliya umo uakele nakuhita mu ngila ije, omo uahete kucihela cije kuakosele uje yala kaha ua mumuene, kaha ua muivuilile cikeketima.
LUK 10:34 Uashuenene kuyehi na kumuzenga ha vimbandu, kaha uamuhakeleho mazi na viniu. Kaha uamuhakele ha Cimulu cendi na kumutuala ku njivo ya vangenzi, naku kamuniungilako.
LUK 10:35 Hakuca ca litangua uambate vimbongo viamu uayauaya vivali na kuhana muka kuniunga njivo ya vangenzi, kaha uahandekele kuli ikeye nguendi, ‘Umuniunge muacili,’ kaha omo njikahiluka nja kukufueta vioshe vije viulinakulikuasesa.”
LUK 10:36 Hanima yevi Yesu uehuile uje mulongisi ua mezi a mashiko a Mosesa nguendi, “Iya hhakati ka vantu ava vatatu uje uapuile ngue mukuavo ou yala, uje uauililile mu mavoko a vezi?”
LUK 10:37 Kaha uahandekele nguendi, “Uje uamumuesele ngozi.” Kaha hanima yevi Yesu uahandekele kuli ikeye nguendi, “Eyo, ya ukalinge ngoco.”
LUK 10:38 Omo Yesu na vandongisi vendi vaile mu ngila, vahete hembo haje hakele mpuevo ua lizina lia Mata ikeye uamutambuile mu njivo yendi.
LUK 10:39 Uakele na munaina Maliya, ou ua tumamene ku viliato via Yesu na kuivuilila viakele na kuhandeka.
LUK 10:40 Vuno honi Mata uakele nakulinga vipangi viavingi, kaha uezile kuli Yesu na kumuihula nguendi, “Muene, kuumono munanana na njecelela vipangi vioshe likaliange? Muleke anjikuaseko.”
LUK 10:41 Vuno honi Yesu uamukumbuluile nguendi, “Mata, Mata, yove ua lijujukila na kunienguela vipangi viavingi.
LUK 10:42 Vuno honi cuma cimo citondeka. Maliya na hangula cuma cacili, oco ku cikahumisila kuli ikeye.”
LUK 11:1 Litangua limo Yesu uakele kumuhela umo na kulombela kuli Njambi. Omo uamanesele kulombela, umo ua vandongisi vendi uamuhandekesele nguendi, “Muene tulongese kulombela, ngue Iuano muka kumbuitika muana longeselele vandongisi vendi.”
LUK 11:2 Yesu uavalekele nguendi, “Omo mulombela kuli Njambi lombeleni ngueni, “Tatetu valemese lizina liove lia kulela vumuene vuove vuije.
LUK 11:3 Tuhaneni cakulia cije tutonda litangua na litangua.
LUK 11:4 Tukonekele ku vipi vuetu, omuo netu tukakonekela vantu vaka kutuvulumuina, keti ututuamenene muvieseko.”
LUK 11:5 Kaha uahandekele nguendi, “Singaniekeni nge uli na kavusamba kove kaha uyako mukati kavutsiki na kumuhandekesa na kumulomba nguove, ‘Kavusamba, njantsantela njilombako vimbolo vitatu lika,
LUK 11:6 Kavusamba kange neja muvungezi vua kunjimenekela kaha kujesi naviakulia viaku mujumbula!’
LUK 11:7 Kaha uje kavusamba kove oku hali mu njivo akutava, ‘Keti unjitanganese njapata laja ku njivo kaha yange na vana vange tuakoso laja, Kunjasa kuhinduka na kukuhana cimo naua.’
LUK 11:8 Njimileka nguange, cipue ngocovene kakahinduka na kukuhana viakulia omuo uapua kavusamba kove, vuno honi akahinduka na kukuhana vioshe vije viutonda omuo akaziva shuamua kuakuhona kukuhana.
LUK 11:9 Kaha njimileka nguange, lombeni, kaha vakamihana, tondeni kaha mukauana, toteni kaha vaka mishokoliela.
LUK 11:10 Uoshe uje alomba akatambula, kaha uoshe uje atonda akauana, kaha kuli uje atota vaka mushokoluela.
LUK 11:11 Iya ishe hhakati keni, nga munendi amulomba itsi, kaha ikeye amuhana linoka?
LUK 11:12 Cipue nga amulomba mayaki amuhana linieue?
LUK 11:13 Nga yeni, vaka vupi mutantekeya kuhana viacili kuli vana veni, kaha honi Ishueni ua muilu akahanavene Cimbembesi ca Kulela kuli vaje vamulomba!”
LUK 11:14 Litangua limo Yesu uakele nakuhumisa lihamba lije vialingikile muntu kupua kaveveve. Omo lije lihamba liahumine kaha uje yala uaputukile kuhandeka. Omo vantu vamuene evi valikomokelele.
LUK 11:15 Vuno honi vamo vavo vahandekele nguavo, “Nahumisa lihamba mu nzili ya Mbelezembulu mukuluntu ua mahamba.”
LUK 11:16 Kaha vamo vatondele kumueseka, lingahoni vamulombele linga apange cikomoueso cije cimuesa nge Njambi ikeye namutumu.
LUK 11:17 Vuno honi Yesu ua tantekeyele vili mu mitima yavo, kaha uahandekele kuli vakevo nguendi, “Nga vantu vavumuene vumo valiluisa hhakati kavo vumuene vuje vukahua. Nga vantu vanjivo imo valiluisa hhakati kavo kaha ije njivo ikaua.
LUK 11:18 Nga vumuene vua Satana vuli navimunga vililuisa vikevio vavenia, kaha vumuene vuendi vukakola vatihoni? Njinehula eci omuo yeni muhandeka ngueni, njikahumisa mahamba mu nzili ya Mbelezembulu.
LUK 11:19 Honi nga njihumisa mahamba mu nzili ya Mbelezembulu, kaha vandongisi veni vaka likuasesa nzili yeya omo muvakahumisa mahamba? Eci cikeco vandongisi veni vaka mihisa.
LUK 11:20 Nga njihumisa mahamba mu nzili ya Njambi, kaha vumuene vua Njambi vuneja kuli yeni.
LUK 11:21 “Omo nga yala ua nzili nalivuahesela laja vitua viendi aniunga njivo yendi, kaha vupite vuendi vuoshe vukaniungiua muacili.
LUK 11:22 Nga uje hali na nzili ya kupulakana eje nakuluisa mukuavo na kumuhiana kaha akambata vitua vioshe via uje via kulahelele. Kaha akalipangezela na vakuavo vije vioshe vianambata.
LUK 11:23 “Kaha uoshe uje kesi kumutambela uange, muavusunga ikeye anjiluisa, kaha uoshe uje kakunguluka nange akashandola.
LUK 11:24 “Omo lihamba lihuma muli muntu, kaha liendakana mu mpambo kutalezeka muhela uakuhuimina. Nga kuliasa kuuana muhela kaha lilihandekesa likelio vavenia ngualio, ‘Njihiluka kuli muntu kuje njahumine.’
LUK 11:25 Kaha omo lihiluka liuana muhela uje uakulela vanauhaka muacili.
LUK 11:26 Kaha liya na kuneha vatanu na vavali mahamba veka vakupihia cikuma kupulakana likelio kaha vakovelamo na kukalamo. Kaha kupihia kua muntu uje kuakukotokela kupulakana kuje kua kuli vanga!”
LUK 11:27 Omo Yesu uakele nakuhandeka vije, mpuevo umo uamuje mu civunga uje uakele nakuivuilila evi uatambakanene cikuma na kuhandeka nguendi, “Uakukuisula uje mpuevo uakusemene na kukulela!”
LUK 11:28 Vuno honi Yesu uamukumbuluile nguendi, “Vakukuisula cikuma vaje vovua lizi lia Njambi naku likava!”
LUK 11:29 Omo civunga ca vantu calivuezelelele, Yesu uahandekele nguendi, “Vantu vavapi va matangua ano vatonda lika cikomoueso vuno honi kuvacimono, kuvanga lika cikomoueso ca Yona.
LUK 11:30 Ngue Yona uapuile cimueso ca vantu vamu Nanive, kaha Muna Muntu akapua cimueso ca vantu va matangua ano.
LUK 11:31 Muene uampuevo uaku Sheva akemana nakuluisa vantu va matangua ano ha litangua lia cisompelo na kuvahisa. Uahuminine kulahako kuakuivua mana a Solomoni. Kaha honi taleni! Umo uakupulakana Solomoni hali kuno, vuno honi muviana kumuivuila.
LUK 11:32 Vantu vaku Nanive vaka katuka nakuluisa vantu vamatangua ano ha litangua lia cisompelo naku vahisa. Vantu vaku Nanive vatengulukile ku vilinga viavo via vipi omo vovuile kuambulula kua Yona. Taleni honi! Uakama cikuma kupulakana Yona halikuno vuno honi muviana kumuvuilila!
LUK 11:33 “Naumo uahi asa kushuameka ndeya yendi naku ishueka cipue kuifuika na liendeko vuno honi ihaka haci tumbiko, kaha linga uoshe uje akovela mu njivo amone ceke.
LUK 11:34 Mesho ove akeuo ceke ca muvila uove. Nga mesho ove amona muacili kaha muvila uoshe ukashula na ceke, vuno honi nga mesho ove avavala kaha muvila uoshe ukapua na milima.
LUK 11:35 Kaha tantekeya muacili nguove ceke cili muli yove keti cipue milima.
LUK 11:36 Nga muvila uove uoshe uashulu na ceke, kua kuhona kapenga kamilima, kaha ukashula na ceke ngue muje ndeya muikaneha misha hali yove.”
LUK 11:37 Omo Yesu uamanesele kuhandeka, Kafaliseo umo uamulaniene linga akalie nendi. Kaha Yesu uakovelele na kutumama nakulia hamo nendi.
LUK 11:38 Kafaliseo ualikomokelele omo uamuene Yesu katanene ku mavoko endi mukulia.
LUK 11:39 Kaha Yesu uahandekele kuli ikeye nguendi, “Taleni yeni Vafaliseo muka lelesa hambanza na lilonga helu, vuno honi mukati keni muashulu na lizangamena na vupi.
LUK 11:40 Yeni vilema! Kumutantekeya ngueni, Njambi uatangele helu lieni, ikeye naua uatangele mukati ndi?
LUK 11:41 Haneni ku tuhutu muje mumuzivukila mu mitima yeni ngueni tunapande kuviana, kaha mukapua vakulela kuli Njambi cipue kuakuhona kutana ku mavoko eni.
LUK 11:42 “Tuyando kuli yeni Vafaliseo! Yeni mukahana kuli Njambi camulikumi ha viuma mukatepesa kuvia kulia ngue minte, na luku, na visapa-sapa vikuavo, vuno honi kumuekulinga muacili vantu naua kumuazangele Njambi. Evi munapande kuvilinga kuakuhona kulikela kuli vije vikuavo.
LUK 11:43 “Tuyando tueni, Vafaliseo! Yeni muazanga kutumama ha vituamo viacili mu vinjivo via malombelo, kaha muzanga vantu kumikandelela na kumihana kasingimiko mu mihela yakulandesela.
LUK 11:44 Tuyando tueni, omuo yeni muapua ngue vihilo vije viakuhona kumoneka. Vantu vakendeho nakupua vaka vupi kuakuhona kutantekeya.”
LUK 11:45 Kaha umo ua valongisi va mezi a mashiko a Mosesa uahandekele kuli Yesu nguendi, “Mulongisi, omo uli na kuhandeka evi, uli nakushaula yetu naua.”
LUK 11:46 Kaha uahandekele kuli vakevo nguendi, “Tuyando tueni, yeni naua valongisi va mezi a mashiko a Mosesa! Omuo mukatuika vantu vituika via kulema vuno honi yeni vavenia kumuekukakulako cipue na munie umo kukuasa vaje vajundula vije viteli.
LUK 11:47 Tuyando tueni, omuo mukavuahesa ha vihilo via tunanguizi va Njambi va Njambi vaje vavatsihile vakukuluila veni.
LUK 11:48 Nkuma yeni mulinavukaleho vuje mutava vije vivalingile vaje vakukuluila veni. Vatsihile tunanguizi va Njambi va Njambi na yeni muatungile vihilo viavo.
LUK 11:49 Kaha cuma eci mana a Njambi ahandeka nguauo, ‘Njikavatumina tunanguizi va Njambi va Njambi na tunganda kaha vakatsihaho vamo vavo na vamo naua muka vayandesa cikuma.’
LUK 11:50 Nkuma vantu va ntsimbu ino vaka vazangamesa ha kutsiha tunanguizi va Njambi va Njambi voshe hume hakutanga kua lifuti,
LUK 11:51 hume hakutsiha Avele nakuheta ha kutsiha Zakaliya uje vatsihilile mukati ka mutula ha Muhela Uakulela. Njimileka nguange, vantu va ntsimbu ino vaka vazangamesa voshe hali evi.
LUK 11:52 “Tuyando tueni, valongisi va mezi a mashiko a Mosesa! Omuo munanieke vantu sapi yakushokoluesa ku cikolo ca mangana, vuno honi yeni vavenia kumue kukovelamo, cipue vaje veseka kukovelamo kumue kuvatavesa!”
LUK 11:53 Omo Yesu uamanesele kuhandeka evi, uahumine kucihela kuje. Valongisi va mezi a Lishiko lia Mosesa na Vafaliseo vaputukile kumuluisa cikuma na kumuihula vihula viavingi vakumunienguesa.
LUK 11:54 Vavandamenene indi nga ahandeka via vipi linga vamukuateho.
LUK 12:1 Ha ntsimbu ije vene vivunga viakama via vantu vavengi viakungulukile hamo, vapuile vavengi mukemuo vakele na kuliliatangela umo na mukuavo, Yesu uaputukile kuhandeka kuli vandongisi vendi nguendi, “Liniungeni ku cimbaluila ca Vafaliseo, cije cikeco civembulu cavo.
LUK 12:2 Keti mupue ngue vakevo omuo nacimo cahi ca kufuika ku cikafukuliua, cipue ca kushueka kuci kajomboloka.
LUK 12:3 Viunahandeka mu milima vaka viziva mu mutania, nevi uayevetela kumuhela vaka vihandeka hambanza.”
LUK 12:4 “Njimileka vavusamba keti muteue atsiha muvila kaha kuhumaho kasa naua kulinga cuma cimo.
LUK 12:5 Vuno honi njimileka uje imunapande kuteua. Muteue uje nga namanesa kutsiha muvila, hanga hali na nzili yaku miumbila mu ngehena. Eyo, njimileka muteueni.”
LUK 12:6 “Singaniekeni tumpiasa, kutuesi naseho cipue tutanu vatulanda ha vimbingo vivali. Vuno honi naumo uahi uavo vakamusuva kuli Njambi.
LUK 12:7 Vuno honi cipue vinkambu viaku mutue uove vana vitanda. Keti muteue, muli naseho yakama cikuma kupulakana tumpiasa vavengi.
LUK 12:8 “Njimileka nguange uoshe uje ahandeka hacivunga nguendi uakundama kuli yange, na Muna Muntu naua aka muhandeka ku tungelo va Njambi.
LUK 12:9 Vuno honi uoshe uje anjiviana hakati ka civunga ca vantu, nange njikamuviana ku tungelo va Njambi.
LUK 12:10 “Uoshe ashaula Muna Muntu vaka musambesa, vuno honi uoshe atuka Cimbembesi Uakulela ku vaka musambesa.
LUK 12:11 “Omo vakamituala mu vinjivo via malombelo kuli vaka kuyula na vaka nzili mukumieseka, keti mukalinienge mu mukaliluila yeni vavenia, kuli vimukahandeka na muje mu mukavakumbuiluila,
LUK 12:12 omuo Cimbembesi Uakulela cikamilongesa ha ntsimbu ije vimuapande kukahandeka.”
LUK 12:13 Muntu umo uakele muje mu civunga uehuile Yesu nguendi, “Mulongisi, leka muanetu linga tulipangele vitenga vije tate uatusezelelele.”
LUK 12:14 Vuno honi Yesu uamukumbuluile nguendi, “Kavusamba, iya nanjihangula kupua muka kuyula cipue muka kuimanena hhakati keni?”
