LUK 12:15 Kaha uahandekele kuli vakevo nguendi, “Liniungeni! Zangameni ku miyati ya lizangamena lioshe: vuyoye vua muntu kuvuesi mu vufuko vuendi.”
LUK 12:16 Kaha uavatelele cisimo eci nguendi, “Kuakele muntu umo uakufuka mu lihia liendi muakele viakuteja viavingi.
LUK 12:17 Kaha uasinganiekele ikeye vavenia nguendi, ‘Njikalinga vati, omuo kunjesi na vishete viakama via kutulikila viakuteja viange?’
LUK 12:18 Kaha naua uahandekele nguendi, ‘Njikalinga eci, njikasiula vishete viange na kutunga viakama, muje mukemo njikahaka vimbuto viange na viuma viange vioshe.
LUK 12:19 Kaha njikahandeka ku muono uange nguange, Muono, uli na viuma viavingi unalitumbikila ha miaka yaingi, huima, lia, nua na kuvuahelela.’
LUK 12:20 Vuno honi Njambi uahandekele kuli ikeye nguendi, ‘Yove cilema! Vutsiki vuno vene muono uove vauambata. Kaha vije viuma viuna livuahesela vikapua vieya?’
LUK 12:21 “Omu mukemuo mucikapua kuli muntu uje, vikakala navaje vakalitulikila vufuko vakevo vavenia vuno honi kuva fukile ku mesho a Njambi.”
LUK 12:22 Kaha Yesu uahandekele kuli vandongisi vendi nguendi, “Nankuma njimileka nguange, keti mulinienge ha vuyoye vueni vimukalia, cipue via muvila ueni vimukazala.
LUK 12:23 Omuo vuyoye vunapu vuaseho kupulakana viakulia, na muvila kupulakana vuzalo.
LUK 12:24 Singaniekeni makololo kuve kulima cipue kuteja, kuvakele na cishete cipue muakutulikila viakulia, vuno honi Njambi alina kuvalisa. Yeni muvaseho cikuma kupulakana tuzila.
LUK 12:25 Iya hhakati keni mu kulinienga asa kuhakelako cipue ka ntsimbu kakandende ku vuyoye vuendi?
LUK 12:26 Nga kumuasa kulinga eci cuma cacindende, kaha vika muliniengela ha vioshe?
LUK 12:27 Singaniekeni vintemo muvikakolela: Kuvie kupanga cipue kulizika. Vuno honi njimileka nguange, cipue vene muene Solomoni mu vufuko vuendi vuoshe kazalele ngue vuzalo ngue vua evi.
LUK 12:28 Nga omu mukemo Njambi akazikilamo vishoni via musenge, vije vikalako lika lelo kaha imene vavintsimika mu tuhia, yeni akamizika cikuma, keti mukale nalikulahelo lialindende ngacije.”
LUK 12:29 “Keti mutualeleleho kulinienge hali vimu kalia cipue vimu kanua.
LUK 12:30 Vaka lifuti vakevo vakatondo evi vioshe viuma. Vuno honi yeni Ishueni azivuka nguendi muvitonda.
LUK 12:31 Vuno honi tondeni tahi vumuene vua Njambi, kaha navioshe evi vaka mihanavio naua.”
LUK 12:32 “Keti muvue liova yeni mpunga yaindende, Ishueni navuahelela kumihana vumuene.
LUK 12:33 Landeseni vufuko vueni nakuvuhana vimbongo kuli tuhutu. Livuaheseleni vikuama vieni vavenia vije kuvikapihia, vukevuo vufuko vua muilu vuje kuvuekuhua cipue vezi kuvasa kuvushuena na tuntembulu kuvasa kuvupihisa.
LUK 12:34 Oko kuli vufuko vuove, kukeko kukakala mutima uove.”
LUK 12:35 “Livuaheseleleni vipangi na vindeya vieni vishuame.
LUK 12:36 Pueni ngue vangamba vavandamena Muene uavo ahuma ku cilika cavulo. Omo nge eja nakutota ku cikolo ohovene kaha va mushokuelela.
LUK 12:37 Vanavezika vaje vangamba omo Muene uavo akavauana vatona na kulivuahesela nge eja. Njimileka muavusunga, Muene uavo akalizitika muiva uendi na kuvalania vatumame ku mesa na kuvahana viakulia.”
LUK 12:38 Vavezika vangamba vaje nga Muene uavo eja avauana vanalivuahesela vualuno cipue eje hhakati ka vutsiki cipue akasholoka hanima.
LUK 12:39 Naua Yesu ualekele vandongisi vendi nguendi tantekeyeni eci, “Nga vavenia njivo akatantekeya ntsimbu ije muizi akeja, nge kekuseza njivo yendi vaituve.
LUK 12:40 Neni naua muapande kuli vuahesela, omuo Muna Muntu akeja ha ntsimbu kumua livuaheselele.”
LUK 12:41 Petulu uehuile nguendi, “Muene, uli nakutulekesa eci cisimo yetu lika indi na voshe?”
LUK 12:42 Muene Yesu uamukumbuluile nguendi, “Kuakele ngamba ua mana na lutsilielo. Muene uendi uamuhakele kuendesa vakuavo vangamba nakukahana viakulia ha ntsimbu yatelamo.
LUK 12:43 Uakukuisula uje ngamba omo Muene uendi ahiluka amuuana hali laja kuvipangi.
LUK 12:44 Njimileka muavusunga, Muene uendi akamupuisa kupua mukuluntu ua vufuko vuendi vioshe.
LUK 12:45 Vuno honi vije vikalingika nga uje ngamba halihandekesa ikeye vavenia nguendi, ‘Muene uange nakotokela ha kuhiluka,’ kaha akaputuka kupupa vangamba vakuavo, va vamala nava va vampuevo na kulia na kunua na kupenda?
LUK 12:46 Nga Muene ua uje ngamba akahiluka ha litangua olio kamuvandamene na ola ije katantekeyele, akamutetanga vimpindi na kumuhaka hamo nava kakuhona kutava.
LUK 12:47 “Nga ngamba uje atantekeya viatonda Muene uendi, vuno honi kuvivuahesa kuahi cipue kalingi viatonda Muene uendi vaka mupupa na vimbanda viavingi.
LUK 12:48 Vuno honi uje katantekeya Muene uendi viatonda, kaha alinga viuma viafuila kashitiku vaka mupupa vimbanda viavindende. Kuli uoshe vanahana viavingi, viavingi naua vakatonda, kuli uje vanatulikisile viavingi, viavingi cikuma vakamuihula.
LUK 12:49 “Njezile nakuneha tuhia ha mavu, njatondo nge tunakuata laja!
LUK 12:50 Ha kulivanga njapandele kuhita mu cimbuitikilo ca tuyando tuatuingi, njinazeye kuvanga cinahiti!
LUK 12:51 Muasinganieka ngueni njinezile mukuneha ciyulo ha mavu? Houe, njimileka vuno honi njinanehe kulitepa.
LUK 12:52 Kuhuma hano ntanga ya vantu vatanu vakalitepa, vatatu valiluisa na vavali kaha vavali valiluisa na vatatu.
LUK 12:53 Vakalipanga, vaishe valuisa vana va vamala, na va vamala kuluisa vaishavo, vaina kuluisa vana vavo va vampuevo kaha na vana va vampuevo kuluisa vainavo, vaina mueno kuluisa vaniotomueno yavo, vaina mueno kuluisa vaniotomueno yavo.”
LUK 12:54 Yesu uahandekele ku civunga nguendi, “Nga mumona lishelua lihuminina kuli katokela litangua, vuasi vuasi muhandeka ngueni, ‘Ikanoka’, kaha inoka.
LUK 12:55 Kaha nga muvua mpunzi ihuminina mu mbuela, muhandeke ngueni, ‘Kukayukuma’, kaha mukemo vene.
LUK 12:56 Yeni vaka civembulu! Muatantekeya kulumbununa cifua ca mavu cipue ca melu, vuno honi vika kumutantekeyela kulumbununa viuma vije Njambi alina kulinga ha vintsimbu vino tulimo?
LUK 12:57 “Vika muhonoua kuli yula yeni vavenia hakulinga viuma viacili?
LUK 12:58 Nga uya na citozi cove kunzango, eseka cikuma kulivuasana nendi mu ngila. Nga kuahi akakutuala kuli muka kuyula, kaha muka kuyula akakutuala kuli mukuluntu ua kamenga kaha akakutuala mu kamenga.
LUK 12:59 Njimileka yeni nguange kumukahumumo kuvanga noho mukafueta vimbongo viama maneselelo via mukuli.”
LUK 13:1 Ha ntsimbu ije kuakele vantu vamo valekele Yesu via Vangalileya vaje Pilato uatsihile te valinakulinga vinkombelo viavo kuli Njambi.
LUK 13:2 Yesu uavehuile nguendi, “Omuo Vangalileya vaje vavatsihile mu ngila ije vene, kaha yeni muayongola ngueni vapuile vaka vupi kupulakana Vangalileya voshe ndi?
LUK 13:3 Njimileka nguange, kuahi! Vuno honi nga kumutenguluka mukanonga ngue vakevo naua.
LUK 13:4 Singaniekeni vaje vantu likumi na vatanu na vatatu vaje vatsile omo kaposhi ka mu Siloame kavauililile. Musinganieka ngueni vapuile vaka vupi kupulakana voshe vaje vakele mu Yelusalema ndi?
LUK 13:5 Njimileka nguange, kuahi! Vuno honi kuvanga mutenguluke keti ngoconi mukanonga ngue vakevo naua.”
LUK 13:6 Kaha Yesu uavatele cisimo eci, “Kuakele yala umo uakunine muti ua mukuyu mu lihia liendi. Kaha uaile nakumonako vushuka vuno honi kavuuaneneko.
LUK 13:7 Kaha uahandekele kuli ndimi yendi nguendi, ‘Tala, mu miaka itatu njinakele nakuija nakutondako vushuka oku ku muti ua mukuyu, hanga nakamo kanjinauanako kahi. Uteke! Vikahoni utualelelaho kushamuisa livu eli?’
LUK 13:8 Vuno honi uje ndimi uamukumbuluile nguendi, ‘Muene, acitaleleleniko muaka umo naua, njikahindako kuuzengeleka nakuhakako vuilo.
LUK 13:9 Nga ukema vushuka mungolosika, kaha muacili, vuno honi nga kuukemi, ambahoni njikauteka.’ ”
LUK 13:10 Ha litangua limo lia Sapalalo Yesu uakele nakulongesa mu njivo ya malombelo.
LUK 13:11 Kaha kuakele mpuevo muje uakele na lihamba lije liamu vavalesele miaka likumi na itanu na itatu. Kaha ikeye uakotamene kasele kuhetuka kuahi.
LUK 13:12 Omo Yesu uamumuene, uamusanene nakuhandeka kuli ikeye nguendi, “Mpuevo, njikukangula ku kuvavala kuove.”
LUK 13:13 Kaha Yesu uakambekele mavoko endi hali ikeye, hajevene uolokele na kuputuka kushangazala Njambi.
LUK 13:14 Vuno honi mukuluntu ua mu njivo ya malombelo uanienguele omuo Yesu uakanguisile muntu ha litangua lia Sapalalo, uakele na kuhandeka ku vantu nguendi, “Kuli matangua atanu na limo aje tunapande kupanga vipangi. Ijeni mu matangua aje linga vamikanguise, keti ha litangua lia Sapalalo, kuahi.”
LUK 13:15 Vuno honi Muene Yesu uamukumbuluile nguendi, “Eni vaka civembulu! Nkuma yeni kumue kuzitula vangombe yeni cipue vimulu ceni nakumutuala ku mema ha litangua lia Sapalalo ndi?
LUK 13:16 Taleni ou Mpuevo! Ikeye mutekulu ua Avilahama uje yakutile Satana miaka likumi na itanu na itatu. Nkuma kuvapandele kumuzitula ha litangua lia Sapalalo ndi?”
LUK 13:17 Kukumbulula nguendi kuazivisile vitozi vendi voshe shuamua, kaha vantu voshe vajolelelele ha viuma viakukomokesa viacili vije vialingile.
LUK 13:18 Kaha Yesu uavehuile nguendi, “Vumuene vua Njambi vunapu ngue vika? Njivuesekesa na vika?
LUK 13:19 Vunapu ngue muje, muntu anona kanona kamo kambuto ya musalata nakukakuna mu lihia citungu. Kaha kakakola kapua muti uakama, kaha tuzila veja vakutungila mashua avo ku mintango yauo.”
LUK 13:20 Kaha naua Yesu uavehuile nguendi, “Vumuene vua Njambi njivuesekesa na vika?
LUK 13:21 Vunapu ngue cimbaluila cije mpuevo uanonele na kuutsingasana na vunga vua vuingi vua tiliku mu lilonga, noho mukasha uoshe uafutunukile.”
LUK 13:22 Yesu uahitile mu Vinganda na mu membo, ualongesele vantu oku hali mu vungenzi vuakuya ku Yelusalema.
LUK 13:23 Kaha umo uamuhuile nguendi, “Muene, nkuma vavandende lika vakovoka ndi?” Yesu uamukumbuluile nguendi,
LUK 13:24 “Licikinineni mukovele mu cikolo ca cindende, muavusunga omuo vavengi vakatonda ku kovelamo vuno honi kuvakasa.
LUK 13:25 Omo vavenia njivo akemana na kushoka lipito, kaha mukemana hambanza na kutota ha lipito ngueni, ‘Muene, tushokolueleko!’ Kaha akamikumbulula nguendi, ‘Kunjitantekeya oku kumuhuma.’
LUK 13:26 Kaha mukaputuka kuhandeka ngueni, ‘Tualile na kunua nove, kaha ualongesele mu nganda yetu.’
LUK 13:27 Vuno honi akahandeka naua nguendi, ‘Kunjitantekeya oku muhuma. Humeni kuli yange, yeni voshe vaka kulinga viavipi!’
LUK 13:28 Mukalila na kulishumanga ku mazo omo mukamona Avilahama, na Isake na Yakomba na tunanguizi va Njambi va Njambi voshe mu Vumuene vua Njambi, vuno honi yeni vakamiumbila hambanza.
LUK 13:29 Vantu vakahuma mu ngangela na mu kangombe ka yambi, ku kunto na mu mbuela, vakatumama ku ciuano mu Vumuene vua Njambi.
LUK 13:30 Cilivene vaka kukotokela vakapua vaka kulivanga, kaha vaka kulivanga vakapua vakevo vaka kukotokela.”
LUK 13:31 Ha ntsimbu ijevene kuezile Vafaliseo vamo kuli Yesu na ku handeka nguavo, “Unapande kuhuma kuno uye kueka, omuo Helonde atonda kukutsiha.”
LUK 13:32 Yesu uavakumbuluile nguendi, “Yeni mukamuleke ouo mbanje ngueni, ‘Njicili nakuhumisa mahamba na kukanguisa vantu kumavezi avo ku litangua lialelo na imene, kaha ha litangua lia mucitatu ambahoni njikamanesa vipangi viange.’
LUK 13:33 Cipue ngoco njinapandele kuenda lelo na imene na imenuavuze, omuo keti cacili kuli kananguizi ua Njambi kutsila kueka vuno honi kuvanga mu Yelusalema.
LUK 13:34 Yelusalema, Yelusalema, yove mu kakutsiha tunanguizi va Njambi va Njambi nakuasha mavue kuli vaje vavakutumina! Vintsimbu viavingi njatondele kukungulula vantu vove hamolika ngue cali muakavutikiya vana vendi mu mambava endi, vuno honi yove kuuanjitavele!
LUK 13:35 Tala, njivo yove ikasala ya mupulungua. Njikuleka nguange, kuukanjimono naua kuvanga noho ntsimbu ikeja omo ukahandeka nguove, ‘Uakuvezika ou eja mulizina lia Muene.’ ”
LUK 14:1 Ha ntsimbu imo omo Yesu uaile ku njivo ya mukuluntu ua Vafaliseo na kulia via kulia ha litangua lia Sapalalo, voshe vaje vakele mu njivo vakele na kumutalela muyehi.
LUK 14:2 Ha lutue luendi hakele yala uakele nakuvavala kuzimba mikono uezile kuli Yesu.
LUK 14:3 Yesu uehuisile Vafaliseo na valongisi va mezi a mashiko a Mosesa nguendi, “Cinapu cacili kuli Lishiko lietu ku kanguisa vantu ha litangua lia Sapalalo, indi kuahi?”
LUK 14:4 Vuno honi vaholokele. Kaha Yesu uamuambate uje yala uakuvavala na kumukanguisa, nakumuecela aye.
LUK 14:5 Kaha uahandekele kuli vakevo nguendi, “Nga hhakati keni hali umo hali na muana cipue ngombe uje nauila mulisima, kumuasa ku muhumisamo ha litangua lia Sapalalo ndi?”
LUK 14:6 Kaha vahonouele kumukumbulula eci.
LUK 14:7 Omo Yesu uamuene vangenzi vanahangula vihela via vituamo viakama, uavatelele cisimo nguendi,
LUK 14:8 “Omo nga vanakulaniako ku cilika cavulo, keti ukatumame ha cituamo ca kasingimiko, omuo hamo kuli umo ua kasingimiko kupulakana yove ivanalania.
LUK 14:9 Kaha uje uamilaniene muvavoshe a kahandeka kuli yove nguendi, ‘Njimilomba mutumameko kuje linga ou yala atumameko ha cihela ceni.’ Kaha mushuamua ukambata cituamo ca cindende kumaneselela.
LUK 14:10 Vuno honi nga vanakulania, ya ukatumame ha cituamo ca cindende ca kumaneselela, nga vavenia cilika akeja, akahandeka kuli yove nguendi, ‘Kavusamba, tumama ku cituamo ca kasingimiko,’ kaha uka tumama na kasingimiko kuli voshe ukatumama navo ku mesa.
LUK 14:11 Kaha voshe vaka lijundula vakevo vavenia va kavaneha ha mavu, kaha voshe vakalikehesa vakevo vavenia vakajundula.”
LUK 14:12 Kaha Yesu uahandekele kuli uje uamulaniene nguendi, “Nga uhana viakulia ha ciuano, keti lika ulanie vavusamba cipue va ndumbuevo cipue vavushoko vove cipue vakufuka vamua lihata navo, hamo vakamisana navakevo naua, kaha cikamuesa ngue vali nakumifueta.
LUK 14:13 Vuno honi nga uana viakulia ha ciuano, lania vihutu, na visualonda, na vilema na tupuputua.
LUK 14:14 Nga ulinga muje ukapua uakuvezika, omuo kuvakasa kukufueta, kaha vaka kufueta ha kusanguka ca vaka vusunga.”
LUK 14:15 Umo mungenzi ivalaniene kukulia omo uovuile eci, uahandekele kuli Yesu nguendi, “uakukuisula uje akatumama ku ciuano mu vumuene vua Njambi!”
LUK 14:16 Kaha Yesu uahandekele kuli ikeye nguendi, “Kuakele muntu umo uje ualingile ciuano cakama kaha ualaniene vantu vavengi.
LUK 14:17 Ha ntsimbu ya ciuano uatumine vangamba kuli vaje valaniene nguendi, ‘Ijeni, omuo vioshe vinavua honi.’
LUK 14:18 Kaha umo na umo uakele nakuhandeka nguendi nazenzama. Uakulivanga ua handekele nguendi, ‘Njinalanda lihia, kaha njitonda njikalimone, tambula kulomba kuange.’
LUK 14:19 Mukuavo uahandekele nguendi, ‘Njinalanda vangombe likumi, kaha njili nakuya na kuveseka, tambula kulomba kuange.’
LUK 14:20 Mukuavo naua uahandekele nguendi, ‘Njinambata mpuevo vene, kaha kunjasa kuija.’
LUK 14:21 Kaha uje ngamba uahilukile na kuambulula kuli Muene yendi. Kaha vavenia njivo uanienguele kaha uahandekele kuli ngamba yendi nguendi, ‘Ya hano vene muvingila na mu vitapalo via mbonge unehe vihutu, na visualonda, na tupuputua na vilema.’
LUK 14:22 Omo ngamba yendi uahilukile uahandekele nguendi, ‘Muene, viunashikile via lingiua, vuno honi kuhucili muhela.’
LUK 14:23 Kaha Muene uahandekele kuli ngamba yendi nguendi, ‘Ya mu vingila via mumikulo na mu vitapalo via mumikulo, usindiye vantu veje vakovele mu njivo yange linga ishule.
LUK 14:24 Kaha njikuleka nguange naumo uahi kuli vaje vanjinalaniene a kevua ku viakulia viange!’”
LUK 14:25 Litangua limo omo vantu vavengi vaile na Yesu, kaha ualulukile na kuhandeka kuli vakevo nguendi,
LUK 14:26 “Uoshe uje eja kuli yange vuno honi kazindi va ishe na vaina, mpuevo yendi na vana vendi, na vandumbuendi na vamuanaye va vampuevo, cilivene, cipue ukeuo muono uendi, kasa kupua ndongisi uange.
LUK 14:27 Uoshe uje kambata cilindakano cendi na kunjikava kasa kupua ndongisi uange.
LUK 14:28 Nga utonda kutunga njivo yakama, kaha utumama ha mavu na kumona vije vitondeka, kumona nga uasa kuimanusula.
LUK 14:29 Vuno honi nga uaputuka kuhinda luvula kaha uonoua kuimanesa, voshe vakaimona kaha vakakujola
LUK 14:30 na kuhandeka nguavo, ‘Uje mukuetu uaputukile kutunga vuno honi nahonoua.’
LUK 14:31 Cipue muene, nga aya ku nzita na kulua na mukuavo muene, kaha atumama ha mavu na kumona nga asa kulua na vantu va kupua makulukazi likumi na uje mukuavo eja na vantu vakupua makulukazi makumi avali.
LUK 14:32 Nga kasa, kaha omo mukuavo acili kulahako, akatumako vantu vakahandeke via ciyulo.
LUK 14:33 Mucifua cimo vene,” “naumo uahi hali yeni apua ndongisi uange nga kaseze vioshe vianafuku.
LUK 14:34 “Muongua uapua uacili, vuno honi nga uashamuka kaha kutovala caco cihiluka vati?
LUK 14:35 Kuukapu uacili ku mavu cipue ku vuilo, vaka umbila kuti. Uoshe hali na matuitui, napande kuivua evi!”
LUK 15:1 Litangua limo omo vaka kutambula lisimu na vaka vupi vezile na kuivuilila Yesu,
LUK 15:2 kaha Vafaliseo na valongisi va mezi a mashiko a Mosesa vakele nakuningozola na kuhandeka nguavo, “Ou yala linakutambula vaka vupi na kulia navo.”
LUK 15:3 Kaha Yesu uava telele cisimo eci nguendi,
LUK 15:4 “Iya hali yeni nga hali na Vampanga cihita kaha azimbalesaho umo, nkuma kaseze vaje makumi atanu na auana na vatanu na vauana (99) mu musenge na kuya nakutonda uje nazimbala kuvanga noho na muuana?
LUK 15:5 Nga namuuana, avuahelela na kumuhaka ha vitsili viendi,
LUK 15:6 omo ha kuya kuimbo, kaha akasana vavusamba vendi nava va lihata navo kaha akahandeka nguendi, ‘Vuaheleleni hamo nange omuo njinauana mpanga uange uje uazimbalele.’
LUK 15:7 Njimileka nguange, mucifua cimo vene kukapua kuvuahelela kuakama muilu hali muka vupi umo nga natenguluka kupulakana vaje makumi atanu na auana na vatanu na vauana vantu vaje kuvatondo kutenguluka.”
LUK 15:8 Yesu uatualeleleho kuleka vantu cisimo eci nguendi, “Nga mpuevo umo ali na vimbongo via mu uayauaya likumi, nga hazimbala imo, nkuma kashuameka ndeya yendi, nakukomba mu njivo na kutonda vuino kuvanga noho hakaiuanena?
LUK 15:9 Nga aiuana, kaha asana vavusamba vendi nava valihata navo na kuvaleka nguendi, ‘Vuaheleleni hamo nange omuo njinaiuana mbongo yange ije njazimbalesele.’
LUK 15:10 Njimileka nguange, mucifua cimo vene, muli kuvuahelela hakati katungelo va Njambi hali umo muka vupi uje atenguluka.”
LUK 15:11 Yesu uatualeleleleho kuhandeka nguendi, “Kuakele yala uakele navana va vamala vavali.
LUK 15:12 Ua kanike uahandekele kuli ishe nguendi, ‘Tate, njihaneko mutambela ua vufuko vuange,’ kaha ishavo uavapangelele vufuko vuendi hakati kavo vana vendi vavali.
LUK 15:13 Kukuahitile ntsimbu yailaha kuhuma haje, ua kanike ua mbate vioshe uakele navio na kuya ku lifuti lilahako na kupihisa viuma viendi vioshe kusenga.
LUK 15:14 Muamanusuile kupihisa viuma viendi vioshe, kaha kuakele njala mu lifuti lioshe, kaha uaputukile kutsa njala na vuhutu.
LUK 15:15 Kaha uaile na kutonda vipangi kuli muntu umo uamu lifuti lije kaha ua mutualele ku lihia naku lisa vangulu.
LUK 15:16 Uatondele kulia vije vakele na kulia vangulu, vuno honi naumo uahi uamuhaneneko cimo ca kulia.
LUK 15:17 Omo mana ahilukile muli ikeye, uahandekele kuli ikeye vavenia nguendi, ‘Vaka kupanga va vatate vali na viakulia viavingi, yange kuno njili nakutsa njala!
LUK 15:18 Njikuta vungenzi njihiluke kuli tate kaha njikahandeka kuli ikeye nguange, “Tate, njapihisila Njambi nove,
LUK 15:19 kunjapandele naua kunjisana munove, njipuise kupua umo uava Vaka kupanga vove.”’
LUK 15:20 Kaha uakatukile nakuya kuli ishe. “Omo uakele nakuendela kulako, ishe ua mumuene kaha ua muivuililile cikeketima kaha ishe uamushatukilile, uamuvumbatele na kumutsuemba.
LUK 15:21 Muana uahandekele kuli ikeye nguendi, ‘Tate njapihisila Njambi nove. Kunjapandele naua kunjisana munove.’
LUK 15:22 Vuno honi ishe uahandekele kuli vangamba vendi nguendi, ‘Zambuleni! Neheni cikovelo cacili mumuzike nakumuzika kanzeya ku munie uendi na vinkaku ku viliato yendi.
LUK 15:23 Neheni muna ngombe uakuhindala mumutsihe, kaha tulieni na kuvuahelela,
LUK 15:24 omuo munange ou uatsile vuno honi nahinduka naua, uazimbalele vuno honi nauaniua.’ Kaha vaputukile kulia na kuvuahelela.
LUK 15:25 “Ha ntsimbu ijevene, muana ua mukuluntu uakele mulihia. Omo uezile hayehi na njivo, uovuile miaso na vakakukina.
LUK 15:26 Kaha uasanene umo ua vangamba na kumuihula vika ‘vili nakulingika.’
LUK 15:27 Uamukumbuluile nguendi, ‘Ndumbuove neja kaha isho natsihi muana ngombe uakuhindala omuo nahiluka oku alimuacili.’
LUK 15:28 Muana ua mukuluntu ua nienguele na kuviana kukovela mu njivo. Kaha ishe uatuhukile na kumulambelela akovele mu njivo.
LUK 15:29 Vuno honi uakumbuluile ishe nguendi, ‘Tala! Ha miaka yoshe njinakupangela ngue ndungo kaha kunjashauile mashiko ove. Vuno honi kuuanjihaneko cipue muna mpembe linga njivuahelele na vavusamba vange.
LUK 15:30 Vuno honi omo ou munove nahiluka, uje na pihisa vufuko vuove na vukoyi kaha neja kuimbo, kaha una mutsihila muana ngombe uakuhindala!’
LUK 15:31 Ishe uahandekele kuli ikeye nguendi, ‘Munange, ntsimbu yoshe unakele nange, kaha vioshe njilinavio vinapu viove.
LUK 15:32 Vuno honi tuapande kuvuahelela na kujolela, omuo shongoyove ou uatsile kaha nayoyo naua, uazimbalele vuno honi nauaniua.’ ”
LUK 16:1 Kaha Yesu uahandekele kuli vandongisi vendi nguendi, “Kuakele yala umo ua kufuka uje uakele na muka kutulika vufuko vuendi. Muka kufuka uje vamulekele nguavo muka kutulika vitenga viove hali nakupihisa vimbongo viove.
LUK 16:2 Kaha uamusanene na kuhandeka nguendi, ‘Vika evi njili nakuivua hali yove? Njihane vukaleho vua viuma vioshe muje munatulikilamo vufuko vuange, omuo kukapu naua muka kutulika uange.’
LUK 16:3 Muka kutulika ualihandekesele ikeye vavenia nguendi, ‘Nga muene uange anjihumisa vipangi, njilinga vatihoni? Kunjesi na nzili yakuhinda vina, nganjihuma vipangi kuno, kaha naua njili na shuamua yakulomba.
LUK 16:4 Kaha honi njatantekeya vinjikalinga linga vantu vakanjitambule mu vinjivo viavo! Omo vipangi viange vikahua.’
LUK 16:5 Kaha uasanene vantu vaje vakele na mikuli kuli muene uendi. Uehuile uakulivanga nguendi, ‘Vungahi uakonguele kuli muene uange?’
LUK 16:6 Kaha uamukumbuluile nguendi, ‘Vihita vitanu na vitatu via mingomo ya mazi a olive.’ Kaha uje muka kutulika uahandekele naua nguendi, ‘Livulu liove eli lije limuesa makongo ove, tumama ha mavu sonekamo viseteko via vihita viuana via mingomo.’
LUK 16:7 Kaha uehuile mukuavo ua mucivali nguendi, ‘Uakonguele cingahi?’ Kaha uamukumbuluile nguendi, ‘Cihita cimolika ca masaka a tiliku,’ kaha uamulekele nguendi, ‘Ambata livulu liove eli sonekamo makumi atanu na atatu a masaka a tiliku.’
LUK 16:8 Kaha uje muene uendi uashangazalele uje muka kutulika uakuhona kulongua hakukala na mana, omuo vantu va lifuti lino vatantekeya muakukela navakuavo kupulakana vana vamu ceke.”
LUK 16:9 Njimileka nguange, pangeseni vufuko vua ha mavu kulinga vusamba kuli yeni na tuhutu. Kaha omo vufuko vueni vukahua, omo mukatsa vaka mitambula mu vihela via kuhona kuhua.
LUK 16:10 Uoshe akala na vusunga muvia vindende na mu viakama akakala na vusunga, kaha uje kakala na vusunga muvia vindende kaha kakakala na vusunga mu viakama.
LUK 16:11 Kaha nga kuuakele na vusunga na vufuko vua ha mavu, iya honi akutsiliela na vufuko vua vusunga?
LUK 16:12 Kaha nga kuuakele na vusunga ha vitenga via muntu, iya akakuhana vufuko vuje vuakupande?
LUK 16:13 “Uahi ngamba asa kupangela vamiene vavali omuo uje ngamba akazindaho umo naku zangaho mukuavo, cipue halihanako kuli umo na kushaula mukuavo. Kuuasa kupangela Njambi na vimbongo.”
LUK 16:14 Vafaliseo vaje vapuile vaka kuzanga vimbongo, omo vovuile vioshe evi, kaha vashendumuine Yesu.
LUK 16:15 Kaha uahandekele kuli vakevo nguendi, “Yeni vaje vaka limuesa kupua vaka vusunga ku vantu, vuno honi Njambi atantekeya mitima yeni, omuo coshe cije vashangazala hakati ka vantu, ku mesho a Njambi cinapu ca ngoco ngoco.
LUK 16:16 “Lishiko lia Mosesa na tunanguizi va Njambi va Njambi vatuamenene vantu noho Iuano muka kumbuitika uezile. Kuhuma oho naha ntsimbu ino muzimbu uacili ua vumuene vua Njambi vauambulula. Muntu uoshe alinakueseka cikuma kukovela omu mu vumuene.
LUK 16:17 Vuno honi cacasi melu na mavu kuhita kupulakana ka lizi kakande kamu mukanda ua Lishiko lia Mosesa kuhua.
LUK 16:18 “Uoshe akondola mpuevo yendi na kuambata ueka nalingi vupangala, kaha uoshe ambata mpuevo uakukondola kuli yala liendi alinga vupangala.
LUK 16:19 “Kuakele yala umo uakufuka uje uakele nakuya vuzalo vua vunengu vuandando yakutula, uakele na ciuano ca kulia cakama halitangua na tangua.
LUK 16:20 Kuakele yala uacihutu lizina liendi Lazalu uje ivakele nakuneha ku cikolo ca muka kufuka, uje uakele na vimbandu muvila uoshe.
LUK 16:21 Lazalu uakele nakuvandamena kulia viakele na kuua ku mesa ya uje yala uakufuka, na tutali vakele nakuija na kuliasa ha vimbandu viendi.
LUK 16:22 Uje yala uacihutu uatsile kaha tungelo vamuambate kukakala na Avilahama. Kaha na uje yala uakufuka naikeye uatsile kaha vamutsindile.
LUK 16:23 Uakele mu ngehena na kuyanda. Uatalele kuilu kaha uamuene Avilahama kulahako hali na Lazalu ku mukulo uendi.
LUK 16:24 Kaha uasanene nguendi, ‘Tate Avilahama, njizivileko cikeketima tuma Lazalu ambuitike munie uendi mu mema anjitontuese ha ndaka yange, omuo njili na kuvua kuvavala muno mu tuhia.’
LUK 16:25 Vuno honi Avilahama uamukumbuluile nguendi, ‘Munange, anuka ha ntsimbu yove uakele nakuyoya uakele nakutambula viuma viove via cili, na ntsimbu ya Lazalu uatambuile via vipi, vuno honi hali nakuyoya muacili yove uli na kuyanda.
LUK 16:26 Kaha naua mukati kove netu hali cina cakama, ngeci uoshe atonda kujavuka kuhuma kuli yetu kuija oko keti ase, kaha naumo uahi asa kujavuka kuhuma oko kuija kuno kutuli.’
LUK 16:27 Kaha yala ua kufuka uahandekele nguendi, ‘Honi, tate, njilomba yove utume Lazalu ku njivo ya tate,
LUK 16:28 omuo njili na vandumbuange vatanu. Ecela Lazalu aye nakuvanangula linga keti vakeje naua kuno kucihela ca tuyando.’
LUK 16:29 Kaha Avilahama uakumbuluile nguendi, ‘Vali na visoneka via Mosesa na tunanguizi va Njambi va Njambi, vanapande kuvovuilila.’
LUK 16:30 Uje yala ua kufuka uahandekele nguendi, ‘houe, tate Avilahama, vuno honi nga umo akasanguka kuvatsi aya kuli vakevo kaha vakatenguluka.’
LUK 16:31 Avilahama uamukumbuluile nguendi, ‘Nga kuvevuilila ku visoneka via Mosesa na tunanguizi va Njambi va Njambi, kaha cipue muntu uakuhuma ku vatsi ku vakatava.’ ”
LUK 17:1 Yesu uahandekele kuli vandongisi vendi nguendi, “Viaseko via vupi mua vusunga vihita, vuno honi tuyando kuli uje avineha!
LUK 17:2 Cacili kuli ikeye nga vaka mukutilila livue liakama muntsingo na kumumbila mu cisali, kuhona akovelese umo ua vanike vavandende mu vupi.
LUK 17:3 Zangameni ku vije muli nakulinga. Nga mukueni alinga vupi munangule nga halitavela mukonekele.
LUK 17:4 Kaha nga muntu umo vene akupihisila lutanu na luvali ha litangua limo, kaha eja kuli yove lutanu na luvali na kuhandeka nguendi, ‘njatenguluka,’ unapande kumukonekela.”
LUK 17:5 Kaha tunganda vahandekele kuli Muene Yesu nguavo, “Vuezelela lutsilielo luetu!”
LUK 17:6 Kaha Muene Yesu uahandekele nguendi, “Nga muli nalutsilielo lualundende ngue mbuto ya musalata, nge muasa kuhandeka ku muti ou uakama ua mizi yaingi ngueni, ‘Tukuka uka shimbame ha mema a kalunga!’ Kaha ukeuo ukamiononoka.
LUK 17:7 “Nga ulina ngamba muka kulima cipue muka kuniunga vampanga uasa kuhandeka kuli ikeye nga ahuminina ku mehia nguove, ‘Ija hano vene uakutumame na kulia’?
LUK 17:8 Houe! Ukahandeka kuli ikeye nguove, ‘Vuahesa viakulia viange via cinguezi, Naua lizitikile vualumo muiva uove nakunjipangela noho njikalia na kunua, nga njamanesa ambahoni ulie na kunua!’
LUK 17:9 Honi ngamba kuveku mutsatsela hakulinga vije vivamushikile kulinga ndi? Mua vusunga kuahi!
LUK 17:10 Neni naua vene, omo mualingile vioshe vije vivamishikile kulinga, handekeni ngueni, ‘Tuva ngamba vangoco, tunalingi lika vipangi vietu.’”
LUK 17:11 Yesu hakuya ku Yelusalema uahitile mukati ka Samhaliya na Ngalileya.
LUK 17:12 Kaha uakovelele muimbo muje vamala vambumba likumi vamuuanene, vemanene kulahako.
LUK 17:13 Vatambakanene cikuma na kuhandeka nguavo, “Yesu, Muene tuvuileko cikeketima!”
LUK 17:14 Omo Yesu uavamuene, uahandekele kuli vakevo nguendi, “Yeni mukalimuese yeni vavenia kuli tusasendote.” Omo vakele nakuya vavalelesele.
LUK 17:15 Kaha umo uavo omo uamuene nguendi nakanguka, uahilukile na kushangazala Njambi na lizi liakama,
LUK 17:16 Uauile na cihanga cendi ku viliato ya Yesu na kumutsatsela. Ikeye uapuile Kasamaliya.
LUK 17:17 Kaha Yesu uahandekele nguendi, “Kuvapuile likumi vanakanguka? Ava vatanu na vauana vali kulihoni?
LUK 17:18 Vikahoni cipue umo kuija nakuhana cisantsela kuli Njambi kuvanga lika ou keti kayunda?”
LUK 17:19 Kaha Yesu uahandekele kuli ikeye nguendi, “Katuka uye, lutsilielo liove lua kukanguisa.”
LUK 17:20 Kaha Yesu vamuihuile kuli Vafaliseo nguavo, “Ntsimbu muka vumuene vua Njambi vukeja?” Kaha uavatavele nguendi, “Vumuene vua Njambi kuvukeja mungila ije muasa kuvumona na mesho eni kuahi.
LUK 17:21 Kukuesi akahandeka nguendi, ‘Tala, vuno vulikuno!’ Cipue ‘Taleni, vuje vuli kuje!’ Omuo vumuene vua Njambi muli navuo hakati keni.”
LUK 17:22 Kaha honi Yesu uahandekele kuli vandongisi vendi nguendi, “Matangua akeja omo mukatonda kumona litangua limo lia Muna Muntu, vuno honi kumukasa kuli mona.
LUK 17:23 Kaha kukakala vamo vakahandeka kuli yeni nguavo, ‘Taleni ali kuje!’ Cipue, ‘Taleni ali kuno!’ Keti muyeko, keti muvakavangeye.
LUK 17:24 Ngue muhiato mukahiatula muilu, kaha vaumona uhuma kumuhela umo ua lilu nakuya ku muhela ukuavo ua lilu, mukemovene naua Muna Muntu muakafua ha litangua liendi liakuhiluka.
LUK 17:25 Vuno honi napande kuyanda cikuma na kumuyengula kuli vantu va ntsimbu ino.
LUK 17:26 Nge mucapuile ku matangua a Noua mukemovene mucikapuilamo naku matangua a Muna Muntu.
LUK 17:27 Vantu vakele nakulia na kunua, na kuliambata na kushombuesa, noho Noua uakovelele mu vuato. Kaha livazi liezile nakuvanongesa voshe.
LUK 17:28 Nge mucapuile ku matangua a Lote: vantu voshe vanuine, valile, valandesele na kulandulula, vakunine na kutunga,
LUK 17:29 vuno honi ha litangua lije Lote uahumine mu Sondoma, tuhia na mavue vianokele ngue mema a kuhuma muilu, kaha via vanongesele voshe.
LUK 17:30 Cikapua ngue mujevene ha litangua liakasholoka Muna Muntu.
LUK 17:31 “Ha litangua lijevene, uoshe uje yala hali helu lia njivo keti akovele mu njivo na kuambata viuma viendi, naua na uje hali mu lihia liendi keti ahiluke ku njivo yendi.
LUK 17:32 Singaniekeni hali mpuevo ya Lote.
LUK 17:33 Voshe vaje vatonda kuniunga muono uavo vavenia vaka uzimbalesa, vuno honi vaje vazimbalesa muono uavo vakau uana.
LUK 17:34 Njimileka, ha vutsiki vuje kukakala vantu vavali ha muhela umo, umo vakamuambata ou mukuavo vakamuseza.
LUK 17:35 Kaha kukakala vampuevo vavali vali mukutua hamo mucini cimo, mukuavo vaka muambata na mukuavo vakamuseza.”
LUK 17:36 [Vamala vavali vakapanga mu lihia, umo vakaya nendi mukuavo vakamuseza.]
LUK 17:37 Kaha vandongisi vendi vamuihuile nguavo, “Kulihoni kuvikalingika, Muene?” Kaha Yesu uavatavele nguendi, “Kuoshe kuje kuli civimbi kukeko kukalikunguluila makuvi.”
LUK 18:1 Yesu ualekele vandongisi vendi cisimo eci kuvalongesa nguendi, vapande kulombela ntsimbu yoshe cakuhona kuecela.
LUK 18:2 Uahandekele nguendi, “Mu mbonge imo muakele muka kuyula uje kateuele Njambi cipue kusingimika vantu.
LUK 18:3 Kaha naua mu mbonge ijevene muakele ntuluue uje uakele nakuija kuli ikeye vintsimbu viavingi na kuhandeka nguendi, ‘njihaneko kapandi kange ha vitozi vange!’
LUK 18:4 Ha ntsimbu yaindende uje muka kuyula uavianene, hajevene uahandekele kuli ikeye vavenia nguendi, ‘Cipue kunjiteue Njambi cipue kusingimika vantu,
LUK 18:5 vuno honi ou ntuluue nanjishupu cikuma, njapande kumuhana kapandi kendi, omuo nga atualelelaho kuija kaha aka njihonesa!’”
LUK 18:6 Kaha Muene Yesu uahandekele nguendi, “Ivuilileni vije viahandeka uje muka kuyula uakuhona vusunga!
LUK 18:7 Nkuma Njambi kasa kuyula mu vusunga ku vantu vendi vaje valinakulilila kuli ikeye vutsiki na mutania? Nkuma ngueni akasimbula mukuvakuasa ndi?
LUK 18:8 Njimileka nguange, hajevene akavahana kapandi kavo. Vuno honi omo Muna Muntu akeja, akauanaho vantu vali nalutsilielo hano ha mavu ndi?”
LUK 18:9 Yesu uate cisimo eci naua kuli vantu vaje vaka kutsiliela vusunga vuavo vavenia nakushaula vakuavo,
LUK 18:10 Uahandekele nguendi, “Vamala vavali vayile ku njivo ya Njambi nakulomba, umo Kafaliseo, mukuavo muka kutambula lisimu.
LUK 18:11 Kafaliseo uemanene na kulomba nguendi, ‘Njikutsantsela Njambi, yange kunjafuile ngue vakuetu vantsintsa, vaka kuhona vusunga, vaka vupangala. Yange kunjafuile ngue uje muka kutambula lisimu nemana kuje.
LUK 18:12 Njikaliumina kulia ha matangua avali mu simano, njikahana cimo kulikumi ca vioshe vinjikauana.’
LUK 18:13 Vuno honi uje muka kutambula lisimu uemanene ku lahako, kaha kasele cipue kutala kuilu, vuno honi ualivete ha ntulo na kuhandeka nguendi, ‘Njambi, civuile cikeketima yange muka vupi.’
LUK 18:14 Njimileka,” nguange, “uje muka kutambula lisimu uaile kuimbo liendi mu vusunga kupulakana uje Kafaliseo, voshe vaje valijundula vakevo vavenia vaka vakehesa, vuno honi voshe vaje valikehesa vakevo vavenia vakava jundula.”
LUK 18:15 Vantu vanehelelele Yesu vanike vavandende linga avasaleke mavoko, kaha omo vandongisi vendi vacimuene, vesekele kuvindika vaje vantu.
LUK 18:16 Vuno honi Yesu uasanene vanike vavandende veje kuli ikeye, uahandekele nguendi, “Eceleni vanike vavandende veje kuli yange keti muvavindike, omuo vumuene vua Njambi vuli ku vantu ngue ava vanike vavandende.
LUK 18:17 Mua vusunga njimileka nguange, uoshe uje katambula vumuene vua Njambi ngue kanike uamundende, kakakovela mu vumuene vua Njambi.”
LUK 18:18 Litangua limo umo mukuluntu ua Vayunda uehuile Yesu nguendi, “Mulongisi uacili, vika njinapande kulinga linga njikauane muono uakuhona kuua?”
LUK 18:19 Yesu uamukumbuluile nguendi, “Vika unjitumbuila nguove uacili?” Naumo uahi “uacili kuvanga Njamba lika.
LUK 18:20 Uatantekeya mashiko a Njambi nguauo, ‘Keti ulinge vupangala, keti utsihe, keti uive, keti uvangeye mukueni vukaleho vua makuli, singimika isho na noko.’ ”
LUK 18:21 Kaha uje yala uakumbuluile Yesu nguendi, “Mashiko oshe aua njaononoka laja hume kuvuanike vuange.”
LUK 18:22 Kaha omo Yesu uevuile evi, uahandekele kuli ikeye nguendi, “Kunasupila cuma cimo ciunapande ku linga. Ya ukalandese vioshe viulinavio kaha ukahane vimbongo vioshe kuli tuhutu, kaha ukakala na vufuko muilu, kaha uije, uakunjikave.”
LUK 18:23 Vuno honi uje yala omo uevuile evi, kaha uanienguele, omuo ikeye uakele navufuko vua vuingi.
LUK 18:24 Omo Yesu uamuene nguendi naniengua, kaha uahandekele nguendi, “cinapu cacikalu kuli vaka kufuka kukovela mu vumuene vua Njambi!
LUK 18:25 Cacikalu kuli kamelu kukovela mu lisho lia nguya vuno honi cacikalu cikuma kuma muntu muka kufuka kukovela mu vumuene vua Njambi.”
LUK 18:26 Kaha vaje vantu vovuile, vamuihuile nguavo, “Iya honi akovoka?”
LUK 18:27 Kaha Yesu uavakumbuluile nguendi, “Kuli viuma vije vantu kuvasa kulinga vuno honi Njambi asa kulinga coshe.”
LUK 18:28 Kaha Petulu uahandekele nguendi, “Tala! Yetu tunaseza vioshe vituli navio, nakukukava.”
LUK 18:29 Kaha Yesu uahandekele kuli vakevo nguendi, “Eyo, mua vusunga njimileka uoshe uje naseza njivo yendi, cipue mpuevo yendi, cipue munaina, cipue visemi vendi, cipue vana vendi, omuo vumuene vua Njambi,
LUK 18:30 akatambula viavingi cikuma mu muono ou na muono ua yaye mu miaka ije ikeja kulutue.”
LUK 18:31 Yesu uatualele vandongisi vendi likumi na vavali kuavo lika, kaha uahandekele kuli vakevo nguendi, “Evuilileni! Tulinakuya mu Yelusalema kuje viuma vioshe vije vivasonekele kuli tunanguizi va Njambi va Njambi hali Muna Muntu linga vika lishulisise.
LUK 18:32 Muna Muntu vakamuhana ku mavoko a Maloma vaje vaka mushendumuna na kumutuka na kumujekuila malenzi.
LUK 18:33 Vaka muveta, kaha vaka mutsiha, vuno honi munima ya matangua atatu akasanguka.”
LUK 18:34 Vuno honi vandongisi vendi kuvovuisisile nacimo cahi ha viuma evi, omuo kulumbunuka kua mezi aua vavashuekeleleuo linga keti vatantekeye vije via handekele Yesu kuli vakevo.
LUK 18:35 Omo Yesu uahete kuyehi na Yeliko, kuakele yala umo ua kapuputua uakele kumukulo ua ngila nakulomba.
LUK 18:36 Kaha omo uevuile civunga ca vantu cili nakuita, kaha uehuile nguendi “Vika vili nakulingika?”
LUK 18:37 Kaha vamulekele nguavo, “Yesu uaku Nazaleta hali nakuhita.”
LUK 18:38 Kaha uatambakanene nguendi, “Yesu! Muna Ndaviti! Njivuileko cikeketima!”
LUK 18:39 Kaha vantu vaje vakele kulutue lia civunga, vamulekele linga aholoke. Vuno honi ikeye uatambakanene cikuma nguendi, “Ove Muna Ndaviti! Njivuileko cikeketima!”
LUK 18:40 Yesu uemanene nakushika nguendi, “Muneheni kuno”. Omo uje yala uashuenene kuyehi, Yesu uamuhulisile nguendi,
LUK 18:41 “Vika utonda linga njikulingile?” Kaha uamukumbuluile nguendi, “Muene njitonda linga njimone naua.”
LUK 18:42 Kaha Yesu uahandekele kuli ikeye nguendi, “Mona! Lutsilielo luove luna kukanguisa.”
LUK 18:43 Kaha hajevene uaputukile kumona, uakavele Yesu, na kushangazala Njambi. Omo vantu vacimuene, kaha voshe vashangazalale Njambi.
LUK 19:1 Hanima yevi Yesu kukovela mu Yeliko na kuputuka kuhitanganamo.
LUK 19:2 Muakele yala umo mu mbonge ije, uje uapuile mukuluntu ua vaka kutambula lisimo lizina liendi Sangeo, uje uapuile muka kufuka.
LUK 19:3 Uatondele kumona Yesu, vuno honi kasele kumumona omuo uapuile uamuihi, kaha naua kuakele civunga cakama.
LUK 19:4 Kaha uashatukilile kulutue lia civunga, ualondele ku muti ua linongo linga amone Yesu uje uahitilile mu ngila ijevene.
LUK 19:5 Omo Yesu uahete ha mutambela uje, uatalele kuilu, kaha uahandekele kuli Sangeo nguendi, “shuluka vuasi Sangeo, omuo lelo njapande kuija ku njivo yove.”
LUK 19:6 Sangeo uashulukile vuasi na kumutambula na kuvuahelela cikuma.
LUK 19:7 Vantu voshe vaje vamuene vialingiuile vaninguile nguavo, “Ou Yala nai kupua mungezi ku njivo ya muka vupi!”
LUK 19:8 Kaha Sangeo uemanene na kuhandeka kuli Muene Yesu nguendi, “Muene ivuilila njihana mutambela ua vufuko vuange kuli tuhutu, nga njambate cimo kuli umo mu ngila ya makuli, kaha njika mufueta vintsimbu viuana.”
LUK 19:9 Yesu uahandekele nguendi, “Kuovoka ku neja mu njivo muno lelo, omuo yala ou nalimuesa kupua muana ua vusunga ua Avilahama.
LUK 19:10 Mua vusunga Muna Muntu uezile nakutonda na kuovola vaje vana zimbala.”
LUK 19:11 Tele vantu vakele nakuivuilila vije Yesu uakele nakuhandeka, uavatele cisimo omuo uakele kuyehi na Yelusalema, kaha vasinganiekele nge vumuene vua Njambi hajevene vuavuno vusholoka.
LUK 19:12 Kaha Yesu uahandekele nguendi, “Kuakele muntu uaku vumuene uje uaile ku lifuti lia kulahako linga vakamupuise muene, hanima yevi uasinganiekele kuhiluka linga akuendese vantu vendi.
LUK 19:13 Tele kanda aye, uasanene vangamba vendi likumi kaha uahanene umo na umo mbongo ya ngolinde na kuvaleka nguendi, ‘Landululeni noho njikeja.’
LUK 19:14 Vuno honi vantu vamu lifuti liendi vamuzindile cikuma, kaha vatumine tunganda vamukave munima yendi na kukahandeka nguavo, ‘Ou yala kutumutondo linga apue Muene yetu kuahi.’
LUK 19:15 “Omo uje yala uahilukile, hanima ya kumuhaka kupua muene, uashikile vaje vangamba vahanene vimbongo linga veje kuli ikeye linga atantekeya cingahi vana landuluilaho.
LUK 19:16 Kaha uakulivanga uezile nakuhandeka nguendi, ‘Muene, mbongo imolika ije iuanjihanene yasemuininahoni vimbongo likumi vikuavo.’
LUK 19:17 Kaha uahandekele kuli ikeye nguendi, ‘Unalingi muacili cikuma, ngamba uacili! Kaha muene uahandekele kuli ikeye nguendi, omuo unakala nalutsilielo mu viuma viavindende, njikakuhana nzili yakama ya kutuamenena vimbonge likumi.’
LUK 19:18 Kaha uamucivali naua uezile uahandekele nguendi, ‘Muene, mbongo yove imolika ije iuanjihanene yasemuinina vimbongo vitanu.’
LUK 19:19 Kaha naua muene uahandekele kuli ikeye nguendi, ‘Njikakupuisa muka kutuamenena vimbonge vitanu.’
LUK 19:20 Kaha mukuavo ngamba uezile uahandekele nguendi, ‘Muene, mbongo yove eyi, hanga njaitulikilile akantanga kakandende.
LUK 19:21 Njakutinine, omuo yove uapua muntu uavutenu. Ukambata cije keti cove na kuteja vije kuuakuvile.’
LUK 19:22 Kaha muene uahandekele kuli ikeye nguendi, ‘Yove ngamba uamupi! Njikakuhisa na mezi akuhuma mu kanua kove! Utantekeye nguove yange nji yala uavutenu, njikambata vije keti viange na kuteja vije kunjakuvile?
LUK 19:23 Vikahoni kuua yakele kuli vaka kusekasana mbongo yange? Omo yange njineja nge njinauana mbongo yange hamo na kakondueso kayo.’
LUK 19:24 Kaha muene uahandekele kuli vaje vemanene kumukulo nguendi, ‘Muniekeni oyo mbongo, muihane kuli uje hali na vimbongo likumi.’
LUK 19:25 Vuno honi vakevo vahandekele kuli ikeye nguavo, ‘Muene, hali laja na vimbongo likumi!’
LUK 19:26 Kaha ikeye uavatavele nguendi, ‘Muavusunga njimileka nguange, uje hali naco, vakamuhakelako viavingi, vuno honi uje kesi navio, cipue vene vije viavindende viali navio vakamuniekavio.
LUK 19:27 Kaha honi ku vitozi vange, vaje kuvatondele linga yange njipue muene uavo, vaneheni kuno nakuvatsihila ha mesho ange.’ ”
LUK 19:28 Omo Yesu uamanesele kuhandeka evi, kaha uaile kulutue luavo nakuya ku Yelusalema.
LUK 19:29 Omo Yesu uahete kuyehi na Mbetefenje na Mbeteniya ku munkinda ua Oliveta, kaha uatumine vandongisi vavali kulutue,
LUK 19:30 Uavalekele nguendi, “Yeni ku limbo lije lili kulutue lueni, omo mukakovelamo mukauana muna cimulu vanamukutu, uje kanda muntu alondeho. Kaha muzituleni mumunehe kuno.”
LUK 19:31 Nga muntu umo amihula nguendi vika mumuzituila, mulekeni ngueni Muene amutonda.
LUK 19:32 Kaha vaje vatumine vaile vakauanene muje muahandekelele Muene.
LUK 19:33 Tele vali nakuzitula uje muna cimulu, kaha vavenia cimulu uavehuile nguendi, “Vika mumuzituila ou muna cimulu?”
LUK 19:34 Kaha vamutavele nguavo, “Muene hali nakumutonda.”
LUK 19:35 Kaha vatualele uje muna cimulu kuli Yesu. Kaha vajalele tuzaku tuavo ha muongo ua cimulu, kaha valondeseleho Yesu.
LUK 19:36 Omo uakele nakuya ha cimulu, vantu vajalele tuzaku tuavo mu ngila kulutue lua Yesu.
LUK 19:37 Omo Yesu uahete kuyehi na Yelusalema, kucikulo ca munkinda ua Oliveta, kaha civunga cacingi ca vandongisi vendi vaputukile kuvuahelela na kulemesa Njambi na mezi akama ha vikomoueso vioshe viakama vivamuene vije Yesu ualingile,
LUK 19:38 nguavo “Uakukuisula muene uje akeja mu lizina lia Muene Njambi! Ciyulo cikale muilu na vumpau kuli Njambi!”
LUK 19:39 Kaha Vafaliseo vamo vaje vakele mu civunga vahandekele kuli Yesu nguavo, “Mulongisi, shika vandongisi vove vaholoke”
LUK 19:40 Yesu uavatavele nguendi, “Njimileka nguange, nga ava valikela kulemesa kaha aua mavue akaputuka kutambakana.”
LUK 19:41 Omo Yesu uahete kuyehi na kumona Yelusalema, uailililile,
LUK 19:42 uahandekele nguendi, “Nga uatantekeyele lika lelo nguove vika vitondeka linga kukale ciyulo! Vuno honi vuavuno vacishuekesa ku mesho ove!
LUK 19:43 Ntsimbu ikeja hali yove, omo vitozi vove vaka kutungila cimpaka, nakukuhaka mukati kavo, na kukushetuilamo mukati ku mitambela yoshe.
LUK 19:44 Kaha vakevo vakakunongesa hamo na vantu vove vaje vali mu vivumbe viove, kuvakaseze livue limo mu muhela ualio, omuo yove kuuatantekeyele ntsimbu omo Njambi uezile nakukuovola.”
LUK 19:45 Yesu uakovelele mu njivo ya Njambi, na kuputuka kushekamo voshe vaje vakele na kulandesa,
LUK 19:46 uahandekele kuli vakevo nguendi, “Vanasoneka mu visoneka nguavio, ‘Njivo yange ikapua njivo ya Malombelo’, vuno honi yeni muaipuisa muhela ua vizi!”
LUK 19:47 Yesu uakele nakulongesa mu njivo ya Njambi ha litangua na litangua. Vakuluntu va tusasendote na valongisi va mezi a Lishiko lia Mosesa na vantuama va vantu vatondele kumutsiha,
LUK 19:48 vuno honi kuvauanene ngila yaku cilingila, omuo vantu voshe vakele naku muvuilila linga keti vasezeho cipue lizi limo.
LUK 20:1 Litangua limo Yesu uakele nakulongesa mu njivo ya Njambi na kuambulula muzimbu uacili ku vantu, kaha vakuluntu va tusasendote na valongisi va mezi a Lishiko lia Mosesa, hamo na vakuluntu vezile.
LUK 20:2 Kaha vahandekele kuli ikeye nguavo, “Tuleke, nzili muka ukalikuasesa nayo kulinga viuma evi? Iya nakuhana nzili eyi?”
LUK 20:3 Yesu uavakumbuluile nguendi, “Nange naua njimihula cihula cimo. Njilekeni,
LUK 20:4 nzili ya likuasesele Iuano muka kumbuitika ya humine kuli Njambi indi kuli vantu?”
LUK 20:5 Vaputukile vimpata hhakati kavo nguavo, “Vika tuhandeka? Nga tuhandeka nguetu, ‘ya humine kuli Njambi,’ kaha akatuihula nguendi, ‘Vikahoni kumua mukulahelele Iuano?’
LUK 20:6 Vuno honi nga tuhandeka nguetu, ‘Ihuminina ku vantu,’ Kaha civunga coshe ca vantu vakatutsiha mukutuasha mavue, omuo vovuisisile nguavo Iuano uapuile Kananguizi ua Njambi.”
LUK 20:7 Kaha vakumbuluile Yesu nguavo, “Kututantekeya kuje kuya humine.”
LUK 20:8 Kaha Yesu uahandekele nguendi, “Nange naua kunjimileke kuihuminina nzili injili nakulikuasesa kulinga viuma evi.”
LUK 20:9 Kaha Yesu uaputukile kuleka vantu cisimo eci nguendi, “Kuakele yala umo uakele na citungu ca mikolovozi ya vushuka vua viniu, kaha uacikumuisile kuli vandimi vamo, kaha uaile vungezi vuendi ha ntsimbu yalaha.
LUK 20:10 Omo ntsimbu ya kuteja vushuka yahete, uatumine ngamba uendi kuli vaje vandimi, muku katambulako mutambela uendi kuli vije vanateje. Vuno honi vaje vandimi vapupile uje ngamba, na kumuhiluisa mavoko voko.
LUK 20:11 Kaha uje vavenia citungu uatumineko naua ngamba mukuavo, vuno honi vaje vandimi vamupupile na kumulinga mua mupi, kaha uamuhiluisile mavoko voko.
LUK 20:12 Uatumineko naua ngamba uamu citatu, kaha vaje vandimi vamu vulumuine naua nakumumbila hambaza lia citungu.
LUK 20:13 Kaha honi vavenia citungu uahandekele nguendi, ‘Njilinga vati? Njikatuma munange injazanga, hamo vaka musingimika!’
LUK 20:14 Vuno honi omo vandimi vamumuene, kaha valihandekesele hhakati kavo nguavo, ‘Ou ikeye muna uje vavenia citungu. Ijeni tumutsihe, kaha tukafungulula vufuko vuendi!’
LUK 20:15 Nkuma, vamumbilile hambaza lia citungu, kaha vamutsihile.” Yesu uavehuile nguendi, “Vika akalinga uje vavenia citungu kuli vaje vandimi?
LUK 20:16 Akeja na kutsiha vaje vantu na kuhana cije citungu kuli vandimi veka.” Kaha omo vantu vavuile evi, vahandekele nguavo, “Mua vusunga vene keti ngoco kuahi!”
LUK 20:17 Yesu uavatalele nakuvehula nguendi, “Visoneka vilumbunuka vika omo vihandeka nguavio, ‘Livue lije livavianene vaka kutunga ngue kuliesi na seho likelio vuavuno linapu liaseho kupulaka mavue oshe’?
LUK 20:18 Kaha uoshe uje akauila ha livue lije akapokoka, vuno honi nga lije livue lika uila hali muntu umo, likamusaniuna.”
LUK 20:19 Kaha valongisi va mezi a Lishiko lia Mosesa na tusasendote vayonguele kukuata Yesu haje vene, omuo vatantekeyele nguavo cisimo eci nacitela vakevo, vuno honi vateuele vantu.
LUK 20:20 Nankuma, vatatele ntsimbu ya cili. Kaha vahanene lizika kanua kuli vantu vamo valipuise nge vaka vusunga, kaha va vatumine kuli Yesu linga vakamueseke na vihula linga vamuhane ku mavoko a Nguvulu ua Maloma.
LUK 20:21 Kaha vaje vavatumine vehuile Yesu nguavo, “Mulongisi tuatantekeya nguetu yove ukahandeka vusunga na kulongesa vusunga naua kuue kutala hali muntu cipue uapua ua vulemu, cipue keti ua vulemu vuno honi ntsimbu yoshe ukalongesa vantu vusunga muje muatondela Njambi vayoyemo.
LUK 20:22 Tuleke, nkuma Lishiko lietu litutavesa kufueta lisimo kuli Sezale indi kuahi?”
LUK 20:23 Vuno honi Yesu uatantekeyela kuzangama kuavo, kaha uahandekele kuli vakevo nguendi,
LUK 20:24 “Njimueseni mbongo ya siliva. Cihanga ceya na lizina lieya viliho?” Kaha vamukumbuluile nguavo “via Sezale!”
LUK 20:25 Kaha Yesu uahandekele kuli vakevo nguendi, “Muacili, haneni kuli Sezale vije viapande kuli Sezale, kaha haneni kuli Njambi vije viapande kuli Njambi.”
LUK 20:26 Kaha kuvasele kumu uanenaho mulonga ha mezi aua ku mesho a vantu. Valikomokelele ku kukumbulula cendi kaha vaholokele kuluu.
LUK 20:27 Kaha Vasanduki vamo, vaje vakulahela nguavo vantu kuvakasanguka ku vatsi, vezile kuli Yesu nakumuihula nguavo,
LUK 20:28 “Mulongisi, Mosesa uatusonekelele Lishiko eli nguendi, ‘Nga yala atsa, kaha aseza mpuevo yendi vuno honi kesi na vana, kaha munaina ambate uje ntuluue linga vakase kukala na vana va uje natsi.’
LUK 20:29 Kuakele vamuanaye vatanu na vavali, kaha uje uamukuluntu uambate mpuevo, uatsile kuakuhona vana.
LUK 20:30 Kaha uje ua mucivali uambate uje mpuevo naua uatsile kuakuhona vana
LUK 20:31 kaha mucitatu naua. Cuma cimo cafuile mujevene kuli voshe vatanu na vavali, voshe vatsile kuakuhona vana.
LUK 20:32 Kaha kukumanusuila uje mpuevo uatsile.
LUK 20:33 Nankuma, ha litangua lije omo vatsi vaka sanguka, uje mpuevo akapua ueya hhakati kavaje voshe vamuambate vatanu na vavali?”
LUK 20:34 Yesu uavakumbuluile nguendi, “Vantu va lifuti lino vakambata na kushombuesa naua,
LUK 20:35 vuno honi vampuevo na vamala vaje vapande kusanguka ku vatsi na kuyoya mu ntsimbu ije ikeja kulutue kuva kambata cipue kushomboka.
LUK 20:36 Vakevo vakapua ngue tungelo kuvakasa naua kutsa omuo vanapu vana va Njambi, omuo vanasanguka kuvatsi.
LUK 20:37 Mosesa nahana vukaleho linga vatsi vaka sanguka. Mu visoneka vije vihandeka via lifo liakele nakuuema Mosesa ahandeka hali Muene Njambi ikeye vene ‘Njambi ya Avilahama, Njambi ya Isake, na Njamba ya Yakomba.’
LUK 20:38 Ikeye uapua Njambi ua vaka kuyoya, keti ua vaka kutsa kuahi, omuo ku mesho a Njambi voshe vantu vendi vayoya.”
LUK 20:39 Kaha vamo valongisi va mezi a Lishiko lia Mosesa vahandekele nguavo, “Mulongisi, uakumbulula muacili!”
LUK 20:40 Kuhuma ha ntsimbu ije kuvasele naua kuihula Yesu vihula vieka.
LUK 20:41 Yesu uavehuile nguendi, “Vatihoni vali nakuhandeka nguavo, Kilistu akapua ua ku ntanga ya muene Ndaviti?
LUK 20:42 Ndaviti vavenia nahandeka mu livulu lia miaso nguendi, ‘Muene Njambi uahandekele kuli Muene uange nguendi, Tumama ku livoko liange lia cilio,
LUK 20:43 noho njikapuisa vitozi vove ngue cituamo caku viliato viove.’
LUK 20:44 Ndaviti ikeye vavenia uamutumbuile nguendi, ‘Muene,’ vatihoni Kilistu apua mutekulu lia Ndaviti?”
LUK 20:45 Kaha omo civunga ca vantu vakele nakuvuilia, kaha Yesu uakele nakuhandeka kuli vandongisi vendi nguendi,
LUK 20:46 “Zangameni kuli valongisi va mezi a Lishiko lia Mosesa, vaje vazanga kuenda na vikovelo viavo via laha viandando na kutsetsela na kasingimiko mumihela yakulandesela na kuhangula vituamo viacili mu vinjivo via Njambi via malombelo na mihela ya vantu va vulemu ku viuano.
LUK 20:47 Vakevo vakakuisi vantuluue na kuvevila vinjivo viavo, kaha vashueka vilinga viavo na malombelo alaha! Kaha nakuzangamesa kuavo kukapu kuakama cikuma!”
LUK 21:1 Litangua limo omo Yesu uakele nakutalazeka, uamuene vaka kufuka vali nakuhana mulambu uavo mu njivo ya Njambi,
LUK 21:2 kaha naua uamuene ntuluue umo ua cihutu uahanene tumbongo tuvali.
LUK 21:3 Kaha Yesu uahandekele nguendi, “Mua vusunga njimileka nguange, ou ntuluue ua cihutu nahana viavingi kupulakana voshe vaje vantu vakufuka,
LUK 21:4 njahandeka evi omuo veka vanakala nakulambuila via kusalaho ku vufuko vuavo, vuno honi ou mpuevo nalambuila vioshe vianakele navio via kulikuasa navio.”
LUK 21:5 Vamo va vandongisi va Yesu vakele nakuhandeka ha njivo ya Njambi, ha vucili vua mavue aje vaitungisile, na vuana vuje vakele nakuhana mukuivuahesa, kaha Yesu uahandekele nguendi,
LUK 21:6 “Maneni njimileke ha viuma vioshe evi munamono. Ntsimbu ikaheta omo vitozi veni vaka humisa livue lioshe lia njivo mu muhela uhalio, kaha mavue oshe a ka siuka.”
LUK 21:7 Vandongisi va Yesu vamuihuile nguavo, “Mulongisi, muaka muka evi viuma vikalingika?” Na cimueso muka tukatantekeya naco nguetu ntsimbu inahete ya viuma vioshe evi vilingiue.
LUK 21:8 Yesu uahandekele kuli vakevo nguendi, “Zangameni keti vamikuise. Vantu vavengi vakeja mu lizina liange na kuhandeka nguavo, ‘Yange vene ikeye!’ Kaha naua nguavo, ‘Ntsimbu inahete vuavuno!’ Vuno honi keti mukava kavangeye.
LUK 21:9 Omo mukevua vizita na kulitengulukila, keti mukateue, viuma evi vinapande kulingika tahi, vuno honi kuvilumbunuka nge kuhua kua mavu kunahete.”
LUK 21:10 Kaha Yesu uahandekele naua nguendi, “lifuti likalua nzita na lifuti likuavo, kaha vumuene vukalua na vumuene vukuavo.
LUK 21:11 Kukala mandundumua, na njala yakama, na mishongo ya kulitambuisa kuoshe, kukakala viuma viakuteuesa na vitantekeyeso viaku komouesa vikahuminina muilu.
LUK 21:12 Omo ntsimbu kanda viuma evi visholoke. Vakamikuata na kumiyandesa, vakamituala kuvi njivo via malombelo avo naku kamiyula naku mihaka mutumenga, kaha vakamituala ku vimiene naku vanguvulu mukunieseka omuo lizina liange.
LUK 21:13 Ikapua ntsimbu yacili kuli yeni ya kuambulula Muzimbu ua Cili.
LUK 21:14 Nankuma, vihakeni mu mitima yeni keti muvisinganiekele vualumo ngueni vika tukahandeka,
LUK 21:15 omuo njikamihana mana akutantekeya vije vimukahandeka linga vitozi veni kuvakasa kumihisa cipue kuviana vimukahandeka.
LUK 21:16 Cipue visemi vieni, na vamuanoko, na vavushoko veni na vavusamba veni vakamienda vungungu. Kaha vamo hhakati keni vaka vatsiha.
LUK 21:17 Kaha voshe vakamizinda omuo lizina liange.
LUK 21:18 Vuno honi cipue cinkambu cimo ca kumutue ueni ku cikazimbala.
LUK 21:19 Takameseni, kaha mukohiela miono yeni.
LUK 21:20 “Omo mukamona Yelusalema vana izengeleka ku civunga ca masualale, tantekeyeni ngueni kunonga kuayo kuli muyehi.
LUK 21:21 Nankuma, vaje vali mu Yundeya vapande kuteuela ku minkinda, kaha vaje vali mu mbonge vapande kuhumamo, kaha Vaje vali hambaza ya mbonge naku mehia vapande keti vakovelemo mu mbonge.
LUK 21:22 Aua akeuo matangua akuzangamesa, vivahandekele mu visoneka linga vilishulisise.
LUK 21:23 Luvinda ku vampuevo vaje vakakala na mazimo na vampuevo vaje vaka jamuesa ha ntsimbu ije! Tuyando tuakama tukeja ha lifuti eli, na vukalu vua Njambi vukeja hali vantu ava.
LUK 21:24 Kaha vamo vaka vatsiha na mukuale, kaha vakuavo vakavatuala ku vunzinda ku mafuti eka, kaha vaje keti Vayunda vaka pihisa Yelusalema noho ntsimbu yavo ikaheta.
LUK 21:25 “Kaha viuma via kukomouesa vikapangiua ku litangua naku ngonde naku vingongonosi. Vantu voshe vaha mavu vakevua liova lia kuohia kua mema a kalunga na kukuma kua mankimba kaha kuvakatantekeya vivakalinga.
LUK 21:26 Vantu vaka lezimuka kuliova omo vakatatela vije vikasholoka hano ha mavu oshe, omuo viuma vioshe via muilu vikalininganga.
LUK 21:27 Kaha vakamona Muna Muntu akeja mu mashuelua na nzili na vumpau vuakama.
LUK 21:28 Omo viuma evi vikaputuka kupangiua, katukeni nanzili na kutala kuilu, omuo kuohela kueni kuli hayehi.”
LUK 21:29 Kaha Yesu uavatelele cisimo eci nguendi, “Singaniekeni ha muti ua mukuyu na miti yeka yoshe.
LUK 21:30 Omo mumona mafo auo aputuka kuzovelela, muapande kutantekeye ngueni ntondue ili muyehi.
LUK 21:31 Kaha mucifua aci vene, omo mukamona viuma evi vipangiua mutantekeye ngueni vumuene vua Njambi vuli muyehi.
LUK 21:32 “Muavusunga njimileka, viuma vioshe evi vikapangiua oku vantu voshe va ntsimbu ino vaciyoya.
LUK 21:33 Melu na mavu vikahita, vuno honi mezi ange kuakahiti.
LUK 21:34 “Zangameni! Keti mushoshomue cikuma mitima yeni ha ciuano viakulia na kunua na kulinienga ha viuma vije via lifuti. Nga muvilinga litangua lije lika miniangumuna ngue mukapiluka muheto.
LUK 21:35 Litangua lije likeja ku vantu voshe vali hano ha mavu.
LUK 21:36 Livuaheseleni na kulombela ntsimbu yoshe linga mukakale na nzili yakuhiana vioshe vije vikapangiua na kuimana ku mesho a Muna Muntu.”
LUK 21:37 Yesu uakale na kulongesa mu njivo ya Njambi ha matangua aje, kaha kuheta ku ntsimbu ya cinguezi, uakele nakuhumamo na kuya ku munkinda ua Oliveta kukakalako vutsiki vuoshe.
LUK 21:38 Kucimenemene coshe vantu voshe vakele nakuya mu njivo ya Njambi na kumuivuilila.
LUK 22:1 Omo ntsimbu yahete kuyehi ya ciuano ca kulia mbola ya kuhona cimbaluila, civasana nguavo Ciuano ca Paseka.
LUK 22:2 Kaha vakuluntu vatusasendote na valongisi va mezi a Lishiko lia Mosesa vatondele ngila ya vushueke ya kutsilamo Yesu omuo vakele na liova lia vantu.
LUK 22:3 Kaha Satana uakovelele muli Yundasa ivasana Sakaliote, umo uavaje likumi na vavali ua vandongisi.
LUK 22:4 Kaha Yundasa uaile na kukahande kuli vakuluntu vatusasendote na vaka kuniunga Njivo ya Njambi, uavamuesela ngila yakuendela Yesu vungungu.
LUK 22:5 Kaha vakevo vavuahelelele cikuma, valitaivatumbuile nendi kumuhana vimbongo.
LUK 22:6 Yundasa uatavele, kaha uatalazekele ngila imo ya kuendelamo Yesu vungungu kua kuhona vantu kutantekeya.
LUK 22:7 Litangua liete ha ntsimbu ya ciuano ca mbolo ya kuhona cimbaluila, omo vatsihile vana va vampanga vakulia ha Ciuano a Paseka.
LUK 22:8 Yesu uatumine Petulu na Iuano nguendi “Yemuye muka vuahesele vualumo mutu kalila Ciuano ca Paseka.”
LUK 22:9 Kaha vamuihuile nguavo, “Kuli ku utonda linga tuka civuaheleseko?”
LUK 22:10 Kaha uavakumbuluile nguendi, “Omo mukakovela mu mbonge, muka uana muntu nambata njava ya kutekuila mema. Mukaveni noho akaheta mu njivo ya kakovela.
LUK 22:11 Handekeni kuli vavenia njivo ngueni, ‘Mulongisi natutumu kukuihula nguendi, cilikuli cihela cituakulila yange na vandongisi vange Ciuano ca Paseka?’
LUK 22:12 Kaha akamimuesa cihela cakama helu lia njivo, vanauvuahesa vualumo, kuje mukavuahese viakulia.”
LUK 22:13 Kaha vaile vauanene viuma vioshe nge muavalekelele Yesu, vavuahesele viakulia via Ciuano ca Paseka.
LUK 22:14 Kaha omo ntsimbu ya hete Yesu uatumamene ku mesa hamo na tunganda vendi.
LUK 22:15 Kaha uahandekele kuli vakevo nguendi, “Njatondele cikuma kulia eci Ciuano ca Paseka hamo neni ntsimbu kanda njiyande,
LUK 22:16 omuo njimileka nguange, kuhuma lelo kunjikacili naua kuvanga noho calishulisilila muacili mu Vumuene vua Njambi.”
LUK 22:17 Kaha Yesu uanonele hambanza ya viniu, kaha uahandekele kuli Njambi, na kuhandeka kuli vandongisi vendi nguendi, “Ambateni hambanza eyi mulishumuine hhakati keni.
LUK 22:18 Njimileka nguange, kuhuma lelo kunjikanu naua neni viniu kuvanga noho vumuene vua Njambi vuneja.”
LUK 22:19 Kaha uambate naua mbolo uakandelele kuli Njambi, kaha uaitavuile uava haneneyo nguendi, “ Ei inapu muvila uange uvanahana ha yeni. Lingelingeni eci mukunjivuluka yange.”
LUK 22:20 Omo vamanesele kulia uambate kambanza uahandekele nguendi, “Eyi kambanza inapu litavasano lihaliha lia Njambi livanakutu na maninga ange aje ahitikila hali yeni.
LUK 22:21 “Vuno honi taleni! Ou anjenda vungungu hali hamo nange kuno ku mesa!
LUK 22:22 Muna Muntu akatsa nge muje muasinganiekelemo Njambi, vuno honi tuyando tuendi uje akamuenda vungungu!”
LUK 22:23 Kaha vandongisi vendi vaputukile kulihozola hhakati kavo nguavo, iya honi akalinga cuma eci.
LUK 22:24 Kaha kuaputukile vimpata hhakati ka vandongisi va Yesu nguavo, iya umo hhakati kavo napu uakama kupulakana.
LUK 22:25 Kaha Yesu uandekele kuli vakevo nguendi, “Vamiene va vaje keti Vayunda vali na nzili ha vantu vavo. Kaha vaje vaka kushika vavatumbula vakuasi va vantu.”
LUK 22:26 Vuno honi ei keti ikeyo ngila hhakati keni, vuno honi uoshe uje uakama hhakati keni napande kupua uamundende, kaha ntuama yeni napande kupua ngue ngamba.
LUK 22:27 Iya uakama kupulakana? Uje natumama kukulia cipue uje hamuhana viakulia? Nguetu uje natumama kukulia ikeye uakama ndi? Vuno honi yange njili hakati keni nguange muka kuhana viakulia.
LUK 22:28 Yeni munakala nange mu tuyando tuange tuoshe.
LUK 22:29 Nge mua nanjihanena Tate nzili ya kuyula, neni naua njikamihana nzili yakuyula.
LUK 22:30 Linga yeni mukalie na kunua mu vumuene vuange, kaha mukatumama ku vituamo vua vumuene na kuyula miyati likumi na ivali ya Isaleli.
LUK 22:31 Simoni, Simoni! Ivuilila, Satana atonda linga amieseke yeni mu vavoshe, ku hangununa vacili ku vavapi nge muka kulima muaka hangununa tiliku ku mujungu.
LUK 22:32 Vuno honi yange njakulombelela linga lutsilielo luove keti luhue. Kaha omo ukatenguluka na kuhiluka kuli yange, unapande kukolesa vamuanoko.
LUK 22:33 Kaha Simoni Petulu uamukumbuluile nguendi, “Muene, njalivuahesela laja kuya mu kamenga nove na kukatsa nove!”
LUK 22:34 Kaha Yesu uamukumbuluile nguendi, “Muavusunga, Petulu” njikuleka nguange, “vutsiki vuno vene kanda ndemba atambeke, ukanjiviana lutatu.”
LUK 22:35 Yesu uehuile vandongisi vendi nguendi, “Muje njamitumine cakuhona cikuama, ngonga cipue vinkaku muahonoueleko cuma cimo ndi?” Kaha vamukumbuluile nguavo, “houe!”
LUK 22:36 Kaha Yesu uahandekele kuli vakevo nguendi, “Vuno honi” ntsimbu ino, “Ou hali na cikuama cipue ngonga napande kuambata, kaha uoshe nahonoua mukuale napande kulandesa kazaku kendi alande mukuale.
LUK 22:37 Muomu vanacisoneka nguavo, ‘Vamutandelele kumo na vaka kushaula Lishiko.’ Kaha njimileka nguange eci cinapande kulishulisisa hali yange. Eyo vioshe vije vivanasoneka hali yange vili nakulishulisisa.”
LUK 22:38 Kaha vandongisi vahandekele nguavo, “Muene tala! Kuli mikuale ivali ei!” Kaha uavakumbuluile nguendi, “Mukemo vene!”
LUK 22:39 Kaha Yesu uahumine mu mbonge, kaha uaile ku munkinda ua Oliveta nge muakele nakulingilamo. Kaha vandongisi vendi vamukavele.
LUK 22:40 Omo uahete kuje uavalekele nguendi, “Lombeleni linga keti mukovele muvieseko.”
LUK 22:41 Kaha uahumine kavundende kuli vakevo kaha uatsikamene na kulombela,
LUK 22:42 nguendi, “Tate nga mutonda hambanza eyi ya tuyando ihite kulahako nange. Keti nge ku cizango cange kuahi, vuno honi cizango cove cilingiue.
LUK 22:43 Kangelo uahumine kuilu uasholokele kuli ikeye na kumusimpisa.
LUK 22:44 Omuo ha tuyando tuakama ua lombelele cikuma, kaha ntuima yendi yapuile ngue mambase a maninga anduekelele ha mavu.”
LUK 22:45 Kaha omo uakatukile kuhuma ku kulombela, uaile kuli vandongisi vendi uavauanene vanakosa tulo, omuo vazeyele na vusiua.
LUK 22:46 Kaha uahandekele kuli vakevo nguendi, “Vikahoni muakosela? Hindukeni mu lombele, linga keti mukovela muvieseko.”
LUK 22:47 Kaha te Yesu uakele nakuhandeka navo, hajevene civunga ca vantu cahete. Yundasa Sakaliote uje uava likumi na vavali uatuamene kulutue luovo. Kaha uashuenene kuli Yesu na kumuntsuemba.
LUK 22:48 Kaha Yesu uahandekele kuli ikeye nguendi, “Yundasa nkumani yove uenda Muna Muntu vungungu na kumutsuemba ndi?”
LUK 22:49 Kaha omo vandongisi vaje vakele hamo na Yesu vamuene vije viapangikile vahandekele nguavo, “Muene tulikuasese mikuale ndi?”
LUK 22:50 Kaha umo ua vandongisi va Yesu uavatuile lituitui lia ngamba ua kasasendote uakama.
LUK 22:51 Vuno honi Yesu uamu vianesele nguendi, “Ecela” kaha uakuate lituitui lia uje yala nakulihiluisilako naua.
LUK 22:52 Kaha Yesu uahandekele kuli vaje vakuluntu va tusasendote na vamo vakuluntu va vaka kuniunga njivo ya Njambi na vakuluntu vaje vezile na kumukuata nguendi, “Nkumani muneja namikuale na vimbueti ngue njimuizi ndi?
LUK 22:53 Njinakele neni mu njivo ya Njambi ha matangua oshe vikahoni kumuanjikuate. Vuno honi eyi ikeyo ntsimbu yeni yakuipanga, omo nzili ya milima ili nakuhiana.”
LUK 22:54 Vakuate Yesu kaha vamutualele ku njivo ya Kasasendote uakama, kaha Petulu uamukavele munima uakele kulahako.
LUK 22:55 Vamo vavuekele tuhia mukati ka cipango vatumamene nakuota, kaha Petulu uatumamene navo.
LUK 22:56 Omo ngamba umo uampuevo uamuene Petulu natumama kuje ku tuhia, uamutalele ntoma, kaha uahandekele nguendi, “Yala ou naua uakele hamo na Yesu.”
LUK 22:57 Vuno honi Petulu uavianene nguendi, “Yove mpuevo yange kunjimutantekeya!”
LUK 22:58 Kaha omo kuahitile ka ntsimbu kakandende, yala ueka naua uamuene Petulu, kaha uahandekele nguendi, “Nove naua ua umo vendi” Vuno honi Petulu uamukumbuluile nguendi, “Yala, kuahi, keti yange!”
LUK 22:59 Omo kuahitile ola lika, kaha yala mukuavo naua uahandekele nanzili nguendi, “Ou yala cilivene uakele hamo na Yesu, nendi naua Kangalileya!”
LUK 22:60 Vuno honi Petulu uamukumbuluile nguendi, “Yove yala yange kunjitantekeya evi ulinakuhandeka!” Hajevene te acili nakuhandeka kaha ndemba uatambekele.
LUK 22:61 Kaha Yesu uatengulukile uatalele kuli Petulu, kaha Petulu uavulukile vije via mulekele Yesu nguendi, “Ntsimbu kanda ndemba atambenge vutsiki vunovene ukanjiviana lutatu”
LUK 22:62 Kaha Petulu uatuhukile hambanza na kulila cikuma.
LUK 22:63 Vamala vaje vaniungile Yesu vamushendumuine na kumupupa.
LUK 22:64 Vamukitile tanga ha mesho, kaha vahandekele kuli ikeye nguavo, “Nga ukananguizi, tuleke! Iya na kupupu?”
LUK 22:65 Vahandekele viuma viavingi via kumushaula.
LUK 22:66 Kaha omo kuacele vakuluntu voshe va vantu valiuanene hamolika. Vakuluntu va tusasendote, na valongisi va mezi a Lishiko lia Mosesa voshe kuvakele, kaha vanehele Yesu ku mpunga yavo.
LUK 22:67 Kaha vamuihuile nguavo, “Tuleke, yove Kilistu ndi?” Kaha Yesu uavakumbuluile nguendi, “Cipue nga njimileka nguange yange, kumukanjikulahela.”
LUK 22:68 Kaha naua nga njimihula cihula, kumukasa kunjitava.
LUK 22:69 Vuno honi hume lelo nakutuala kulutue Muna Muntu akatumama ku livoko lia cilio lia Njambi muka nzili yoshe.
LUK 22:70 Kaha voshe vamuihuile nguavo, “Nkuma yove u Muna Njambi ndi?” Ikeye uavakumbuluile nguendi, “Mumu nahandeka mukemo vene.”
LUK 22:71 Kaha vahandekele nguavo, “Vikahoni tutondela naua vukaleho vueka? Yetu vavenia tualivuila laja muanacihandeka.”
LUK 23:1 Kaha mpunga yoshe yakatukile na kutuala Yesu kuli Nguvulu Pilato.
LUK 23:2 Kaha vaputukile kumuvangeya nguavo, “Tuauana ou yala aleka vantu vetu linga valuise Fulumende yetu, alina kuvavindika kufueta lisimu kuli Sezale na kulihandeka ikeye vavenia nguendi ikeye Kilistu Muene uetu.”
LUK 23:3 Kaha Pilato uamuhulisile nguendi, “Yove Muene ua Vayunda ndi?” Yesu uamukumbuluile nguendi, “Munahandeka mukemo vene.”
LUK 23:4 Kaha Pilato uahandekele ku tusasendote vakama na civunga nguendi, “Yange kunjauanene mulonga kuli ou muntu.”
LUK 23:5 Vuno honi vakevo vahandekele na nzili nguavo, “Ikeye alinakulinga mpindakano ku vantu na vilongesa viendi linga valuise Yundeya yoshe. Uaputukilile mu Ngalileya, kaha hano vene nejakuno.”
LUK 23:6 Omo Nguvulu Pilato uevuile eci, kaha ueuile nguendi, “Nkuma ou yala ka Ngalileya ndi?”
LUK 23:7 Omo Pilato uatantekeyele nge Yesu uahumine ku nganda ije yakele nakuyula Muene Helonde naua mukemo muakele, kaha uamutumine kuli Muene Helonde, uje uakele mu Yelusalema ha ntsimbu ije.
LUK 23:8 Muene Helonde uavuahelele cikuma omo uamuene Yesu, omuo uovuile viendi na laja uakele nakutonda cikuma kumumona. Uakele nalishungu lia kumona Yesu alinga vikomouesa.
LUK 23:9 Kaha Muene Helonde ueuile Yesu vihula viavingi, vuno honi Yesu katavele cipue lizi limo.
LUK 23:10 Kaha vakuluntu va tusasendote na valongisi va mezi a Lishiko lia Mosesa vaile kulutue nakuvangeya Yesu muakama.
LUK 23:11 Kaha Muene Helonde na masualale vendi vamushendumuine naku mupanga mua mupi, kaha vamuzikile mukanjo uandando, kaha Helonde vamuhiluisile kuli Pilato.
LUK 23:12 Kaha ha litangua lije vene Helonde na Pilato valikuate vusamba, te kanda lievi vapuile muntu na citozi cendi.
LUK 23:13 Pilato uasanene hamo vakuluntu va tusasendote na vantuama na vantu,
LUK 23:14 Kaha uahandekele kuli vakevo nguendi, “Muanehe ou yala kuli yange na kuhandeka ngueni alinakulekesa vantu linga valuise Fulumende. Ivuilileni, yange njamuihuile ku mesho eni, kaha kunjauanene mulonga ua cuma cimo cacipi cimunamuvangeya.
LUK 23:15 Cipue Helonde kauanene mulonga muli ikeye mukemo namuhiluisa kuli yetu. Ou yala kukuesi cuma canalingi linga va muuaneneho mulonga ua kutsa.
LUK 23:16 Njikamupupa lika kaha njikamuecela linga aye.”
LUK 23:17 Kuakele cilika cavo cije Pilato uatondele kuhumisila vantu cinzinda umo mu kamenga uje ivatondele ha ntsimbu ya Ciuano ca Paseka.
LUK 23:18 Kaha civunga coshe ca vantu ca tambakanene nguavo, “mutsihe!” Tuzituile Mbalambasa.
LUK 23:19 (Mbalambasa vamuhakele mu kamenga omuo uakele nakuluisa Fulumende mu mbonge na kuntsiha vantu.)
LUK 23:20 Vuno honi Pilato uatondele kuecela Yesu, kaha uahandekele naua ku civunga.
LUK 23:21 Vuno honi vakele nakutambeka nguavo, “Mushukike ha cilindakano! Mushukike ha cilindakano!”
LUK 23:22 Kaha Pilato uahandekele naua lua mucitatu nguendi, “Vupi muka vuanapanga? Yange kunjauanene cuma cimo ca kumutsihila! Njimupupa lika na kumuecela aye.”
LUK 23:23 Vuno honi vantu vatualeleleho kutambeka nguavo Yesu vamushukike ha cilindakano, kaha hakutambeka nguavo uavahaneneye.
LUK 23:24 Nankuma, Pilato uatete cije cimpande, ngue muvalombele vakevo.
LUK 23:25 Kaha Pilato uecelele Mbalambasa muntu ivatondele, uje uakele mu kamenga ha mulonga ua kuluisa Fulumende na kutsiha vantu. Kaha uavahanene Yesu linga vamulinge muje muvatondelele vavenia.
LUK 23:26 Kaha masualale vatualele Yesu mukumushukika te vali nakuya valiuanene na yala umo ua lizina lia Simoni uaku Silene, uje uezile mu mbonge kuhuma ku mehia. Kaha vamukuate nakumutuika cilindakano ca Yesu kaha vamulekele linga akave Yesu munima.
LUK 23:27 Civunga cakama ca vantu ca mukavele, hhakati kavo hakele vampuevo vaje vakele nakulilila ikeye cikuma.
LUK 23:28 Yesu uatengulukile kuli vakevo nakuhandeka nguendi, “Yeni vampuevo vamu Yelusalema! Keti mulile yange vuno honi lilileni yeni vavenia na vana veni.
LUK 23:29 Kaha matangua alina kuija omo vantu vakahandeka nguavo, ‘Vanakuisuliua vaje vantsimpi, vaje kuvasemene tukeke na vaje kuvalelele.’
LUK 23:30 Ikapua ntsimbu ije vantu vakahandeka ku minkinda nguavo, ‘Tuuileni! Naku malundu nguavo, tufuikeni!’
LUK 23:31 Nga valinga viuma evi ku muti uakutontola, kaha honi cikafua vati ku muti uakuma?”
LUK 23:32 Kaha naua kuakele mihuza vavali va vamala vavatualele hamo na Yesu na kuvashukika.
LUK 23:33 Omo vahete kumuhela vatumbuile nguavo, “Cikola,” kaha vashukikile Yesu ha cilindakano na vaje mihuza vavali umo ku livoko lia cilio mukuavo ku livoko lia cimoshue.
LUK 23:34 Yesu uahandekele nguendi, “Tate vakonekele! Omuo kuvatantekeya cije civali nakulinga.” Kaha masualale valipangezelele vuzalo vuendi na kuta nkela.
LUK 23:35 Kaha vantu vemanene kuje nakutalela te vantuama va Vayunda vamushendumuine nguavo, “Uovuele vakuavo, nendi aliovole ikeye vavenia nga ikeye Kilistu uje ya nahangula Njambi!”
LUK 23:36 Kaha masualale vamushendumuine naua vezile hayehi kuli ikeye vamuhanene viniu via kushasha.
LUK 23:37 Vahandekele kuli ikeye nguavo, “Liovole yove vavenia nga u Muene ua Vayunda!”
LUK 23:38 Helu lia cilindakano cendi hakele mezi aua nguavo, “Ou ikeye Muene ua Vayunda.”
LUK 23:39 Kaha muhuza umo ivamushukikile hamo nendi uahandekele lizi lia kumushaula nguendi, “Nkumani keti yove Kilistu ndi? Liovole yove vavenia netu naua utuovolo!”
LUK 23:40 Kaha uje mukuavo muhuza uamutenukilile nguendi, “Nkuma yove kuuteue Njambi ndi? Yove unambata cihiso ngue ikeye.
LUK 23:41 Cihiso cetu cinatupande, omuo tunambata fueto ya vilinga vuetu, vuno honi yala ou kesi na vupi.”
LUK 23:42 Kaha uahandekele kuli Yesu nguendi, “Yesu njivuluke omo ukeja mu vumuene vuove.”
LUK 23:43 Yesu uamukumbuluile nguendi, “Mua vusunga njikuleka nguange lelo vene ukakala hamo nange mu vumuene vua muilu.”
LUK 23:44 Omo ntsimbu yapuile hhakati ka litangua, kaha litangua liazivalele kuakekele milima mu lifuti lioshe ije yakeleko noho ha ola ya citatu ya cinguezi.
LUK 23:45 Kaha ntanga ije yakele mu njivo ya Njambi yatavukile hhakati kuhuma kuilu na mavu.
LUK 23:46 Kaha Yesu uatambekele na lizi liakama nguendi, “Tate! Njihaka muono uange mu mavoko ove.” Hanima yakuhandeka mezi aua uatsile.
LUK 23:47 Omo mukuluntu ua masualale uamuene vije via lingiuile, ualemesele Njambi nakuhandeka nguendi, “Mua vusunga yala ou uapuile muka vusunga.”
LUK 23:48 Omo vantu vaje vakungulukilile kuje ku muhela vamuene viuma vije valingiuile, kaha vahilukile ku vinjivo viavo vali pupangele ha vintulo viavo mu vusiua.
LUK 23:49 Kaha voshe vaje vatantekeyele Yesu ha mutuntu uendi hamo na vampuevo vaje vamukavele kuhuma ku Ngalileya vemanenene kulahako nakutala viuma evi.
LUK 23:50 Kuakele yala umo lizina liendi Yosefa uaku mbonge ya Alamatiya mu nganda ya Yunda. Uapuile yala uacili ua kasingimiko,
LUK 23:51 uje uakele nakutalelela kuija kua vumuene vua Njambi. Cipue vene uapuile umo uamu mpunga, katavele ku vutumbe vuavo vua kuluisa Yesu na vilinga viavo.
LUK 23:52 Uaile kuli Pilato nakulomba muvila ua Yesu.
LUK 23:53 Uahumisile muvila ua Yesu ha cilindakano, kaha uauzengelele ha ntanga ya liniu, kaha ualangekele muvila ua Yesu mu cihilo cije civa cokuele mu livue lije kanda vantsindemo muntu kuyehi na munkinda uaundende.
LUK 23:54 Liapuile litangua lia mucitanu cinguezi omo litangua lia Sapalalo kanda lihete.
LUK 23:55 Vampuevo vaje vakavele Yesu kuhuma ku Ngalileya vaile hamo na Yosefa, vakamuene cihilo cije na kumona muje muvalangekelelemo muvila ua Yesu.
LUK 23:56 Kaha vaile ku vinjivo viavo nakukavuahesa mukundu na mazi aluengo luacili linga vaka vuahese muvila ua Yesu. Kaha ha litangua lia Sapalalo vahuimine kuya ku Lishiko lia Mosesa.
LUK 24:1 Omo kuacele lia calumingo vampuevo vaile ku cihilo, vambate mazi avavuahesele.
LUK 24:2 Kaha vauanene livue liakama vana lihumisa ku cikolo ca cihilo.
LUK 24:3 Kaha vakovelelemo vuno honi kuuanenemo muvila ua Muene Yesu.
LUK 24:4 Vemanene kuje te valikomokela, kaha hajevene kuasholokele vamala vavali mu vuzalo vuakuviakuma kuli vakevo.
LUK 24:5 Vaje vampuevo vovuile liova cikuma kaha vakotamene ha mavu, vaje vamala vavehuile nguavo, “Vika mutondela muka muono ku vantsi?
LUK 24:6 Uahiko kuno nasanguka laja. Vulukeni muje muahandekele kuli yeni tele ali ku Ngalileya.
LUK 24:7 ‘Muna Muntu vaka muhana mu mavako a vantu vavupi, kaha vaka mushukika, a kasanguka hanima ya matangua atatu.’ ”
LUK 24:8 Kaha vampuevo vavulukile mezi endi.
LUK 24:9 Kaha vahumine kuje ku cihilo vakalekele viuma vioshe vivamuene kuli vaje likumi na umo lia vandongisi na vakuavo voshe.
LUK 24:10 Vaje vampuevo vapuile Maliya Mangandalena, na Njuana, na Maliya vaina ya Yakomba na vampuevo vakuavo valekele evi viuma kuli tunganda va Yesu.
LUK 24:11 Vuno honi tunganda vasinganiekele nge vije vivahandekele vampuevo keti viaseho kaha kuva vakulahelele.
LUK 24:12 Vuno honi Petulu uakatukile na kushatukila ku cihilo, uakotamenenemo kaha uamuenemo lika vintanga na ceka cahi. Kaha uahilukile kuimbo na kulikomokela ha viuma vije via lingiuile.
LUK 24:13 Ha litangua lijevene vandongisi vavali va Yesu vendele kuya ku limbo lije liivatumbuile nguavo Emausi, ntunda yakele matambo likumi na imo kuhuma ku Yelusalema.
LUK 24:14 Vakele nakuhandeka ha viuma vioshe vije vialingiuile.
LUK 24:15 Tele vacili nakuhandeka na kuliyongola, Yesu uezile hayehi navo nakuenda navo.
LUK 24:16 Vamumuene vuno honi kuvamutantekeyele.
LUK 24:17 Yesu uahandekele kuli vakevo nguendi, “Vimpande muka muli nakuhandeka oku muenda?” Vemanene kaha vihanga viavo viasolokele mu vusiua.
LUK 24:18 Kaha umo uavo lizina liendi Kolopase, uamukumbuluile nguendi, “Yove lika mungezi muno mu Yelusalema uje katantekeya vinapangika ha matangua ano.”
LUK 24:19 Kaha uavehuile nguendi, “Viuma muka?” Vamutavele nguavo, “Via Yesu uaku Nazaleta. Yala ou uapuile kananguizi ka Njambi na vantu voshe vamutavele kupua muka nzili mu viuma vioshe uahandekele na vije via lingile na Njambi uamu kulahelele.
LUK 24:20 Kaha tusasendote vakama na vakakuyula vamuhanene kuli Nguvulu ua Maloma linga vamutsihe, kaha vamushukikile ha cilindakano.
LUK 24:21 Tuakele na likulahelo nguetu ikeye akapatula Isaleli! Kaha lelo linapu litangua lia mucitatu kuhuma haje vialingiuile viuma evi.
LUK 24:22 Vampuevo vamo hhakati ketu vatukomokesele, vamenekelele ku cihilo cimenemene,
LUK 24:23 vuno honi kuvakauanene muvila uendi. Kaha vahilukile nguavo vakamuene cimona ca tungelo vaje vavalekele nguavo hali nakuyoya.
LUK 24:24 Kaha vamo hakati ketu vaileko ku cihilo, kaha vakauanene nge muje muvahandekelele vaje vampuevo, vuno honi kuvamumuene.”
LUK 24:25 Kaha Yesu uahandekele kuli vakevo nguendi, “Yeni vilema, vaka kusimbula kutsiliela vije vioshe vivahandekele tunanguizi va Njambi va Njambi!
LUK 24:26 Nkumani Kilistu kapande kuyanda ha viuma evi nakukovela mu vumpau vuendi ndi?”
LUK 24:27 Kaha Yesu uaputukile kuvalumbuinina vioshe viuma vije vahandekele mu visoneka hali ikeye, kuputuka na mavulu a Mosesa na kutuala ku visoneka via tunanguizi va Njambi va Njambi voshe.
LUK 24:28 Kaha omo vahete kuyehi na limbo kuje vakele nakuya, Yesu ualingile ngue atuvakana kamandende kuya kulutue,
LUK 24:29 Vuno honi vamulombele na kuhandeka nguavo, “Tumama netu omuo cinguezi na litangua liatoko.” Kaha uaile na kukala navo.
LUK 24:30 Uatumamene navo mukulia kaha uambatele mbolo naku ikuisula uaipazuile na kuvahana.
LUK 24:31 Kaha mesho avo ashokolokele vatantekeyele nguavo nkumani ikeye, vuno honi ualavukile ku mesho avo.
LUK 24:32 Kaha valihandekesele umo na mukuavo nguavo, “Nkumani mukemo mitima yetu yovuile kuvuahelela cikuma omo uakele nakuhandeka netu mu ngila na kutulumbunuina viuma viamu visoneka.”
LUK 24:33 Vakatukile ha ntsimbu ijevene vahilukile ku Yelusalema, vauanene vandongisi likumi na umo vanalikungulula na vaje vakuavo veka naua.
LUK 24:34 Vahandekele nguavo, “Mua vusunga vene Muene Yesu nasanguka! Nalisholola kuli Simoni!”
LUK 24:35 Kaha vaje vavali vambuluile vije vialingiuile mu ngila, nomu vatantekeyele nguavo nkuma ikeye Muene Yesu omo uatavuile mbolo.
LUK 24:36 Tele ntsimbu vaje vavali vakele nakuvaleka viuma evi, vuasi vuasi Yesu vavenia uemanene hakati kavo uahandekele nguendi, “Ciyulo cikale neni.”
LUK 24:37 Kaha vovuile liova cikuma, omuo vasikaniekele nguavo vanamono ndumba ya muntu.
LUK 24:38 Vuno honi uahandekele kuli vakevo nguendi, “Vikahoni munalijujukila? Omo vika muli na vimpata mu mitima yeni?
LUK 24:39 Taleni mavoko ange na mu viliato viange. Taleni yange vene. Njikuateni, kaha mutantekeya omuo nduma ya muntu kakele na ntsitu na vitsiha ngue evi muomono njili navio.”
LUK 24:40 Uahandekele evi na kuvamuesa mavoko na viliato viendi.
LUK 24:41 Cipue ngoco kuva kulahelele omuo vavuahelele cikuma na kulikomokela kaha Yesu uavehuile nguendi, “Muli na viakulia linga njilie ndi?”
LUK 24:42 Kaha vamuhanene mbazuvuila ya intsi uakuoca.
LUK 24:43 Kaha uaitambuile na kulia ha mesho avo.
LUK 24:44 Kaha uahandekele kuli vakevo nguendi, “Evi vikevio viuma vije njamilekele omo njakele neni nguange viuma vioshe vije vasonekele hali yange mu Lishiko lia Mosesa, na visoneka via tunanguizi va Njambi va Njambi na mu miaso viapande kulishulisisa.”
LUK 24:45 Kaha uashokoluele mana avo linga vovuisise visoneka
LUK 24:46 na kuhandeka kuli vakevo nguendi, “Visoneka viahandeka nguavio, Kilistu napande kuyanda kaha akasanguka hanima ya matangua atatu.”
LUK 24:47 Visoneka viahandeka naua nguavio linga kualuluka na lukonekelo lua vipi vaka viambulula mu lizina liendi ku mafuti oshe, kuputukila mu Yelusalema.
LUK 24:48 Yeni munapu muvakaleho ha viuma evi.
LUK 24:49 Kaha yange njikatuma Cimbembesi Cakulele kuli yeni cije cakulahesele Tate. Muapande kuvandamena mu mbonge noho mukatambula nzili ei kuhuminina muilu.
LUK 24:50 Kaha uahumine navo mu mbonge uavatualele kuyehi na Mbeteniya kuje uajunduile mavoko endi naku vakuisula.
LUK 24:51 Tele hali nakuvakuisula, ualisezele navo nakumutuala muilu.
LUK 24:52 Vamushangazalele kaha vahilukile mu Yelusalema na kuvuahelela cikuma.
LUK 24:53 Kaha vakele ntsimbu yoshe mu njivo ya Njambi na kusantsela Njambi.
JOH 1:1 Hambangelo kuakele Lizi, kaha Lizi liakele hamo na Njambi, kaha Lizi liapuile vene Njambi.
JOH 1:2 Hume hambangelo, lizi liakele hamo na Njambi.
JOH 1:3 Muli ikeye Njambi uatangele viuma vioshe, kukuesi cuma civatangele kuakuhona ikeye.
JOH 1:4 Muli ikeye muakele muono, kaha muono uapuile ceke ca vantu voshe.
JOH 1:5 Ceke catuile mu milima, kaha na milima kuyasele kucihiana.
JOH 1:6 Kuakele yala ivatumine kuli Njambi, lizina liendi liapuile Iuano.
JOH 1:7 Uezile ngue mukaleho, mukuhandeka vukaleho vua ceke, linga voshe vatsiliele kuhitila muli ikeye.
JOH 1:8 Ikeye kapuile ceke, vuno honi uezile nakuambulula vukaleho vua ceke.
JOH 1:9 Ceke ca vusunga cije cikatuila hali muntu uoshe cezile ha mavu.
JOH 1:10 Lizi liakele ha mavu, kaha na mavu va atangele kuhitila muli ikeye, vuno honi cipue ngoco vene mavu ka amutantekeyele.
JOH 1:11 Uezile ku lifuti liendi, vuno honi vantu vendi kuvamutambuile.
JOH 1:12 Vuno honi kuli voshe vaje vamutambuile, vaje vatsilielele mu lizina liendi, uavahanene nzili yakupua vana va Njambi,
JOH 1:13 vaje vasemukile keti ku maninga cipue ku mashungu a yala, cipue ku cizango ca kusemuka ku yala, vuno honi Njambi ikeye vavenia uapuile Ishavo.
JOH 1:14 Kaha lizi liahimpukile muntu nakukala hhakati ketu, uashulile na kavumbi na vusunga, tunamono vumpau vuendi, vumpau vuje hakupua Muana umolika ua Ishe.
JOH 1:15 Iuano uahandekele vukaleho hali ikeye nakutambeka nguendi, “Ou ikeye uje injahandekele nguange, ‘Ou eja munima yange napu uakama kupulakana yange, omuo ikeye uakeleko te kanda yange!’ ”
JOH 1:16 Hakushula cendi, yetu voshe tunatambula kavumbi ha kavumbi.
JOH 1:17 Omuo lishiko cilivene valihanene kuhitila muli Mosesa, vuno honi kavumbi na vusunga viezile kuhitila muli Yesu Kilistu.
JOH 1:18 Naumo uahi uamonaho Njambi, kuvanga lika Muana uje umolika, uje ali kuyehi na mutima ua Ishe, uje ikeye namutantekeyesa.
JOH 1:19 Ovu vukevuo vukaleho vuahanene Iuano omo Vayunda vatumine tusasendote na Valevi kuhuma ku Yelusalema mukumuihula nguavo, “Yove iya?”
JOH 1:20 Iuano uahandekele vukaleho, kavianene kuvakumbulula, vuno honi uahandekele kuli vakevo nguendi, “Keti yange Kilistu.”
